gaurīgarbhagataṃ smaret bhūmau vibhūtiṃ saṃstīrya tasminkoṇatrayaṃ likhet  k tatropaveśya śiṣyaṃ ca bandhayitvā vilocane garbhādhānaṃ puṃsavanaṃ sīmantonnayanaṃ tataḥ  k jātakarma ca dīkṣāṅgaṃ pūjayeddaśavārakam tasya dakṣiṇakarṇe ca upadiśyād daśākṣaram  k rasagāyatrīrasendrabhairavaṃ mantraṃ gāyatrīṃ rasasaṃjñikām sa binduhutabhugbījaṃ rasendrasya padaṃ tataḥ  k bhairavaṃ ca caturthyantaṃ karmāstraṃ ca daśāṃśakam vahnibījaṃ dīrghayuktaṃ karanyāsaṃ samācaret  k aghorākhya ṛṣiśchando virāḍdevo maheśvaraḥ pūrvasevājapaṃ lakṣaṃ daśāṃśaṃ homatarpaṇam  k tilājyavrīhibhiḥ kuryāddhomaṃ niścalamānasaḥ pūrvoktāṃ rasagāyatrīṃ japellakṣaṃ ca tarpaṇam  k huneddaśāṃśamājyena satilavrīhibhiḥ priye dadyācchiṣyāyākṣamālāṃ rasaliṅgaṃ rasāgamam  k pūrvoktācāravān bhūtvā rasaliṅgaṃ samarcayet svaśāstrārthāvagamanaṃ kuryātsūtendrasaṃskṛtim  k gurusevārataṃ nityaṃ śiṣyamājñāpayediti śiṣyo baddhāñjalir namrastavājñām ācarāmyaham  k ityuktā sādhakā dīkṣā nirvāṇākhyā praśasyate nirvāṇadīkṣākṛtanityakriyaḥ pūrvaṃ kṛtanaimittikārcanaḥ  k pūrvavacchivakumbhādi vardhanīṃ sthāpayetkramāt svavāme bhasma saṃstīrya ṣaṭkoṇaṃ bhūgṛhaṃ likhet  k śiṣyaṃ saṃveśya kumbhasthajalaiḥ saṃprokṣayedguruḥ mūlābhimantritaṃ bhasma tasya mūrdhni nikṣipet  k gandhapuṣpākṣataṃ dadyāt badhnīyāddakṣiṇe kare kaṅkaṇaṃ caraṇāṅguṣṭhabrahmarandhrāntamānakam  k sūtraṃ tanmūlamantreṇa mantritaṃ surabhīkṛtam śivahastaṃ ca tanmūrdhni nidhāya gurusattamaḥ  k rasāṃkuśāṃ dvādaśārṇām upadiśyān manuṃ param rasabhairavadaivatyaṃ dadyācchiṣyāya deśikaḥ  k ṛṣiśchando devatā ca nyāsaṃ pūrvoktavatpriye tarpaṇaṃ cātha homaṃ ca dhyānaṃ kuryācca pūrvavat  k utthāya ca guruṃ natvā bahuśaḥ stotramuccaret guruḥ śiṣyāya vai dadyādvyāghracarmāsanaṃ ca yatra  k bhastrikāṃ vastrasampūrṇāṃ dadyādbhaiṣajyabhastrikām rasāgamaṃ pāṭhayitvā bhava śiṣya cikitsakaḥ  k rudrarūpī bhavān jātaḥ sarvabhūtahito bhava ityādiśedguruḥ śiṣyaṃ śiṣyo hṛṣṭamanāstataḥ  k kṛtakṛtyosmi pūtosmi tīrṇasaṃsārasāgaraḥ iti vijñāpayecchiṣyaḥ stutvā ca bahudhā gurum  k proktā nirvāṇadīkṣeyam athācāryābhiṣecanam ācāryadīkṣānirvāṇadīkṣitasyāsya śiṣyasyāpi mahātmanaḥ  k ācāryadīkṣāṃ kurvīta yathāvadgurusattamaḥ yathā nirvāṇadīkṣāyāstathā sarvaṃ prakalpayet  k viśeṣācchivavardhanyoḥ purataḥ sthāpayedghaṭam rūpyagandhādilohāśādivyauṣadhagaṇānvitam  k śivakumbhavadanyacca sarvamasmin vinikṣipet gurukumbhaṃ japetspṛṣṭvā mūlamaṣṭottaraṃ śatam  k gurukumbhamimaṃ viddhi gurumantreṇa pūjayet āvāhanāsanārghyādyair upacāraiśca ṣoḍaśaiḥ  k śivādipaṅktiṃ tatraiva pūjayedguruṇā saha yathāpūrvaṃ samāsīnaṃ śiṣyaṃ caikāgramānasam  k pūrvavacchivavardhanyorambunā pariṣecayet pūrvavacchivahastaṃ ca mūlamantropadeśakam  k kṛtvā taduttamāṅge ca gurupaṅktiṃ guruṃ tathā āvāhanādyaiḥ sampūjya gandhasragdīpakaiḥ  k phalagandhottamopetairnaivedyaiḥ pūjayetkramāt guruḥ kumbhajalaiḥ kuryātprokṣaṇaṃ pañcapallavaiḥ  k mūlamantreṇa śatadhā śivapaṅktyā trisaptadhā tathaiva siddhapaṅktyā ca gurupaṅktyā tathaiva ca  k śiṣyāya gurubhaktāya śaktiyuktāya dhīmate hārakeyūrakaṭakamudrikāmakuṭāni ca  k vāhanāsanasacchatracāmaravyajanāni ca maṇikuṇḍalayugmaṃ ca bhūtyāḍhyaṃ pātramakṣayam  k saśirastrāṇamuṣṇīṣaṃ paṭṭakūrpāsamuttamam yogapaṭṭaṃ yogadaṇḍaṃ tathaivoḍyāṇabandhanam  k dadyāttasmai tathaivājñāṃ tvamācāryosi saṃprati īśvarosyadya dhanyosi sarveṣāṃ deśiko bhava  k rasāgamānāṃ divyānāṃ vyākhyātā bhava tattvavit ityādiśedguruḥ śiṣyaṃ praṇataṃ guruvatsalam  k iti cācāryadīkṣeyaṃ siddhadīkṣādya kathyate siddhadīkṣānavaṃ saptarātraṃ vā pañcarātraṃ trirātrakam  k vīrāḥ śaktiyutāḥ pūjyāḥ ekaviṃśati cānvaham tatsaṃkhyā yoginaḥ pūjyāḥ kumārāḥ kanyakāḥ striyaḥ  k gandhapuṣpākṣataiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalagandhottamārpaṇaiḥ toṣayitvā pradadyācca vastrābharaṇadakṣiṇāḥ  k athāsanasamāsīnaṃ śiṣyaṃ bhaktiyutaṃ śucim spṛṣṭvā karābhyāṃ tacchīrṣaṃ dakṣiṇe śravaṇe manum  k vahniṃ sabījaṃ śītāṃśuṃ savisargaṃ ca dīkṣayet mūlādhārātsamudbhūtaṃ rephaṃ vahniśikhopamam  k ṣaḍādhārāmbujaṃ tīrtvā brahmarandhrāntagaṃ smaret brahmarandhrāddravībhūtaṃ sakāraṃ somarūpiṇam  k āplāvayantaṃ sarvāṅgaṃ siddhaḥ saṃcintayenmanum ucchvāsaniśvāsabhavaṃ saṃhārasthitikāraṇam  k jñātvetthaṃ manasā nityaṃ sarvamantrātmakaṃ sadā sarvadevamayaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakam  k jīvato muktidaṃ śuddhaṃ śivaśaktyātmakaṃ param rasamantramimaṃ viddhi cāgnīṣomātmakaṃ bhaja  k ekaviṃśatisāhasraṣaṭśatādhikasaṃkhyakam pravartitaṃ divārātraṃ manastatra nidhehi ca  k mantrasyāsya ṛṣirjīvaś chandetyuktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ raso devastu raṃ bījaṃ saṃ śaktistu prakīrtitaḥ  k rephadīrghayutaṃ kuryātkarāṅganyāsamācaret dhyāyeddhṛdambuje devi koṭisūryendusannibham  k śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ rasaṃ saṃsārapāradam evaṃ niṣkalarūpaṃ taṃ dhyātvā tanmayatāṃ vrajet  k niṣkalarasastotramtvaṃ rasastvaṃ śivastvaṃ hi śaktistvaṃ bhairaveśvaraḥ tvaṃ brahmā tvaṃ hi rudraśca sūryastvaṃ śītadīdhitiḥ  k tvaṃ bhūstvaṃ salilastvaṃ ca vahnistvaṃ ca sadāgatiḥ tvaṃ vyoma tvaṃ parākāśaḥ tvaṃ jīvastvaṃ parā gatiḥ  k tvaṃ siddhastvaṃ prabuddhastvaṃ sugandhastvaṃ ca manmathaḥ tvaṃ lokapālastvaṃ tārā mātṛkāstvaṃ gajānanaḥ  k tvaṃ skandastvaṃ gurustvaṃ ca tvaṃ sarvajanakaḥ śuciḥ tvaṃ yajvā tvaṃ haristvaṃ ca tretāgnistvaṃ ca ṛtvijaḥ  k yena tvamarcyase tena pūjitāḥ sarvadevatāḥ tvayi tuṣṭe ca saṃtuṣṭā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  k tvatpādodakapānena sarvatīrthaphalaṃ labhet yastvāṃ paśyati sadbhaktyā tam ālokayate śivaḥ  k yastvāṃ saṃkīrtayettasya sarvamantraphalaṃ bhavet yatra tvaṃ kṣaṇamātre ca puṇyakṣetraṃ taducyate  k tvaṃ yaṃ paśyati siddhendra sa brahmā viṣṇurīśvaraḥ yatra bhuṅkṣe nnakavalaṃ tatra trailokyamati hi  k yena tvaṃ dhriyase nātha tvayāyaṃ striyatekṣaṇam sa eva citsadānandaḥ paramātmā dhruvaṃ bhavet  k evaṃ niścitacittasya siddhasya tava yoginaḥ varṇāśramasadācārāḥ kṛtyākṛtyavivekataḥ  k pāpaṃ puṇyaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ śītamuṣṇaṃ priyāpriye snānāsnānaṃ hānivṛddhī śuddhāśuddhaṃ bhayābhayam  k grāhyāgrāhyaṃ kṣudhā tṛṣṇā na kiṃcid iha vidyate svecchāhāravihāraśca sukhī saṃhṛṣṭamānasaḥ  k nirmamaḥ sarvakāryeṣu kalatrādiṣu bandhuṣu evamācāryavacanamaṅgīkṛtya ca dīkṣitaḥ  k adya prabhṛti vandyastvaṃ mā kuru praṇatiṃ kvacit matsamānosi siddhosi jīvanmuktosi saṃprati  k ityuktvācāryavaryopi siddhamāliṅgya ca kṣaṇam siddhadīkṣeyamākhyātā śivasāyujyadāyinī  k durlabhā sarvatantreṣu tava prītyā prakāśitā devītthameva mantavyaṃ durlabhaṃ samayeṣu ca  k k  rasasaṃkārāḥśrībhairavī rasasaṃskāramīśa tvaṃ yathāvatkathayasva me śrībhairavaḥ aṣṭādaśa syuḥ saṃskārā rasasya parameśvari  k tānsiddhasādhakābhyarcye yathāvatkathayāmi te athādau svedanaṃ karma dvitīyaṃ mardanaṃ priye  k mūrchā tṛtīyamutthānaṃ caturthaṃ pātanaṃ śive pañcamaṃ rodhanaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ niyāmaṃ saptamaṃ smṛtam  k dīpanaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ devi navamaṃ cānuvāsanam daśamaṃ cāraṇaṃ devi jāraṇaṃ rudrasaṃkhyakam  k garbhadrutirdvādaśī syāt bāhyadrutistrayodaśī caturdaśaṃ syādrāgākhyaṃ sāraṇā daśapañcamī  k anusāraṇā ṣoḍaśī ca vikhyātā pratisāraṇā saptadaśī cāṣṭadaśaṃ vedhanaṃ dehalohayoḥ  k rasasaṃskāraprakāraḥatha vakṣyāmi saṃskārān rasarājasya pārvati liṅgasya dakṣiṇe bhāge likhet ṣaṭkoṇamaṇḍale  k tadbahiścāṣṭapatraṃ ca kamalaṃ caturaśrakam digdvāraśobhitaṃ tasya karṇikāyāṃ nyasecchive  k tāmrajaṃ kāntajaṃ vāpi khalvaṃ tu svarṇarekhitam tanmadhye rasarājaṃ tu palānāṃ śatamātrakam  k tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā kṣiptvā bhaktyā prapūjayet sādhako rasarājasya tataḥ saṃskāramācaret  k svedanamdhānyāmlasandhānaprakāraḥyavagodhūmakalamamāṣamudgacaṇādibhiḥ śyāmākakodravādyaiśca nānādhānyaiśca nistuṣaiḥ  k dhānyaṃ caturguṇajale mṛdghaṭe nikṣipetpriye prāpnoti yāvadamlatvaṃ tāvadyatnena rakṣayet  k tanmadhye haṃsapādīṃ ca mīnākṣīṃ dvipunarnavām citrakaṃ bhṛṅgarājaṃ ca viṣṇukrāntāṃ śatāvarīm  k sarpākṣīṃ girikarṇīṃ ca muṇḍīṃ ca sahadevikām triphalāṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ kṛtvā sarvānetānvinikṣipet  k dhānyasya ca caturthāṃśān dhānyāmlamidamuttamam svedanādiṣu kāryeṣu pāradasya viśiṣyate  k ātapte kāntaje khalve rasarājaṃ vinikṣipet cūrṇaṃ ca gṛhadhūmaṃ ca svedayettamaharniśam  k tamuddhṛtya punaḥ soṣṇair āranālaiḥ śarāvake prakṣālayetsūtarājamevaṃ kuryāttrisaptadhā  k prasveditaṃ sūtarājaṃ tataḥ saṃmardayet priye mardanamathāto mardanaṃ karma vakṣyāmi śṛṇu bhairavi  k cūrṇādipūrvavaddravyaṃ viśālāṃ rājavṛkṣakam aṅkolaṃ kṛṣṇadhuttūraṃ trikaṭuṃ ca samaṃ samam  k sarvaṃ sūtakalāṃśaṃ ca taptakhalve rasaṃ kṣipet mardayet pūrvadhānyāmlair divārātraṃ punaśca tam  k kṣālayenmṛṇmaye pātre tataḥ soṣṇāranālakaiḥ mardanaṃ kṣālanaṃ caivamekaviṃśativāsaram  k evaṃ vimarditaṃ sūtaṃ samādāyātha mūrchayet abhrajīrṇothavā bījajīrṇaḥ sūtopi mardyate  k cūrṇādipūrvadravyaiśca rāgān gṛhṇāti nirmalaḥ mūrcchāatha mūrchāṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tvaṃ sāvadhānataḥ  k rājikā meṣaśṛṅgī ca citrakaṃ ca phalatrayam kṣīrakandaṃ sūraṇaṃ ca sarpākṣī kākamācikā  k nīlā vacā balā kanyā kṛṣṇonmattastathākulī śvetāparājitāṅkolaṃ gojihvā garuḍī tathā  k eteṣāṃ svarasairmardyo ravikṣīreṇa pāradaḥ vyastānāṃ vā samastānāṃ rasaireṣāṃ dināvadhi  k mardayettaptakhalve ca mūṣāyāṃ taṃ rasaṃ kṣipet nirudhya bhūdhare yantre vipacettaṃ punaḥ priye  k rājikādyauṣadhabhavai rasais triḥ saptavāsaram mardanaṃ bhūdhare pākaṃ kuryātsaṃmūrchito rasaḥ  k bhavettadutthānavidhiṃ prakurvīta surārcite utthāpanavidhiḥevaṃ saṃmūrchitaṃ sūtaṃ kṣālayetkāṃjikena ca  k soṣṇena vāriṇā vāpi sūtamutthāpayetpriye pātanāyantrayoge vā rasasyotthāpanaṃ bhavet  k pātanampātanaṃ trividhaṃ kṣipet mardayettaptakhalve ca rasaṃ dhānyāmlakena ca  k tatkalkena lipedūrdhvaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ samyak nirodhayet ūrdhvabhāṇḍasya pṛṣṭhe tu dadyāllaghupuṭaṃ tataḥ  k ityadhaḥpātanaṃ kuryātsaptavāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ adhaḥpātanaśuddhasya tiryakpātanamācaret  k tiryakpātanavidhiḥvakṣyāmi tiryakpatanaṃ sūtaṃ dhānyābhrakaṃ samam dhānyāmlairmardayedyāmaṃ tiryakpātanayantrake  k caṇḍāgninā pacedevaṃ saptavāraṃ tāmravatpādamātrakam pāṭhādikarasaiḥ kuryānmardanaṃ pātanaṃ kramāt  k yadyaddravyānvitaḥ sūtas tattaddravyaguṇapradaḥ pātane tāmrayogena nāgavaṅgau tyajedrasaḥ  k athavā dīpikāyantre śuddhaḥ syātpātito rasaḥ nirodhanamkadarthito bhavetsūtaḥ svedādyaiḥ pañcakarmabhiḥ  k āpyāyanārthaṃ sūtasya karma kuryānnirodhanam atha karma nirodhākhyaṃ peṣayellavaṇaṃ jalaiḥ  k sthālīmadhye rasaṃ kṣiptvā tadūrdhvaṃ lavaṇaṃ kṣipet kiṃcij jalaṃ ca nivapettaṃ śarāveṇa rodhayet  k kuryātsamyak sandhilepaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ ca puṭellaghu evaṃ nirodhanaṃ karma vidadhyātsaptadhā priye  k āpyāyito bhavetsūtonena ṣaṇḍatvavarjitaḥ nirodhakarmasiddhosau vīryavān suniyamyate  k niyāmanamatho niyāmanaṃ karma kathayāmi varānane yavaciñcā kṣīrakandaṃ sarpākṣī paṭu bhṛṅgarāṭ  k vandhyā karkoṭakī nimbaḥ sarvaṃ dhānyāmlapeṣitam kṛtvāloḍyāranālena taddravaiḥ svedayeddinam  k yantre niyāmake saptavāsaraṃ taṃ ca dīpayet dīpanamathāto dīpanaṃ karma vadāmi tava pārvati  k svarṇapuṣpī ca marīcaṃ trikṣāraṃ pañcapuṣpikā bhūkhagaḥ pañcalavaṇaṃ rājikā śigrumūlakam  k kāsīsaṃ vijayā kanyā pātālagaruḍī kaṇā kṣīrakandaṃ ca karkoṭī girikarṇī jayā madhu  k citrakaṃ kākajaṅghā ca sarvamamlagaṇena ca  k tumbī tumburur aṅkolabalāpāmārgakāḥ priye gṛhītvaiṣāmekarasaṃ savyoṣaṃ ca sakāṃjikam  k bhāṇḍamadhye vinikṣipya ḍolāyantre pacettryaham pūrvābhraṃ ca tatastasmātsamuddhṛtyātha sādhayet  k ṭaṅkaṇaṃ k piṣṭatāṃ yāti sahasā gaganaṃ carati kṣaṇāt aṣṭamaḥ prakāraḥtrikṣāraṃ pañcalavaṇaṃ kāṅkṣī kāsīsaṭaṅkaṇam  k bhūkhagaṃ hemamākṣīkaṃ saurāṣṭrī vatsanābhakam tuvarī vetasāmlaṃ ca sarvametatsamāṃśakam  k vajrakanakadvandvamelāpralepanam  k guñjā kāntamukhaṃ tulyaṃ dvandvayordviguṇaṃ balim stanyena yoṣitāṃ piṣṭvā mūṣāyāmantare tathā  k melayedvajramelāpoyaṃ kathito mayā dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥśilādhātuḥ biḍaḥ prokto nāmnā jvālāmukhaḥ smṛtaḥ  k  agnijihvakabiḍaḥpalāśasya rasairbhāvyaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ śatadhā priye lohānāṃ jāraṇe śreṣṭho biḍo nāmnāgnijihvakaḥ  k  vaḍabābiḍaḥkāntāsyaṃ gandhakaṃ cūlī caikaikaṃ vahnibiḍaḥjambīrāmlena śatadhā vanaśigrurasena ca  k gandhakaṃ bhāvayedeṣa biḍaḥ syād vahnisaṃjñakaḥ navasāropi ca tathā gandhavatsa biḍo bhavet  k  citrabhānubiḍaḥgandhakaṃ niculakṣāraṃ guṃjābījaṃ ca puṣpaṃ ca khadiraṃ raktacandanaṃ kukkuṭī tathā  k niśādvayaṃ ca saralaṃ devadāruṃ japāsumam anyāni raktapuṣpāṇi lākṣātoyena mardayet  k etaccaturguṇaṃ tailaṃ tailādraktaprasūnajam dravaṃ caturguṇaṃ kṣipettasminpracālayet  k palāśadaṇḍenāmardyaṃ caturyāmena bhasmati tadbhasma gandhakaṃ tulyamamle yāmaṃ prapeṣayet  k ruddhvā puṭedgajapuṭe svāṅgaśītaṃ taduddharet taccaturthāṃśakaṃ gandhaṃ dattvā piṣṭvā puṭe pacet  k evaṃ dvisaptavāreṇa nāgaṃ syādraktavarṇakam vāśāpañcāṅgacūrṇaṃ ca taccūrṇaṃ kakubhasya ca  k śigrukiṃśukakoraṇḍaśākapuṣpāṇi nāginīm ahimāraṃ kumārīṃ ca nāgakanyāṃ ca cūrṇayet  k etatsarvaṃ caikabhāgaṃ dvibhāgaṃ ca manaḥśilām bhāṇḍe sarvaṃ vinikṣipya gavāṃ mūtre caturguṇe  k pacetpādāvaśeṣaṃ tu pūrvanāge kṣipankṣipan cullyāṃ pacedbrahmadaṇḍaiścālayetsaptavāsaram  k idaṃ nāgaṃ pakvabīje drute nirvāhayettridhā rañjitaṃ jāyate bījaṃ mukhyaṃ syādrasarañjane  k bījarañjanaprakāraḥtāpyasatvaṃ ca kṛṣṇābhrasatvacūrṇaṃ dhametsamam tasmindrute tāpyacūrṇaṃ mṛtaśulbaṃ kramādvahet  k triguṇaṃ tadbhavedbījaṃ rañjakaṃ parameśvari anyaḥ prakāraḥkunaṭī mākṣikaṃ gandhaṃ daradaṃ peṣayetsamam  k raktavargasya gomūtre peṣitasya rase priye peṣayecchoṣayet saptavāraṃ taccūrṇayetkṣipet  k dvaṃdvite tīkṣṇatāmre ca tulyaṃ kṣiptvā dhameddṛḍham jyotiṣmatītailayukte raktavarge niṣecayet  k punaśca pūrvacūrṇaṃ tu tulyaṃ kṣiptvā dhamet priye secayet saptadhā tvevaṃ syādbījaṃ rasarañjakam  k anyaḥ prakāraḥtāraṃ ca vimalāsattvaṃ samāṃśaṃ drāvayet tataḥ saraktavarge gomūtre bhāvitaṃ daradaṃ tridhā  k tattulyaṃ nikṣipet tasmin dhamed evaṃ tu saptadhā kṣiptvā kṣiptvā ca daradaṃ syādbījaṃ rasarañjakam  k anyaḥ prakāraḥghanasattvam ahiṃ svarṇaṃ samāṃśaṃ dvaṃdvitaṃ dhamet kharpare raktavargaṃ ca mākṣikaṃ gairikaṃ śilām  k samaṃ saṃcūrṇayet tasmin vāpayecca samaṃ samam daśavāraṃ bhaved etad bījaṃ sūtendrarañjakam  k anyaḥ prakāraḥyavaciñcārasairbhāvyā raktavarṇā manaḥśilā viṃśadvāraṃ prayatnena tena kalkena lepayet  k nāgapatraṃ puṭe pacyādyāvaccūrṇamupāgatam rasakasya tu bhāgāṃstrīn bhāgaikaṃ daradasya ca  k śilāgandhaviṣāṇāṃ ca trayāṇāmekabhāgakam secayenmātuluṅgāmlaiḥ tena kalkena lepayet  k mūṣāgarbhe kṣipet tattatpūrvanāgaṃ dhamet tataḥ drutaṃ yāvat samuddhṛtya liptvā mūṣāṃ punar dhamet  k ityevaṃ saptadhā dhāmyaṃ nāgaṃ svarṇanibhaṃ bhavet anyaḥ prakāraḥpītābhrakasya satvaṃ tu pūrvanāgaṃ ca tatsamam  k dvaṃdvitaṃ pūrvayogena hyabhiṣiktaṃ ca kārayet anena dvandvayogena vāpo deyo drutasya ca  k pakvabījasya vārāṃstrīn tadbījaṃ rañjitaṃ śubham tārabījarañjanamathātas tārabījānāṃ rañjanaṃ śṛṇu pārvati  k nānābhūruhasambhūtaśvetapuṣparase priye caturbhāge caikabhāgaṃ kaṅguṇītailakaṃ kṣipet  k tailāvaśeṣaṃ vipacettārabījāni tatra vai bhūyo bhūyo drāvayitvā secayedekaviṃśatim  k bījāni rañjitānyevaṃ bhaveyū rasarañjane evaṃ vaṅgasya bījāni rañjayet parameśvari  k rañjanakramaḥdrutijīrṇasya sūtasya catuḥṣaṣṭitamāṃśakam nikṣipedrañjakaṃ bījaṃ taptakhalve dināvadhi  k mardayet taptakhalve tu pacet kacchapayantrake evaṃ grāsakrameṇaiva ṣaḍguṇaṃ jārayet priye  k    sāraṇatrayamsāraṇārthe vajrabījasādhanamprathamaḥ prakāraḥrañjitasya rasendrasya pravakṣye sāraṇātrayam sāraṇā yogyabījāni divyāni ca surārcite  k svarṇaṃ dvādaśabhāgaṃ syāt tadardhaṃ śuddhapāradam rasendrārdhaṃ nāgabhasma caturbhāgaṃ mṛtaṃ pavim  k etaccatuṣṭayaṃ cāmlairmardayettaptakhalvake uddhṛtya dvandvamelāpamūṣāyāṃ rodhayeddhamet  k haṭhāttacca milatyeva vajrabījam idaṃ priye dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥbhāvayecchāribākṣīrair mṛtaṃ vajraṃ dinaṃ tataḥ  k mardayed golakaṃ kṛtvā śoṣayeccaikabhāgakam tribhāgaṃ rasarājaṃ ca caturbhāgaṃ suvarṇakam  k amlena mardayet piṣṭiṃ kṛtvā tadvajragolakam tatpiṣṭyā veṣṭayet tacca bhūrjapatreṇa veṣṭayet  k pakṣaṃ nyased dhānyarāśau tad uddhṛtya punaḥ priye dhameddhaṭhānmilatyeva vajrabījam idaṃ bhavet  k vajraṣoḍaśabhāgena svarṇapatreṇa veṣṭayet tatkṣiptvā liptamūṣāyāṃ svarṇāṃśaṃ śvetakācajam  k cūrṇaṃ vā nṛkapālaṃ vā cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā vinikṣipet nirudhya ca dhamet tīvram evaṃ kuryāt punaḥ punaḥ  k kṣiptvā kṣiptvā śvetakācaṃ nṛkapālamathāpi vā saptadhaivaṃ milatyeva vajrabījamidaṃ bhavet  k sāraṇātailamataḥ paraṃ sāraṇāyāṃ pravakṣye tailasādhanam jyotiṣmatīkarañjākṣakaṭutumbīsamudbhavam  k tailaṃ kūrmavarāhādimeṣamatsyasamudbhavam jalūkābhekajātā ca vasā grāhyā vidhānataḥ  k raktavargaḥ pītavargaḥ kvāthyaḥ kṣīraiścaturguṇaiḥ puṣpāṇāṃ raktapītānām anekānāṃ dravaṃ haret  k pāṭalīkākatuṇḍyutthamahārāṣṭrīdravaṃ tathā ekāṃśaṃ tailam ekāṃśā vasā kvāthaścaturguṇaḥ  k dvyaṃśaiḥ puṣpadravair dvyaṃśān pāṭalyādidravānapi sarvaṃ tāmramaye pātre mṛdunā vahninā pacet  k tasminkṣipet ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ bhūlatāmalatāpyakam vikhyātaṃ sāraṇātailaṃ rasarājasya jāraṇe  k rañjitaṃ rasarājaṃ tu sāraṇātailasaṃyutam nikṣipetsāraṇāyantre nālamūṣāṃ gataṃ drutam  k bījaṃ tu ḍhālayetsūte catuḥṣaṣṭitamāṃśakam uddhṛtya taptakhalve tu paṭvamlair mardayeddinam  k tataḥ kacchapayantre tu savivye pācayed dinam ityevaṃ ṣaḍguṇaṃ sāryaṃ sārito jāyate rasaḥ  k evaṃ dvitīyavāre tu kṛte sūtonusāritaḥ tathā tṛtīyavāre tu rasaḥ syāt pratisāritaḥ  k  vedhaḥsāritasya rasendrasya haritālaṃ samāṃśakam mardayed dhūrtatailaiśca dinaṃ divyauṣadhidravaiḥ  k tata uddhṛtya kṣiped vajramūṣāyāṃ vipaceddinam karīṣāgnāviti punar mardyaṃ pācyaṃ tridhā priye  k anena karmaṇā devi sūto baddhamukho bhavet baddhavaktrasya sūtasya bhāgamekaṃ surārcite  k sutāratāmratīkṣṇānāṃ cūrṇānām ekabhāgakam sarvaṃ saṃmardayed devadālīnīrair dinaṃ tataḥ  k madhvājyaiśca dinaṃ mardyaṃ tena kuryāt sugolakam nikṣiped vajramūṣāyāṃ ruddhvā tīvrāgninā dhamet  k sa rasaḥ khoṭabaddhaḥ syāt tatkhoṭaṃ kācaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ tejaḥpuñjo bhavedyāvat tāvat kuryād dhaman dhaman  k taṃ rasaṃ yojayed dehe lohe roge ca pārvati dehavedhakramaḥdehavedhaṃ pravakṣyāmi sāvadhānaṃ śṛṇu priye  k pācanasnehanasvedavamanārecanaiḥ kramāt śarīraṃ śodhayelloṇakṣārāmlādivivarjitaḥ  k tatastvāroṭakaṃ sūtaṃ bhakṣayet parameśvari kṣetraṃ kṛtvā śarīraṃ tu tataḥ siddharasaṃ kṣipet  k śatavedhirasaṃ pūrvaṃ tataḥ sāhasravedhakam daśasāhasravedhaṃ ca lakṣavedhakaraṃ rasam  k vedhakaṃ daśalakṣasya koṭivedhaṃ surārcite gandhakena yutaṃ sūtaṃ krameṇānena suvrate  k sa rasaḥ kramate dehe siddhayaḥ sambhavanti hi rasāyane tu yāḥ proktā mūlikā dehasiddhidāḥ  k tābhiryukto rasendrastu dehe saṃkramate priye krāmati tanau hi sūto janayati putrāṃścadevatāgarbhān  k khe gamanena ca nityaṃ saṃcaraṇaṃ sakalabhuvaneṣu dhātā bhuvanatritaye sraṣṭādyo brahmayoniriva  k viṣṇuriva pālanārthe saṃhartā rudradevavatsatkalam lohavedhakramaḥkrāmaṇaṃ lohavedhasya vakṣyāmi śṛṇu bhairavi  k daradaṃ mākṣikaṃ kāntaṃ śilāṃ gandhaṃ viṣaṃ ghanam rasakaṃ bhūlatāṃ hiṅgu kāntāsyaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ priye  k gandhakena hataṃ tāmraṃ bhujaṅgaṃ śilayā hatam daradena hataṃ tīkṣṇaṃ mahiṣīkarṇasambhavam  k malaṃ vāyasaviṣṭhāṃ ca prathamārtavaraktataḥ anena veṣṭayet siddhasūtaṃ loheṣu vedhayet  k tārakṛṣṭyaṣṭanavatiḥ svarṇamekaṃ tathā rasaḥ śatavedhī tu vikhyātastvevaṃ sāhasravedhakaḥ  k vedhayeddaśasāhasraṃ lakṣaṃ koṭimathārbudam jāraṇāyāṃ balaṃ yāvat tāvallohāni vedhayet  k  krāmaṇayogaḥmākṣikaṃ bhūlatāṃ sūtaṃ kunaṭīṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ tathā strīstanyaraktaṃ sampiṣṭaṃ krāmaṇaṃ kṣepalepayoḥ  k  krāmaṇayogaḥhiṅgulaṃ rasakaṃ kāntam indragopaṃ viṣaṃ tathā mardayet tailaraktābhyāṃ krāmaṇaṃ kṣepalepayoḥ  k  krāmaṇayogaḥgaṇḍolaviṣabhekāsyamahiṣīnetrajaṃ malam rudhireṇa samāyuktaṃ rasasaṃkrāmaṇe hitam  k  krāmaṇayogaḥrocanaṃ gugguluṃ stanyam indragopaṃ viṣaṃ tathā sarvaṃ saṃmardayed devi rasasaṃkrāmaṇe hitam  k  krāmaṇayogaḥviṣṇukrāntā madhūcchiṣṭaṃ māhiṣaṃ karṇajaṃ malam bhūlatā kākaviṣṭhā ca lāṅgalī dvipadīrajaḥ  k nararaktaṃ brahmasomā surasā śailajaṃ priye śṛṅgī ca lakṣmaṇā gṛdhrakarṇī ca krāmaṇaṃ param  k  krāmaṇayogaḥśrīveṣṭanimbaniryāsastrīstanyaviṣaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ goghṛtena samāyukto lohe saṃkrāmate rasaḥ  k  krāmaṇayogaḥparamaṃ krāmaṇaṃ vaṅgaṃ mṛganābhaṃ ca pārvati mātṛvāhaḥ kulīraśca śaṅkhābhyantarajo malaḥ  k tathā kapitthaniryāso rasasaṃkrāmaṇaṃ param krāmaṇaṃ rasarājasya vedhakāle pradāpayet  k k  viśeṣajāraṇākramaḥśrībhairavī sāmānyajāraṇā proktā tvayā pūrvaṃ sadāśiva viśeṣajāraṇaṃ brūhi yathā jānāmyahaṃ prabho  k śrībhairavaḥ śṛṇu devi vakṣyāmi bhūcarākhyaṃ tu jāraṇam bhūcarī jāraṇākṛṣṇaṃ pītaṃ tathā raktaṃ śulbe tīkṣṇe ca melayet  k śulbaṃ śuddhaṃ yadā jīrṇaṃ dvāviṃśatiguṇaṃ mate gandhanāgaṃ tatordhaṃ tu krameṇaiva tu melayet  k hemnā tu saha dātavyaṃ sūtakaikena ṣoḍaśa gandhanāgaṃ yadā jīrṇaṃ tadā baddho bhaved rasaḥ  k hemni jīrṇe tatordhena mṛtalohena rañjayet gandhakena hataṃ śulbaṃ mākṣikaṃ daradāyasam  k puṭena mārayecchuddhaṃ hema dadyāttu ṣaḍguṇam sūtake hemabījaṃ ca yadā jīrṇaṃ caturguṇam  k baddharāgaṃ vijānīyāddhemābho jāyate rasaḥ sāraṇāyantramadhyasthaṃ tenaiva saha sārayet  k tribhāgaṃ sāritaṃ kṛtvā punastatraiva jārayet jāritaḥ sāritaścaiva punarjāritasāritaḥ  k saptaśṛṅkhalikāyogāt koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ bhūcarī jāraṇā proktā khecarīṃ jāraṇāṃ śṛṇu  k khecarī jāraṇāhīnarāgāni ratnāni rasocchiṣṭāni kārayet kaṭutuṃbasya bījāni tasyārdhena tu dāpayet  k mahājārasamāyuktaṃ kalkaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ vajramūṣāmukhe caiva tanmadhye sthāpayed rasam  k katakaṃ kanakaṃ caivam ekīkṛtya vimardayet padmarāgapralepaṃ tu rase grāsaṃ tu dāpayet  k bhakṣitavyaṃ prayatnena natvā ca gurudevayoḥ sarvasiddhān namaskṛtya devatāśca viśeṣataḥ  k mūrcchāṅgadāhaśca tato jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ātmānamutthitaṃ paśyed divyadeho mahābalaḥ  k śaṅkhakāhalanirghoṣaiḥ siddhavidyādharaiḥ saha icchayā vicarellokān kāmarūpī vimānagaḥ  k devā vai yatra līyante siddhastatraiva līyate anyo jāraṇāprakāraḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi jāraṇāyogam uttamam  k sughṛṣṭaṃ pātitaṃ sūtaṃ sarvadoṣojjhitaṃ tataḥ śākapallavasāreṇa viṣṇukrāntārasena ca  k pālāśapuṣpatoyena bhāvitaṃ gandhakaṃ samam samaṃ kṛṣṇābhrasatvaṃ ca rasakaṃ cāṣṭakaṃ guṇam  k tīkṣṇaśulboragaṃ caiva kūrmayantreṇa jārayet kāñcanaṃ jārayet paścād biḍayogena pārvati  k tataḥ siddhaṃ vijānīyād dvaidhaṃ śulvasya dāpayet karmasaṃkhyāpramāṇena nāgo bhavati kāñcanam  k ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi jāraṇākramam uttamam bījacūrṇāni tailena bhāvayitvā punaḥ punaḥ  k ṣoḍaśāṃśena taṃ grāsamaṅgulyā mardayecchanaiḥ ārdrakādi tato yogād dātavyaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśataḥ  k bhūrje dattvā tato deyaṃ ḍolāyantre vinikṣipet ahorātreṇa tadbījaṃ sūtako grasati priye  k samuddhṛtya rasaṃ devi khalve saṃmardayet tataḥ tato yantre vinikṣipya divārātraṃ dṛḍhāgninā  k taptaṃ samuddhṛtaṃ yantrāt taptakhalve vimardayet mardayitvārdrake piṇḍe kṣiptvātha tripuṭaṃ dahet  k tato garbhe patatyāśu jarate tatsukhena tu ḍolāyantre tato dadyād ārdrapiṇḍena saṃyutam  k tṛtīyadivase sūto jarate grasate tataḥ samajīrṇaṃ tato yāvat ḍolāyantre vicakṣaṇaḥ  k paścātkacchapayantreṇa samajīrṇaṃ tu pārvati tāmrāṃśadvādaśāṃśena kacchapena tu jārayet  k prāgvad ārdrakayogaṃ ca garbhadrāvaṇam eva ca paścāt taṃ devi nikṣipya puṭaṃ dadyād vicakṣaṇaḥ  k aṣṭāṃśena tato grāsaṃ garbhadrāvaṃ ca pūrvavat kandodare sūraṇasya taṃ vinikṣipya sūtakam  k puṭayedvārtikastāvat yāvat kando na dahyate pādāṃśena tu mūṣāyāṃ grāsaḥ sūte vidhīyate  k pūrvavacca biḍaṃ dadyādgarbhadrāvaṇameva ca evaṃ caturguṇe jīrṇe sūtako balavān bhavet  k tataḥ śalākayā grāsamagnistho grasate rasaḥ tato ratnāni jāryāṇi vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa tu  k abhrakaṃ bhrāmakaṃ caiva śaṅkhanābhiṃ tathaiva ca rasānuparasāndattvā mahājārasamanvitam  k vajrakandalatāṃ brāhmīmeṣaśṛṅgyamṛtāyasam kaṭutumbasya bījāni mṛtalohāni pācayet  k sarvāṇi samabhāgāni śikhiśoṇitamarditam tāvattaṃ mardayetprājño yāvatkarma dṛḍhaṃ bhavet  k mūṣā mallākṛtiścaiva kartavyācchādanaiḥ saha tanmadhye sthāpayetsūtamadhovātena dhāmayet  k ādau tāvatprakartavyaṃ vajramauṣadhalepitam gṛhyate nātra sandeho yathā tīvrahutāśane  k kuliśādi bhaved dagdhaṃ karīṣā tena mardayet yāvadekādaśaguṇaṃ kuliśaṃ jārayedbudhaḥ  k saṃdagdhā śaṅkhanābhiśca mātuluṅgarasaplutā muktāphalaṃ tato deyaṃ vajrajīrṇe tu sūtake  k anena kramayogena hyekādaśaguṇaṃ bhavet kevalaṃ śikhipittaṃ ca nīlīniryāsamiśritam  k nīlotpalāni liptāni nikṣiptāni tu sūtake rasaḥ pibenmahārāgān hīnarāgān parityajet  k ratnāni śikhipittaṃ ca mahāratnasamanvitam sadratnaṃ lepayet tena prakṣiped rasamadhyataḥ  k rajanī caiva kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ brahmaniryāsabhāvitam jāraṇaṃ puṣparāgasya tenaiva saha dāpayet  k bahuratneṣu jīrṇeṣu bhṛṅgarājeṣu suvrate rasendro dṛśyatāṃ devi nīlapītāruṇacchaviḥ  k dhūmavedhīrasaḥśuddhāni hemapatrāṇi śatāṃśenānulepayet puṭena mārayedetadindragopanibhaṃ bhavet  k saṃsparśād vedhayet sarvam idaṃ hema mṛtaṃ priye tribhāgaṃ sūtakendrasya teneva saha kārayet  k mūṣāmadhye sthite tasmin punastenaiva jārayet dhūmavedhī bhaveddevi punaḥ punaḥ prasāritaḥ  k anena kramayogena yadi jīrṇā triśṛṅkhalā vedhayennātra sandeho giripāṣāṇabhūtalam  k pārśve jyotiḥ pradṛśyeta ūrdhvaṃ dṛśyeta tena vai bhūcaraṃ taṃ vijānīyād rasendraṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ  k tenāśrāntagatir devi yojanānāṃ śataṃ vrajet divyatejā mahākāyo divyadṛṣṭir mahābalaḥ  k sarvarogavinirmukto jīveccandrārkatārakam tasya mūtrapurīṣaṃ tu sarvalohāni vidhyati  k anye vedhaprakārāḥsamajīrṇena vajreṇa hemnā ca sahitena ca agnistho jārayellohān bandham āyāti sūtakaḥ  k sārayettena bījena sahasramapi vedhayet sāritaṃ jārayetpaścāt lepyaṃ kṣepyaṃ sahasrataḥ  k sārayettena bījena lakṣavedham avāpnuyāt anena kramayogena koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ  k kevalaṃ tu yadā vajraṃ samajīrṇaṃ tu kārayet baddhaḥ sūtastadā jñeyo niṣkampo nirupadravaḥ  k agnistho jāyate sūtaḥ śalākāṃ grasate kṣaṇāt haṭhāgninā dhāmyamāno grasate sarvamādarāt  k grasate jarate sūtam āyurdravyapradāyakaḥ mūṣāsthaṃ dhamayet sūtaṃ haṭhāgnau naiva kampayet  k jārayet sarvaratnāni baddhaḥ khecaratāṃ nayet aṣṭalohe ṣṭaguṇite jīrṇe syādrasabandhanam  k lohāni sarvāṃstriguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ kanakaṃ tathā dhūmāvaloke vedhī syāt bhavennirvāṇadombaraḥ  k ādāvaṣṭaguṇaṃ jāryaṃ vyomasattvaṃ mahārase samaṃ hemadaśāṃśena vajraratnāni jārayet  k samaṃ ca jārayed vajraṃ tadāsau khecaro rasaḥ krame pradakṣiṇāvartaḥ koṭivedhī ca jāyate  k jīrṇadravyamānabhedādvedhe viśeṣaḥsame tu pannage jīrṇe daśavedhī bhavedrasaḥ dviguṇe śatavedhī syāt sahasraṃ triguṇe bhavet  k caturguṇeyutaṃ devi krameṇānena vardhayet uttarottaravṛddhyā tu jārayet tatra pannagam  k kuṭilaṃ pannagaṃ jāryaṃ navasaṃkhyākrameṇa tu dattvā krameṇa deveśi koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ  k gandhakādimapāṣāṇe ṣaḍguṇe jīrṇatāṃ gate rogahartā rasaḥ syāttu samukhe tavadā bhavet  k tasmin śataguṇe jīrṇe rugjarāmṛtyuhā bhavet abhrakādimapāṣāṇasattvānyātmasamaṃ grasan  k rugjarā maraṇaṃ jitvā śatavedhī raso bhavet śatāyurdviguṇe jīrṇe sūtaḥ sāhasravedhakaḥ  k caturguṇe sahasrāyuḥ pārado yutavedhakaḥ rasaścāṣṭaguṇe jīrṇe lakṣāyur lakṣavedhakaḥ  k brahmāyuḥ ṣoḍaśaguṇe koṭivedhī bhaved rasaḥ dvātriṃśadguṇite jīrṇe khecaratvādisiddhidaḥ  k viṣṇor āyurbalaṃ datte pāradaḥ sparśavedhakaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇe jīrṇe śivāyuḥ śabdavedhakaḥ  k ṣaḍguṇābhrakajāraṇena sarvadoṣanāśaḥrasasya sarvadoṣāstu ṣaḍguṇenābhrakeṇa tu jīrṇena nāśam āyānti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  k tadā grasati lohāni tyajecca gatim ātmanaḥ pañcāvasthādhūmaściṭiciṭiścaiva maṇḍūkaplutireva ca  k sakampaśca vikampaśca pañcāvasthā rasasya tu samajīrṇo bhavedbālo yauvanasthaścaturguṇaḥ  k vṛddhaḥ ṣaḍguṇajīrṇastu sarvakarmakaraḥ śubhaḥ jāraṇe kramaḥgandhakaṃ jārayedādau sarvasattvānyataḥ param  k tataḥ sarvāṇi lohāni dvandvāni vividhāni ca pakvabījāni ratnāni drutisattve ca jārayet  k catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśake pūrvaṃ dvātriṃśāṃśe tṛtīyakaḥ tṛtīyaḥ ṣoḍaśāṃśe tu caturthaścāṣṭamena ca  k pañcamotha caturthāṃśe ṣaṣṭho dvyaṃśe prakīrtitaḥ śatāṃśe saptamo jñeyo grāsamānaṃ rasasya tu  k grāsamānabhedena svarūpabhedaḥcatuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśake grāse daṇḍadhārī bhaved rasaḥ jalūkābho dvitīye tu grāsayoge sureśvari  k grāse rasāt tṛtīye ca kākaviṣṭhāsamo bhavet caturtho golakākāraḥ pañcame dahanaprabhaḥ  k ṣaṣṭhe sūryaprabhaḥ sūtastejaḥpuñjaśca saptame rasarājasya deveśi kramājjīrṇasya lakṣaṇam  k samāṃśaṃ dviguṇaṃ grāsaṃ tataḥ sūte caturguṇam tathā cāṣṭaguṇaṃ devi jārayecca kalāguṇam  k dvātriṃśadguṇitaṃ devi catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ kramāt saṃskārair jāyamānā guṇāḥtīvratvaṃ janayet svedād amalatvaṃ ca mardanāt  k mūrchanād doṣarāhityam utthānāt pūtināśanam rasāyanaṃ pātanena rodhādāpyāyanaṃ bhavet  k acāpalyaṃ niyamanād dīpanātsamukho jvalet vāsanād yogasāṃgatyaṃ cāraṇādbalacāritā  k jāraṇādbandhanaṃ samyagekatvaṃ drāvaṇadvayāt raktatvaṃ rañjanāt tasya vyāpitvaṃ sāraṇātrayāt  k krāmitvaṃ krāmaṇād dehaloheṣvapi ca vedhanāt  k k  dehavedhakramaḥpraṇamya śirasā śambhuṃ papraccha girijātmajā śrībhairavī dehavedhastvayā pūrvaṃ saṃkṣepāt kathitaḥ prabho  k taṃ dehavedham ācakṣva samyak jānāmyahaṃ yathā śrībhairavaḥ devi pravakṣyāmi devānāmapi durlabham  k yogināṃ bhogayuktānāṃ dehavedhaṃ sureśvari pācanādi prakurvīta pañcakarmavidhānataḥ  k pañcakarmāṇi  pācanamlavaṇādisamutkliṣṭān doṣān saṃśodhayet kramāt tato jīrṇarasaṃ cādyāt kramād evaṃ sureśvari  k laghvāhāro divā bhūtvā kṣudrādhānyākanāgaram etattrayaṃ palonmeyam udakeṣvavaloḍayet  k aṣṭāvaśiṣṭaṃ saṃkvāthya pratirātraṃ pibettryaham anantaraṃ varākvāthaṃ pūrvavat tridinaṃ pibet  k iti pācanam ātanyād atha snehanam ācaret  snehanamghṛtaudanaṃ chāgarasaṃ divā bhuñjīta mātrayā  k ājyānnaṃ vā mudgarasaṃ laghvāśī syāddine sudhīḥ rātrau pibedghṛtaṃ gavyaṃ saindhavena samanvitam  k niṣkamekaṃ saindhavaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ niṣkacatuṣṭayam bhṛṅgāmalakatailena sarvāṅgam abhiṣecayet  k evaṃ saptadinaṃ kuryāt snehanaṃ paramaṃ hitam  svedanammatsyamāṃsaṃ māṣatilayavajāmalasaktavaḥ  k sarvam etad bhavet prastham ekāṣṭhīlāgarūbalā rāsnā vyāghrī ghanāpatraṃ kauśikātiviṣā niśā  k sarvametaddvayapalaṃ takrakṣīrāmbukāṃjikam dvyāḍhake nikṣipet sarvaṃ mṛtpātre kvāthayet sudhīḥ  k kuryāt tasyoṣmaṇā gātraṃ svinnaṃ dvighaṭikāvadhi evaṃ saptadinaṃ kuryāt svedanaṃ paramaṃ hitam  k  vamanammadanasya phalaṃ caikaṃ pāṭhā ṣoḍaśikaṃ jalam pādāvaśiṣṭaṃ saṃkvāthya tajjale vastraśodhite  k pippalīndrayavā yaṣṭilavaṇaṃ karṣamātrakam nikṣipecca pibet prātar vāntiḥ syāt sarvarogahā  k  virecanamsūtaṭaṅkaṇagandhāśma trikaṭuṃ triphalāṃ samam etaiḥ samaṃ tu jepālaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ tat parimardayet  k guñjādvitayamātraṃ tu guḍena saha bhakṣayet virecanam iti proktaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam  k pañcakarmeti kathitaṃ kramāt kuryād virecane doṣaśodhakayogāḥketakīstanajambīraṃ pratyahaṃ kuḍuvaṃ pibet  k saptavāsaraparyantaṃ prātar lavaṇadoṣahṛt salile ṣoḍaśapale triphalaikapalaṃ kṣipet  k kvāthayet pādaśeṣaṃ tat tasmin śīte madhoḥ palam pibet prabhāte tridinaṃ kṣāradoṣaharaṃ param  k viḍaṅgaṃ savacākuṣṭhaṃ ketakīstanasaṃyutam kvathitaṃ tridinaṃ pītamamladoṣaharaṃ pibet  k athavā tintriṇīkṣārasalilaṃ palamātrakam yavakṣārasitākarṣaṃ saṃyojya tridinaṃ pibet  k amladoṣavināśo yaṃ kathitaśca rasāyane vacābiḍālapālāśabījajantughnakarṣakam  k karṣaṃ guḍaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ bhakṣayed uṣṇavāri ca pibet prātastridivasaṃ bhavet tat krimipātanam  k śyāmāvahniviḍaṅgāni vāśā tryūṣaṃ phalatrayam saindhavaṃ devadāruṃ ca mustā caitatsamaṃ samam  k ghṛtaiḥ karṣaṃ lihet prātaḥ saptāhāt sarvarogajit evaṃ kṛtvā dehaśuddhiṃ śālyannaṃ kṣīrabhojanam  k samyagjātabalo bhūtvā tataḥ kuryād rasāyanam rasāyanopayogaḥkṣīrājyāmalakarasakṣaudraiḥ suratarūdbhavam  k tailaṃ nirmathya tatsarvaṃ dvipalaṃ pratyahaṃ pibet māsena kāntirmedhā ca bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ  k dvitīyamāsi pūrvoktaṃ tat pibet taccatuḥpalam tena śāmyanti doṣāśca vikārā netrasambhavāḥ  k punastṛtīye māse tu sevyaṃ ṣaṭpalamātrakam tenāmaravapur bhūyānmahātejā bhaved dhruvam  k āroṭarasasevākramaḥathāroṭarasaḥ sevyaḥ krameṇa parameśvari ayaḥśulbābhratāpyebhyaḥ pātito māritaḥ kramāt  k ayamāroṭakaraso dehasiddhikaraḥ paraḥ svedanādyaiśca saṃskāraiḥ saptabhiḥ saṃskṛto rasaḥ  k mūrchito rañjito devi sūtas tvāroṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ rasāyane rogaśāntyāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvaguṇapradaḥ  k kāntābhrasatvāroṭāśca samaṃ guñjādvayonmitam madhvājyatriphalābhiśca māsamekaṃ bhajediti  k evaṃ krameṇa saṃsevyaṃ dvitrivedeṣuṣaṭkramāt evaṃ ṣoḍaśamāsāntaṃ guñjāṣoḍaśamātrakam  k āroṭakarase cetthaṃ kuryānmatprāṇavallabhe valīpalitanirmukto jīvecca śaradaḥ śatam  k āroṭarasaḥkāntasattvābhrasattvaṃ ca svarṇajīrṇarasastathā sarvametat samīkṛtya bhajed āroṭakaṃ tathā  k kṣetrīkaraṇametaddhi sahasrāyuṣyakārakam abhūmau yojitaḥ sūto na prarohati kutracit  k tasmātkṣetramakṛtvaiva yojayed yastu sūtakam na prarohedasya śubhaṃ bījam ivoṣare  k khoṭabaddharasasevākramaḥpūrvoktakhoṭabaddhasya sūtasya vidhim uttamam krāmaṇaṃ ca kramādvakṣye tathā vidhiniṣedhanam  k śṛṇu pārvati yatnena tvatprītyā kathayāmyaham kāntābhrasvarṇavajrāṇi rasasya krāmaṇaṃ param  k krāmaṇena vinā sūto na sidhyed dehalohayoḥ guñjāmātraṃ khoṭabaddhaṃ krāmaṇakṣaudrasaṃyutam  k māsamekaṃ bhajed itthaṃ punar vidhikrameṇa vai māsaṣoḍaśaparyantaṃ yathāroṭarasastathā  k sa śatāyuṣyam āpnoti sarvarogavivarjitaḥ palamātropayogena vyādhibhir nābhibhūyate  k dvitīye śukravṛddhiḥ syāt tṛtīye balavān bhavet caturthe palitaṃ hanti valiṃ jayati pañcame  k ṣaṣṭhe śrutidharo vāgmī saptame netrarogahṛt aṣṭame tārkṣyadṛṣṭiḥ syād brahmāyurbrahmavikramaḥ  k upayuñjyānnavapalaṃ siddhimelāpakaṃ bhavet viniyuñjyād daśapalaṃ dvitīyaḥ śaṅkaro bhavet  k sahasrāyuṣyakaraṃ sūtaṃ māṣamātraṃ bhajennaraḥ ayutāyuṣkaraṃ sūtaṃ yavamātraṃ bhajetpriye  k lakṣāyuṣyakaraṃ sūtaṃ vrīhimātraṃ bhajetsudhīḥ koṭyāṃ bhajet sūtaṃ khādayan mudgamātrakam  k etat sarvaṃ rasānāṃ tu krāmaṇaṃ pūrvavad bhavet sahasrāyuḥpradaḥ sūto brahmatvaṃ vidadhāti saḥ  k ayutāyuṣkaraḥ sūto viṣṇutāṃ pradadāti ca lakṣāyuṣyakaraḥ sūto rudratvam upapādayet  k koṭyāyuṣyapradaḥ sūtaḥ śivatvaṃ vidadhāti ca mākṣīkajīrṇasūtastu dhanadatvaṃ dadāti vai  k indratvaṃ vimalājīrṇastvabhrajīrṇorkatāṃ dadet brahmatāṃ śulbajīrṇaśca viṣṇutāṃ tārajāritaḥ  k rudratā hemajīrṇe syādīśatvaṃ vajrajārite sadāśivatvaṃ ca dadetpārado drutijāritaḥ  k saccidānandarūpatvaṃ sūtako bījajāritaḥ sāmānyena tu tīkṣṇena rudratvaṃ prāpnuyānnaraḥ  k evaṃ yo lohajīrṇaṃ tu bhakṣayed bhasmasūtakam jalena jalarūpī syātsthalena sthalatāṃ vrajet  k tejastvaṃ tejasā devi vāyunā vāyurūpabhāk kartā hartā svayaṃ sākṣācchāpānugrahakārakaḥ  k yatra mūtrapurīṣaṃ tu sādhakastu parityajet pāṣāṇaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ tatra spṛṣṭaṃ bhavati kāñcanam  k prasvedāt tasya gātrasya lohānyaṣṭau ca vedhayet tatsarvaṃ kanakaṃ divyaṃ bhakṣite dvādaśe pale  k athavā tārajīrṇaṃ tu bhakṣayed bhasmasūtakam śulbāraṃ vaṅgaghoṣaṃ ca tatsvedāt tāratā bhavet  k athavā tīkṣṇajīrṇaṃ tu bhakṣayed bhasmasūtakam mūtreṇa tasya spṛṣṭaṃ tu vaṅgaṃ vrajati tāratām  k ekaikena niṣekena stambhanaṃ nāgavaṅgayoḥ guñjāmātraṃ rasaṃ devi hemajīrṇaṃ tu bhakṣayet  k dviguñjaṃ tārajīrṇasya ravijīrṇasya ca trayam tīkṣṇābhrakāntamāṣaikaṃ guṃjaikā dvethavā bhavet  k vajravaikrāntajīrṇaṃ tu bhakṣayet sarṣaponmitam nāgavaṅgavasākīṭaviṣopaviṣasaṃyutam  k mūtrayuktaṃ haṭhād baddhaṃ tyajet kalkaṃ rasāyane hematārapraveśena jāto yognisahaḥ kramāt  k baddhaśca rasarājoyaṃ dehasiddhiprado bhavet vajrāyaskāntamākṣīkavaikrāntābhrakakāñcanam  k etairjīrṇo yathālābhaṃ rasaḥ śasto rasāyane ṣaḍ evoparasāścaiva bhakṣaṇārthaṃ rasāyane  k bhasmanastīkṣṇajīrṇasya palam ekaṃ tu bhakṣayet daśavarṣasahasrāṇi vajrakāyaḥ sa jīvati  k evaṃ ca dvādaśapalaṃ tīkṣṇajīrṇasya bhakṣayet evaṃ jīvanmahākalpaṃ pralayānte śivaṃ vrajet  k bhasmanaḥ śulbajīrṇasya palena brāhmamāyuṣam dvipale vaiṣṇavāyuṣyaṃ rudrāyustripalena tu  k caturthe tu pale devi śivatvaṃ prāpnuyānnaraḥ hemajīrṇe bhasmasūte tripale bhakṣite kramāt  k aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi yoginyo madadarpitāḥ tasya tiṣṭhanti kiṃkaryaḥ kāmarūpī bhavennaraḥ  k yad yad bhāvayate rūpaṃ tattadrūpadharo bhavet yatra yatra vilīyante siddhistatraiva līyate  k mite pale dvādaśabhir hemabhasmani bhakṣite guṃjaikamātraṃ deveśi jñātvā cāgnibalaṃ nijam  k ghṛtena madhunā cādyāt tāmbūlaṃ kāminīṃ bhajet eko hi doṣaḥ sūkṣmopi bhakṣite bhasmasūtake  k triḥsaptāhādvarārohe kāmāndho jāyate naraḥ kāminīnāṃ sahasraṃ tu kṣobhayed divasāntare  k nārīsaṅgād varārohe dehe krāmati sūtakaḥ nārīsaṅgād vinā devi hyajīrṇaṃ tasya jīryate  k maithunāccalite śukle trisaptāhād adhaḥ kṛtāt jāyate prāṇasaṃdehas tāvanmaithunaṃ tyajet  k yuvatyā jalpanaṃ kāryaṃ yuvatyā cāṅgamardanam yasyāḥ sparśanamātreṇa rasaḥ krāmati vigrahe  k yathā tathā hlādayate sustrīrūpanirīkṣaṇam tathā krāmati deveśi sūtakosau tataḥ kṣaṇāt  k aśvatthasadṛśo yasyā ādhāraśca samaḥ śubhaḥ tādṛśastu bhago devi bhājane tu rasāyane  k nirmāṃsaścaiva dīrghaśca bhagaḥ śuṣkaśirāstathā duḥkhadāridryakartāraṃ varjayettaṃ rasāyane  k pakṣe śukle śubhadine candratārābalānvite sumuhūrte cintya śivānalavipragurūndvijaḥ  k saṃtuṣṭaḥ sumanā bhūtvā rasaṃ seveta siddhidam payasā hemaśuṇṭhībhyāṃ nasyaṃ krāmaṇamuttamam  k hemādi ṣaḍlohakṛtam añjanaṃ krāmaṇaṃ param rasasevāyāṃ pathyāpathyamataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rasasevāhitāhitam  k raktaśālyannagodhūmaṃ gavyaṃ kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ dadhi jāṅgalaṃ palalaṃ mudgaṃ śarkarā madhu saindhavam  k haṃsodakaṃ vāstukaṃ ca meghanādaḥ punarnavā paṭolālābukadalīdhānyakekṣukadāḍimam  k nālikerāmbu viśvaṃ ca sadā asthānamadahāsāśca harṣaḥ kopodhikaspṛhā bahujalpo jalakrīḍā duḥkham atyantacintanam  k kaliṅgaṃ kāravellaṃ ca kūṣmāṇḍaḥ karkaṭī tathā kākamācī kulatthaṃ ca kārkoṭī ca kusumbhikā  k tilātasītailamāṣakapotakamasūrakāḥ takrabhaktaṃ ca sauvīraṃ tiktakaṭvamlalāvaṇam  k kṣāraṃ kṣaudraṃ picchilaṃ ca pittalaṃ ca parūṣakam māhiṣīḥ kṣīravikṛtīr vidaraṃ sahakārakam  k  k mayūrapittaṃ tailaṃ ca lipetsarṣapasaṃbhavam abhāve tailapittasya cūlikālavaṇaṃ balim  k jambīrasya rasairmardyaṃ taṃ rasaṃ hemapatrakam pācayetpūrvavadvahnau jambīrasya rasaiḥ punaḥ  k sampūrṇāṃ ṣoḍaśamāsāntājjarāvyādhibhirujjhitaḥ  k kāntasya sevayā paścādbhavetkāntābhrakārhakaḥ kāntābhrarasāyanammṛtaṃ kāntaṃ ghanaṃ tulyaṃ dhātrībhṛṅgapunarnavāḥ  k dravaireṣāṃ pṛthaṅmardyaṃ kalye guñjādvayaṃ guḍūcītriphalākvāthaṃ palaṃ cānupibetsudhīḥ  k aṣṭaguñjāvadhir vṛddhir bhavet ṣoḍaśamāsataḥ tejasvī balavāndhīmāṃścakṣuṣmān rogavarjitaḥ  k valīpalitanirmuktastrikālaviṣajidbhavet syāt paramāvadhiḥ māsaṣoḍaśayogena valīpalitavarjitaḥ  k taptakāñcanasacchāyaḥ pañcabāṇa ivāparaḥ hemakāntāsvādanena kāntābhrakanakārhakaḥ  k svarṇābhrakāntarasāyanampūrvavanmārayetsvarṇaṃ vajrarasāyanampūrvavadbhasmayed vajraṃ dhātrīnīreṇa mardayet  k bhāvayetsaptadhā dhīmānvrīhimātraṃ lihetpriye ghṛtakṣaudrayutaṃ cānupibeddhātrīrasaṃ palam  k vallāvadhir bhavedvṛddhirmāsaṣoḍaśayogataḥ cirajīvī vajrakāyo divyadṛṣṭir mahābalaḥ  k vajrasya sevayā yogyo bhavedvajrābhrabhakṣaṇe vajrābhrarasāyanampūrvavanmārayedvyoma vajraṃ vajrāccaturguṇam  k ghanaṃ dhātryāḥ śatāvaryā rasair bhāvyaṃ trisaptadhā yavamātraṃ lihetprātarmadhvājyābhyāṃ lihedanu  k dhātrīśatāvarīnīraṃ krāmaṇaṃ palamātrakam caturguñjā parā vṛddhirbhavetṣoḍaśamāsataḥ  k vāksiddhir divyadṛṣṭiḥ syāddevatāsadṛśaprabhaḥ sevayā ghanavajrasya kāntavajrārhako bhavet  k kāntavajrarasāyanampūrvavadbhasmayedvajraṃ kāntaṃ vajrāccaturguṇam kāntaṃ trisaptadhā bhāvyamaśvagandhāvarārasaiḥ  k yavamātraṃ kṣaudraghṛtairyuktaṃ sevayā vajrakāntasya vajrakāntābhrakārhakaḥ  k vajrābhrakarasāyanampūrvavanmārayedvajraṃ kāntābhrāṇi ca hīrakāt caturguṇe ca kāntābhre varābhṛṅgakuraṇḍajaiḥ  k rasaistrisaptadhā bhāvyaṃ yavamātraṃ priye  k ghanādijāritaṃ sūtaṃ mārayetpūrvavatsudhīḥ tasmādbhasmīkṛtāt sūtād dviguṇaṃ hemabhasma ca  k hematulyaṃ mṛtaṃ kāntaṃ kāntatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ ghanam etat sarvaṃ varākvāthamuṇḍībhṛṅgarasair dinam  k saṃpuṭake pacet kṛte laghupuṭe paścādbhāvyaṃ bhṛṅgavarārasaiḥ  k trisaptadhā samadhvājyaṃ māṣamātraṃ pibedanu gavyaṃ kṣīrapalaṃ peyaṃ vṛddhirguñjāṣṭakāvadhiḥ  k evaṃ ṣoḍaśamāsena jīvedācandratārakam etasya sevayā kāntavajrasūtārhako bhavet  k kāntavajrajīrṇarasabhasmakāntaṃ vajraṃ samaṃ jāryaṃ samukhe pārade priye kāntahīrakajīrṇaṃ taṃ pāradaṃ mārayetsudhīḥ  k pūrvoktavidhinā kānte etatpāradabhasma ca pāradāddviguṇaṃ vajraṃ vajrātkāntaṃ caturguṇam  k palāśapuṣpasvarasairdinaṃ mardyaṃ ca saṃpuṭe ruddhvā kukkuṭake paścāttamādāyātha bhāvayet  k palāśapuṣpanīreṇa bhāvayettaṃ trisaptadhā samadhvājyaṃ māṣamātraṃ lihedanu pibetpayaḥ  k aṣṭaguñjāvadhir vṛddhir bhavetṣoḍaśamāsataḥ valīpalitanirmukto jīvedācandratārakam  k etasya sevayā vajrarasakāntābhrakārhakaḥ kāntavajrābhrakajīrṇarasabhasmasamukhe pārade vyomakāntavajrāṇi ca kramāt  k samāni jārayetpaścājjīrṇaṃ taṃ mārayedrasam pūrvavatpāradādvajraṃ samaṃ vajracaturguṇam  k kāntaṃ kāntasamaṃ vyomasatvaṃ caitāni mardayet triphalābhṛṅgajarasai ruddhvā saṃpuṭake pacet  k laghunāgnipuṭenaiva tamādāyātha bhāvayet varābhṛṅgarasair ekaviṃśatiṃ vāramātape  k māṣamātraṃ samadhvājyaṃ lihetprātarviśuddhadhīḥ anupeyaṃ ca gokṣīraṃ vṛddhirguñjāṣṭakaṃ bhavet  k māsaṣoḍaśayogena jīvedācandratārakam etasya sevayā hemavajrasūtārhako bhavet  k svarṇavajrajīrṇarasabhasmasamukhe pārade tulye hema vajraṃ ca jārayet taṃ rasaṃ bhasmayeddevi rasaṃ vajraṃ samaṃ samam  k tayoḥ samaṃ mṛtaṃ hema varākvāthena mardayet tatsarvaṃ saṃpuṭe kṣiptvā bhūdharākhye puṭe pacet  k tamādāya varākvāthairbhāvayecca trisaptadhā māṣamātraṃ lihetprātastilājyamadhusaṃyutam  k gokṣīramanupeyaṃ syādaṣṭaguñjāvadhi kramāt māsaṣoḍaśaparyantaṃ jīyād ācandratārakam  k etasya sevayā vyomahemavajrarasārhakaḥ svarṇavajrābhrakajīrṇarasabhasmasamukhe pārade vyomahemavajrāṇi jārayet  k pāradasya samāṃśāni tataḥ sūtaṃ vimārayet rasatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ vajraṃ tayostulyaṃ ca hāṭakam  k sarvatulyaṃ rasaṃ vyoma tatsarvaṃ brahmabījakaiḥ tailaistryahaṃ peṣayitvā saṃpuṭedbhūdhare puṭe  k taṃ palāśakaṣāyeṇa bhāvanāścaikaviṃśatiḥ taṃ rasaṃ māṣamātraṃ ca tailaṃ brahmadrubījakam  k karṣamātraṃ pibeccānu yāvadguñjāṣṭakāvadhi māsaṣoḍaśayogena siddho bhavati śāśvataḥ  k etasya sevayā kāntahemavajrarasārhakaḥ svarṇakāntavajrajīrṇarasabhasmamukhīkṛte sūtarāje kāntaṃ svarṇaṃ samaṃ samam  k jārayedbhasmayettaṃ ca tatsamaṃ vajrabhasma ca tayostulyaṃ mṛtaṃ hema kāntaṃ sarvasamaṃ priye  k varābhṛṅgarase piṣṭvā bhūdhare saṃpuṭe pacet tato bhṛṅgavarānīrairekaviṃśatibhāvanāḥ  k varākṣaudrair lihet prātarmāṣamātraṃ rasaṃ sudhīḥ gavyaṃ payaḥ palaṃ peyaṃ vṛddhiḥ ṣoḍaśamāṣikā  k māsaṣoḍaśayogena bhavet siddhasamaḥ prabhuḥ etasya sevayā vyomakāntahemapavīrasam  k sevituṃ jāyaterhosau saṃyatātmā maheśvaraḥ svarṇakāntavajrābhrakajīrṇarasabhasmaghanakāntasvarṇavajraṃ jārayet samukhe rase  k pratyekaṃ pāradasamameva kāryaṃ sureśvari tatastaṃ mārayedyuktyā rasatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ pavim  k tayostulyaṃ mṛtaṃ hema sarvatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ ghanam ghanatulyamayaskāntaṃ sarvatulyaṃ suradrujaiḥ  k tailaistataḥ saṃpuṭe ca kṣiptvā bhūdharake pacet guñjāmātraṃ rasaṃ caitaṃ lihet prātaḥ śuciḥ sudhīḥ  k devadārujatailena karṣamātraṃ tu pārvati dhāroṣṇaṃ gopayaḥ peyaṃ palamātramanu priye  k guñjāṣoḍaśaparyantaṃ māsaṣoḍaśayogataḥ ya imaṃ pāradaṃ divyaṃ sevate pathyabhuksadā  k vyādhijanmajarāmṛtyuvarjitaḥ sarvasiddhibhāk sarvajñaḥ sarvagaḥ siddhaḥ sṛjatīva pitāmahaḥ  k viṣṇuvattrāyate viśvaṃ haratīva haraḥ svayam vāñchitārthān svayaṃ datte kalpadruma ivāparaḥ  k kandarpa iva kāmākṣīḥ sahasraṃ ramayet kṣaṇāt saccidānandarūpoyaṃ rasasevī bhaveddhruvam  k ghanādipañcayogotthamekatriṃśadrasāyanam bhavatsnehena kathitaṃ rahasyaṃ devadurlabham  k k  ghuṭikāsiddhiḥpraṇamya parayā bhaktyā bhairavaṃ bhairavī śivam uvāca vinayenedaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāṃkṣiṇī  k śrībhairavī devadeva kṛpāmūrte sarvānugrāhaka prabho tvatprasādānmayā jñātaṃ rahasyam atidurlabham  k kāntābhrahemakuliśarasabhasma rasāyanam ataḥ paraṃ mahādeva śrotumicchāmi bhairava  k etair ghanādyai racitaghuṭikānāṃ rasāyanam śrutvā savinayaṃ vākyaṃ bhairavyāstvādibhairavaḥ  k sthitvetyuvāca vacanaṃ tadvakṣyāmi rasāyanam śrībhairavaḥ  sañjīvanī ghuṭikāśṛṇu pārvati yatnena sāvadhānena sāmpratam  k prathamaṃ jāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ paścātpāradabandhanam tasmājjāraṇabījāni ghanādīnāṃ vadāmi te  k gandhatālaśilātutthakharparīhiṅgulāmalāḥ bhūnāgatāpyakāsīsanṛpāvartābhragairikam  k kāntatrikṣāravaikrāntāstvete cūrṇasamāṃśakaḥ siddhacūrṇamidaṃ khyātaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ syād bījakarmaṇi  k dvandvamelopaliptāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ nikṣipetpriye kṛṣṇasatvābhrasatvaṃ ca drāvayetsamaśulbakam  k samitrapañcakaṃ tasminsiddhacūrṇaṃ muhurmuhuḥ ghanāddaśaguṇaṃ kṣepyaṃ dhamedgāḍhaṃ varānane  k ghanasatvāvaśiṣṭaṃ syāddhamanīyaṃ ca tāvatā kālenedaṃ vyomasatvabījaṃ jāryaṃ rasāyane  k samukhe pārade bījaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśake kṣipet taptakhalvemlavargeṇa mardayed divasatrayam  k taṃ sūtaṃ kacchape yantre sabiḍe jārayetpriye tato dvātriṃśadaṃśaṃ ca ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ rasasya tu  k aṣṭamāṃśaṃ caturthāṃśaṃ dvyaṃśaṃ caiva samāṃśakam pārade jārayedevaṃ kramādbījaṃ sureśvari  k sūtamevaṃvidhaṃ vyomasatvaṃ bījasamaṃ priye taptakhalvemlavargeṇa mardayedekavāsaram  k piṣṭiṃ pāradarājaṃ taṃ jambīrāntarvinikṣipet dolāyantremlayukte taṃ vipacetsaptavāsaram  k tamādāya baliṃ kṣiptvā siddhacūrṇena pārvati tatastaṃ bhūdhare yantre pacellaghupuṭena ca  k yāvatkaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvatkāryaṃ muhurmuhuḥ dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharake puṭam  k mṛtasañjīvanī nāmnā ghuṭikā sarvasiddhidā vaktrāntare gale mūrdhni bāhau karṇethavā vahet  k hemnā suveṣṭitā samyagvalīpalitanāśinī vaktrasthā mṛtyuhā varṣādviṣavigrahanāśinī  k śuddhaṃ gandhaṃ karṣamātraṃ gavyaṃ kṣīraṃ palaṃ pibet anena kramaṇenaiva sūtaḥ saṃkramate tanum  k  divyā ghuṭikākāntamlecchamukhaṃ rūpyaṃ liptamūṣāntare samam drāvayitvā siddhacūrṇaṃ kāntāddaśaguṇaṃ śanaiḥ  k vahenmuhurmuhurdrāvyaṃ yāvatkāntovaśiṣyate kāntabījamidaṃ proktaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ jāryaṃ rasāyane  k samukhe pārade cedaṃ bījaṃ cāryaṃ ca pūrvavat catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakaṃ pūrvaṃ samāṃśaṃ taṃ krameṇa vai  k evaṃvidhaṃ sūtarājaṃ kāntabījaṃ dvayaṃ samam mardayettaptakhalve ca sāmlavarge dinatrayam  k piṣṭībhūtaṃ ca jambīre kṣiptvāmlagaṇapūrite dolāyantre pacetsamyagevam ā saptavārakam  k tamādāya lihedbāhye siddhacūrṇena bhairavi tato divyauṣadhairlipte saṃpuṭe bhūdhare pacet  k yāvatkaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvatkuryātkrameṇa ca dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharapācanam  k puṭe tau jārayed divyanāmnātha parameśvari vaktrāntare gale mūrdhni bāhau karṇethavā vahet  k hemnā suveṣṭitaṃ dhāryaṃ valīpalitanāśanam pūrvavatphaladā puṇyā dhāryā yatnena mānavaiḥ  k pūrvavatkrāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ dehe saṃkramate rasaḥ  kāmeśvarī ghuṭikāsamukhe pārade vyomakāntabījaṃ ca mārayet  k pratyekaṃ pāradasamaṃ pūrvavacca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakaṃ cādau samāṃśaṃ taṃ kramādrase  k asya sūtasya tulyāṃśaṃ kāntabījābhrabījakam taptakhalvemlavargeṇa mardayedvāsaratrayam  k piṣṭīkṛtaṃ ca jambīre kṣiptvā dolāgataṃ pacet punarādāya tāṃ piṣṭiṃ siddhacūrṇena lepayet  k divyauṣadhigaṇairlipte saṃpuṭe bhūdhare pacet yadā kaṭhinatāṃ yāti dvidhā kuryātkrameṇa tu  k dolāsvedaṃ cūrṇalepaṃ kṛtvā bhūdharapācanam kāmeśvarīyaṃ ghuṭikā vaktrasthā sarvasiddhidā  k pūrvavatkrāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ rasendraḥ krāmate tanum  hemasundarī ghuṭikāsvarṇaṃ rūpyaṃ mlecchamukhaṃ kāntasatvābhrasatvakam  k dvandvamelopaliptāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ tadvinikṣipet tasmindrute siddhacūrṇaṃ svarṇāddaśaguṇaṃ kṣipet  k yāvatsvarṇāvaśeṣaṃ syāttāvaddrāvyaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ hemabījam idaṃ khyātaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rasarasāyane  k samukhe pārade devi bījaṃ rasasamaṃ kramāt jārayet pūrvavaddevi catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam  k etadrasaṃ hemabījaṃ samaṃ khalve ca tāpite mardayed amlavargeṇa tryahāt piṣṭir bhavedrasaḥ  k piṣṭiṃ jambīrajāṃ kṛtvā dolāyantremlapūrite ṣaḍahaṃ pācayeddevi siddhacūrṇapralepanam  k tathā saṃpuṭalepaṃ ca tathā bhūdharapācanam yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvatkuryācca pūrvavat  k iyaṃ tu ghuṭikā divyā vikhyātā hemasundarī vaktrasthā siddhidā nḥṇāṃ jarāmṛtyuviṣāpahā  k pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ sūtaḥ saṃkramate punaḥ  madanasundarī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte rase vyomabījaṃ hāṭakabījakam  k samaṃ samaṃ kramājjāryaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam ityevaṃ jāritaṃ sūtaṃ bījaṃ gaganarukmayoḥ  k mardayet pāradasamaṃ taptakhalvemlavargataḥ tridinājjāyate piṣṭiḥ punar jambīragām kuru  k dolāyantremlabharite pacettāṃ saptavāsaram lepanaṃ siddhacūrṇasya tathā saṃpuṭalepanam  k tathā bhūdharapākaśca yāvatkaṭhinatāṃ vrajet siddhidā ghuṭikā hyeṣā nāmnā madanasundarī  k āsyāntarasthitā kuryāt sarvasiddhīś cirāyuṣaḥ vyālavyāghragajādīnāṃ rājñāṃ vaśyaṃ striyāmapi  k pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ kāyam ākrāmate rasaḥ  khecarī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte rase kāntahemabījaṃ samaṃ samam  k rasonmite pṛthak jāryaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam itthaṃ jīrṇaṃ rasaṃ bījaṃ kāntahemno rasonmitam  k pūrvavat piṣṭikāṃ kṛtvā dolāyantre ca pācanam yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvat kāryaṃ muhurmuhuḥ  k ghuṭikā jāyate nāmnā khecarī sarvasiddhidā pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ sugandhaṃ gopayaḥ pibet  k tena saṃkramate dehaṃ ghuṭikāntargato rasaḥ  vajreśvarī ghuṭikāsamukhe pārade vyomakāntahemnāṃ samaṃ samam  k bījaṃ pṛthakpṛthak jāryaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam itthaṃbhūtasya sūtasya samaṃ vyomādibījakam  k trayaṃ tāpitakhalvena tryahamamlena mardayet sa sūtaḥ piṣṭim āpnoti tāṃ piṣṭiṃ pūrvavatpriye  k dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharapācanam yāvatkaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvatkāryam atandritaiḥ  k vajreśvarīti ghuṭikā vaktrasthā sarvasiddhidā pūrvavatkrāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ gātraṃ vyāpnoti pāradaḥ  k  mahāvajreśvarī ghuṭikāśuddhaṃ svarṇaṃ vajrabhasma lohacūrṇābhrasatvakam etaccatuḥsamaṃ nāgaṃ mūṣāyāṃ cāndhritaṃ dhamet  k dvandvamelopaliptāyāṃ punarādāya taṃ priye ekībhūtaṃ ca mūṣāyāṃ prakaṭaṃ ca dhametpunaḥ  k dhautasattvaṃ mākṣikaṃ ca svalpaṃ svalpaṃ muhuḥ kṣipet vajrahemāvaśeṣaṃ tu yāvatsyāt tata uddharet  k etasmin vyomasatvāyaścūrṇanāgāṃśca pūrvavat dvandvamelopaliptāyām andhrayitvā dṛḍhaṃ dhamet  k ekībhūtaṃ samādāya mūṣāyāṃ prakaṭaṃ dhamet hemavajrāvaśeṣaṃ syād yāvat tat punarāharet  k vyomasatvam ayaścūrṇaṃ nāgaṃ vāhyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ pūrvavat kramayogena mākṣikaṃ dhautasattvakam  k muhuḥ kṣipya dhamettaṃ tu bāhyamevaṃ tu ṣaḍguṇam vajrabījamidaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ jāryaṃ rasarasāyane  k samukhe pārade jāryaṃ vajrabījaṃ rasonmitam catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādyaṃ ca kramāt saṃkrāmayet priye  k itthaṃ jāritasūtasya samaṃ kuliśabījakam taptakhalvemlavargeṇa mardayed divasatrayam  k sa piṣṭir jāyate sūtastāṃ piṣṭīṃ ca samāharet dolāpākaḥ siddhacūrṇalepaḥ sampuṭabhūdharam  k kurvīta pūrvavat sarvaṃ yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ vrajet mahāvajreśvarī nāmnā ghuṭikā siddhidāyinī  k vaktrasthā krāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ pūrvavat krāmate rasaḥ  vajrakhecarī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte rase vyomavajrabījaṃ rasonmitam  k pṛthak pṛthak jāraṇīyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam amuṣya jīrṇasūtasya samaṃ vajrābhrabījakam  k taptakhalvemlavargeṇa tridinaṃ mardayeddṛḍham sa raso jāyate piṣṭistāṃ punaḥ pūrvavatpriye  k dolāsvedaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharapācanam yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ yati tāvad evaṃ muhurmuhuḥ  k ghuṭikā jāyate divyā nāmneyaṃ vajrakhecarī vaktrasthā siddhidā nṛṇāṃ pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ priye  k  kālavidhvaṃsinī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte rase kāntavajrabījaṃ rasonmitam pṛthakpṛthag jāraṇīyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam  k asya jīrṇasya sūtasya samaṃ kuliśakāntayoḥ bījaṃ saṃtaptakhalve mlavarge mardyaṃ dinatrayam  k piṣṭir bhavatyeṣa sūtaḥ piṣṭiṃ tāṃ punarāharet dolāsvedaḥ siddhacūrṇalepaḥ saṃpuṭabhūdharam  k yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvadevaṃ muhurmuhuḥ kālavidhvaṃsinī nāmnā ghuṭikā jāyate śubhā  k mukhasthā siddhidā divyā pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ pibet  gaganeśvarī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte sūtarāje vajrakāntābhrabījakam  k pṛthakpṛthaksūtarāje catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam rasasya tasya sadṛśaṃ vajrabījābhrabījakam  k taptakhalvemlavargeṇa tryahāt piṣṭiḥ sumardanāt dolāpākaḥ siddhacūrṇalepaḥ saṃpuṭabhūdharam  k yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvat kuryānmuhurmuhuḥ gaganeśvarīyaṃ ghuṭikā vaktrasthā sarvasiddhidā  k pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ kāryaṃ dehe krāmati sūtakaḥ  vajraghaṇṭeśvarī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte sūtarāje bījaṃ vajrasuvarṇayoḥ  k pṛthakpṛthaksamaṃ jāryaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam asya sūtasya sadṛśaṃ hemno vajrasya bījakam  k taptakhalvemlavargeṇa tryahāt piṣṭir bhavedrasaḥ tāṃ piṣṭiṃ punarādāya pūrvavat parikalpayet  k dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharapācanam yāvat kaṭhinatāṃ yāti tāvat kuryānmuhurmuhuḥ  k vajraghaṇṭeśvarī hyeṣā ghuṭikā siddhidāyinī mukhasthā siddhidā divyā pūrvoktaṃ krāmaṇaṃ pibet  k  vajrabhairavī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte sūtarāje hemavajrābhrabījakam pṛthakpṛthaksamaṃ jāryaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam  k asya sūtasya sadṛśaṃ hemavajrābhrabījakam mardayed amlavargeṇa taptakhalve dinatrayam  k piṣṭirbhavet punastāṃ ca samādāya tataḥ priye dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharapācanam  k yāvat kaṭhinatāmeti tāvatkāryaṃ muhurmuhuḥ ghuṭikā jāyate divyā nāmneyaṃ vajrabhairavī  k mukhasthitā siddhakarī krāmaṇaṃ pūrvavatpriye  tripurabhairavī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte rase kāntavajrahāṭakabījakam  k jāryaṃ pṛthaksūtasamaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam jīrṇasūtasamaṃ kāntavajrakāñcanabījakam  k taptakhalvemlavargeṇa mardayeddivasatrayam jāyate pāradaḥ piṣṭiḥ pūrvavattāṃ samāharet  k dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ bhūdharapācanam yāvat kaṭhinatām eti tāvatkāryaṃ muhurmuhuḥ  k ghuṭikā jāyate divyā nāmnā tripurabhairavī mukhasthā siddhidā hyeṣā pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ priye  k  mahābhairavī ghuṭikāmukhīkṛte rase kāntavajrābhrasvarṇabījakam pṛthaksūtasamaṃ jāryaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakādikam  k asya sūtasya jīrṇasya samaṃ vyomādibījakam mardayed amlavargeṇa taptakhalve dinatrayam  k piṣṭir bhavati sūtendrastāṃ piṣṭiṃ punarāharet dolāpākaṃ siddhacūrṇalepaṃ saṃpuṭabhūdhare  k yāvat kaṭhinatāmeti tāvatkāryaṃ muhurmuhuḥ nāmnā mahābhairavīyaṃ ghuṭikā sarvasiddhidā  k dhārayenmukhamadhye tat pūrvavat krāmaṇaṃ pibet krāmaṇānitriphalā musalī muṇḍī bhṛṅgarājaśca vākucī  k nīlī kanyā kākamācī hayagandhā śatāvarī uttarā śivāmbu ca  k bilvamajjā ca tailaṃ ca tailaṃ jyotiṣmatībhavam etāni krāmaṇārhāṇi cauṣadhāni bhavanti hi  k ete cāṣṭārdhagaditāḥ krāmaṇārthe prayogataḥ rasabhasmaprayoge ca ghuṭikānāṃ rasāyane  k pañcadaśaghuṭikāphalampriye pañcadaśānāṃ ca ghuṭikānāṃ phalaṃ śṛṇu abhrabījena racitaghuṭikā rasasaṃyutā  k mukhasthitā dvādaśābdaṃ sarvarogavināśanī sa jīvedvatsaraśataṃ pumāṃśca parameśvari  k kāntabījena racitā ghuṭikā rasasaṃyutā āsyasthā sarvarogaghnī dvādaśābdaṃ varānane  k dhātudārḍhyaprajananī sahasrāyuṣyadāyinī kāntābhrabījaracitā rasayugghuṭikā śubhā  k dvādaśābdaṃ mukhāntasthā jarāmayavināśinī ayutāyuṣyadā divyā mahābalavivardhinī  k hemabījayutā sūtaghuṭikā mukhamadhyagā ā dvādaśābdaṃ dehasya valīpalitarogahā  k āyuṣyapradā puṇyā nāgāyutabalapradā hemābhrabījaghaṭitā ghuṭikā yuktapāradā  k vaktrāsthitārkasaṃkhyābdaṃ daśalakṣābdajīvadā divyabuddhiprajananī divyasatvapradāyinī  k kāntakāñcanabījābhyāṃ sasūtā ghuṭikā kṛtā dvādaśābdaṃ mukhāntā koṭyāyuṣyavivardhinī  k mahātejaḥprajananī bilanidhyādidarśinī kāntābhrahemaghaṭitā ghuṭikā rasasaṃyutā  k mukhasthā dvādaśābdāntād daśakoṭyabdajīvadā hālāhalādisaṃvartakhecaratvapradāyinī  k nirmuktavajrabījena ghuṭikā rasasaṃkhyābdaṃ mukhasthā sarvasiddhidā  k brahmāyuṣyapradā puṃsāṃ jagat sṛṣṭuṃ kramāt prabhuḥ pūjyate brahmavaddevair vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ  k sarasvatyā ca sāvitryā sevyate sarvalokagaḥ aṣṭābhiḥ siddhibhir yukto hyaṇimādibhir īśvari  k vajrakāñcanabījena sasūtā ghuṭikā kṛtā mukhasthā dvādaśābdāntaṃ viṣṇvāyuṣyapradā nṛṇām  k sa ca viṣṇutvamāpnoti viṣṇuvat pālituṃ kṣamaḥ sevyate sanakādyaiśca śriyā yukto mahābalaḥ  k svecchāgatir mahendrādyair nirjaraiḥ sevyate sadā hemābhravajrabījena racitā ghuṭikā priye  k sapāradā mukhāntaḥsthā dvādaśābdaṃ varānane rudrāyuṣpradā nḥṇāṃ rudratvaṃ sā dadāti hi  k saṃhartā rudravallokaṃ viṣṇvindrādyaiśca sevyate aṇimādyaiśca sahitaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvalokagaḥ  k sevyate pramathaśreṣṭhair divyaśaktyā samanvitaḥ yogīndrair dhyāyate dhīro tasyaiva dakṣiṇe dvāre vidyate kuṇḍaleśvaraḥ tannikṛṣṭe jānumātraṃ khanedbhūmiṃ samuddharet  k raktābhāḥ śrīphalākārāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ sparśavedhakāḥ puruṣeśvaradevasya samīpe kuṇḍamasti hi  k guñjāriḍḍhau ca vidyete vṛkṣau tatpattram aśnīyāt saptāhājjāyate siddho jarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ  k hastiśilātatra hastiśilā dakṣe khaneddhastapramāṇataḥ tatra jambūphalākārā grāhyāste sparśasaṃjñakāḥ  k khyātā hastiśironāmnā khyātā hastiśileti sā chāyāchattraekayojanamātre tu tasyā dakṣiṇabhāgataḥ  k śivarūpaṃ śivaproktaṃ chāyāchattraṃ tu vidyate vartulaṃ śatahastaṃ tu chidraṃ tasyāpyadho vrajet  k na kaiściddṛśyate sopi siddho bhavati tatkṣaṇāt yadṛcchayā rudratulyaḥ krīḍatyeva jagattraye  k siddhyaṣṭakaṃ sādhayedvā sarvasiddhipradāyakaḥ kāntābhrasatvakanakasūtāḥ kramaguṇottarāḥ  k amlena mardayedgāḍhaṃ golaṃ kṛtvā tu veṣṭayet tadgolaṃ dīrghavaṃśāgre baddhvā śrīkālikāmanum  k japenniveśayettatra chāyāchattreṇa tena ca vaṃśāgrabaddhagolāntarjāyate ghuṭikā śubhā  k vaktrāntardhārayettāṃ tu tatkṣaṇātkhecaro bhavet śilāṃ tālaṃ vastrabaddhaṃ kṛtvā vaṃśāgraveṣṭitam  k chāyāchattre nivasyaitattābhyāṃ netre samañjayet nidhiṃ paśyati bhūmisthaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  k vaṃśāgrabaddhakhaḍgaṃ ca chāyāchattre vinikṣipet mantrayetkālikāmantraṃ taṃ khaḍgaṃ dhārayet kare  k trailokyavijayī dhīro bhavedvīro jagattraye vaṃśāgre rocanaṃ baddhvā chāyāchattre niveśayet  k lalāṭe tilakaṃ tena kṛtvā lokaṃ vaśaṃ nayet srotoñjanāñjane tadvacchāyācchatre niveśayet  k tenāñjanenāñjitosau devairapi na dṛśyate pāduke pūrvavadbaddhvā chāyācchatre nidhāpayet  k pādābhyāṃ pāduke dhṛtvā yatra yatrābhivāñchati prayātuṃ tatra tatraiva nayatastaṃ ca pāduke  k pūrvavad raktavastraṃ ca chāyācchatre niveśayet āveṣṭayettaṃ ca paṭamadṛśyo bhavati kṣaṇāt  k samujjhite paṭe paścāddṛśyatesau na saṃśayaḥ kāntaṃ vyoma hema sūtamekīkṛtya vimardayet  k golībhūtaṃ tu vastreṇa vaṃśāgre bandhayetsudhīḥ chāyācchatre sthāpayettatkālīmantreṇa mantrayet  k sparśavedhī bhavedetatsatyaṃ satyaṃ varānane śrīśailapaścimadvāre devo brahmeśvaraḥ sthitaḥ  k durgā devī ca tatrasthā sopānaṃ navamaṃ ca yat tuṅgabhadrāyāṃ ca nadyāṃ tato brahmeśvarasya ca  k dvāradeśe mudgavarṇaṃ catvāraḥ sparśakā amī ciñcāvanaṃ ca nairṛtye sthitaṃ brahmeśvarasya hi  k kuṇḍaṃ ca vidyate tatra ciñcādhaścaṇḍikā sthitā ekapādena satataṃ tacciñcāphalam āharet  k vastreṇa bandhayetkuṇḍe kṣiptvā snānaṃ samācaret snānānte tāni gṛhṇīyāttāvanmatsyā bhavanti hi  k tadindhanaiḥ pacettāśca hyasthipucchaśirastyajet dadyāddevāyaikam aṃśam atithīnāṃ dvitīyakam  k tṛtīyāṃśaṃ svayaṃ bhakṣenmūrchito bhavati kṣaṇāt divyo bhavati siddhoyaṃ bilaṃ paśyati bhūtale  k jarāmaraṇanirmukto hyabadhyo nirjarairapi alampurottare grāmo vidyate bhīmapādukaḥ  k pārśve tu tasya grāmasya hastamātraṃ dharāṃ khanet pāṣāṇā hi phaṇākārāḥ sparśasaṃjñā bhavanti te  k yogīśvarīti devyasti tatrālaṃpuradevatā tasyāgrato ramyaguhā tasyā madhye khanedbhuvam  k pāṣāṇā bhedasaṃkāśā grāhyā mārjālaviṣṭhayā saṃmiśrya nikṣipedvaṅge drute tattāratāṃ vrajet  k madhvājyābhyāṃ pibettāṃśca pāṣāṇānsādhakottamaḥ divyo bhavati siddhoyaṃ valīpalitamṛtyujit  k śrīparvatottaradvāre devo nāmnā maheśvaraḥ tiṣṭhati bhramarāmraśca tatra tatphalamāharet  k sphoṭayecca tadantasthā niryānti bhramarāstathā sajīvā atha tānsarvānbhramarāṃstānvivarjayet  k tatphalāni pacetkṣāre yāvacchakyaṃ payaḥ pibet kṣaṇaṃ mūrcchā bhavettena mūrcchānte ca payaḥ pibet  k evaṃ kuryātprayatnena caikaviṃśativāsaram tena vajraśarīraḥ syādvalīpalitavarjitaḥ  k vedavedāṅgatattvajño jīvedādityatārakam tarasā vāyunā tulyastatkṣaṇādbhavati priye  k tadāmrasya phalenaiva tyaktabhramarakena ca vaṅgasya palasāhasraṃ drāvitaṃ rajataṃ bhavet  k randhramāpādayedāmraphale bhṛṅgaṃ vivarjayet tanmadhye nikṣipetsūtaṃ karṣaṃ kṛṣṇābhrasatvakam  k nirudhya vaktraṃ samṛdā gomayena ca lepayet chāyāyāṃ śoṣayetkāṣṭhaistadīyaiḥ praharaṃ pacet  k svabhāvaśītalaṃ kṛtvā vaktrasthāṃ kārayetsudhīḥ khecaratvamavāpnoti valīpalitavarjitaḥ  k jīveccandrārkaparyantaṃ vāgmitvaṃ brahmaṇā samam sūtaṃ kṛṣṇābhrasatvaṃ cāmraphale pūrvavatkṣipet  k pralipya gośakṛnmṛdbhyāṃ puṭedāraṇyakopalaiḥ svaśītaṃ pāradaṃ grāhyaṃ madhusarpirbhir yutaṃ lihet  k guñjāmātraṃ ca māsāntaṃ bālo bhavati mānavaḥ navanāgopamaḥ satve jīved brahmaikavāsaram  k uttare śrīgirīśasya vidyate śuklaparvate pañcopacāraiḥ sampūjya triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ  k oṃ huṃ phaṭkāramantreṇa nirvikalpena sādhakaḥ paśyetpaścimadigbhāgam antarikṣe vimānakam  k divyaṃ hyanekaruciraṃ sadyaḥ pratyayakārakam tataḥ paścimadigbhāge vrajettīrtvā mahānadīm  k dṛśyate ca guhā tatra praviśetpaścimānanaḥ triyojanaṃ vrajettatra vibhīr eko vikalpakaḥ  k kadalīkānanaṃ tatra dṛśyate pañcayojanam acchodapūrṇā sarasī tanmadhye bhadrapīṭhakam  k tatpīṭhaṃ tu mahaddivyaṃ paśyetsphaṭikasannibham uccārayenmantramimaṃ daṇḍavatpraṇatiṃ bhajet  k oṃ hrīṃ vidyāvāgīśvarādhipataye hrīṃ oṃ svāhā tatra snātvā japenmantraṃ lakṣamekaṃ varānane kandamūlāśano vā yatheṣṭaṃ sādhakaḥ priye  k siṃhāsanāntare devaṃ paśyetsphaṭikasannibham caturbhujaṃ triṇetraṃ ca viśadendukalādharam  k nīlagrīvaṃ nāgabhūṣaṃ paraśvathamṛgāyudham varābhayaṃ vareṇyaṃ taṃ viśiṣṭavibudhārcitam  k namaskuryācca sāṣṭāṅgaṃ mantraiḥ stotrair muhurmuhuḥ tataḥ prasannaḥ sa śivo varaṃ datte yathepsitam  k śatamāyatanaṃ tatra kūpaṃ navaśataṃ yathā ārāmāścāpi tāvanti nandanāni vanāni ca  k vāpyo navaśataṃ santi vivaraṃ caiva tatsamam kalpavṛkṣāśca tāvanti ete sarvepi siddhidāḥ  k tatrāste mohalī nāmnā prathitā yakṣiṇīṣṭadā brūte sā dehi me bhuktiṃ siddhiṃ tvaṃ yadi vāñchasi  k devi dāsyāmyahaṃ bhuktiṃ vaktavyamiha cāmunā kandamūlaṃ phalaṃ tasyai pāyasaṃ vā samarpayet  k sā yakṣiṇī punarvakti yāvadbhuñje sutaṃ mama dhārayer vakṣasā tāvadvaraṃ dāsyāmi te mahat  k visṛjestvaṃ yadi tadā bhavantaṃ hanmi nirdayā evaṃ gatabhayaś cīraḥ kuryāccet siddhibhāgbhavet  k vrajedudīcīdigbhāge tatsaro yojanārdhake tatrāste candanaṃ divyaṃ puṣpapūrṇaṃ maheśvari  k tatpuṣpāghrāṇamātreṇa kṣutpipāsā na bādhate bhakṣayedathavā tasya phalamekaṃ yathocitam  k vajrakāyo bhavettasya bhakṣaṇādeva mānavaḥ sarodakṣiṇadigbhāge gacchedyojanapādakam  k nandanaṃ dṛśyate tatra dāḍimīvṛkṣasaṃkulam tatphalaṃ bhakṣayedyastu jīvedyugasahasrakam  k tasyaiva sarasaḥ pūrvabhāge krośārdhamātrakam gaccheddhātrīphalair yuktaṃ vidyate nandanaṃ vanam  k aśnīyāttatphalaṃ dhīro jīvetsaṃvartakatrayam sarasastasya bhāge ca paścime yojanaṃ vrajet  k tatra śrīphalasampūrṇaṃ nandanaṃ vidyate vanam adyate tatphalaṃ yena jīvaty ācandratārakam  k tatraiva nandanavane liṅgaṃ syānnīlavarṇakam tasyodagdvāramārgeṇa viśennāgo mahābalaḥ  k tatra saptaphaṇopetastūgrabhītikaro mahān evaṃvidhaṃ mahānāgaṃ huṃhuṃkāraṃ vadanmuhuḥ  k namaskuryātprayatnena sādhakaḥ siddhikāṅkṣayā vadatyevaṃ mahānāgas tvadṛśyatvaṃ dadāmi te  k yāhi svaṃ paścimadvāraṃ divyā kanyāsti tatra vai samuccaranmahāmantraṃ vrajettatraiva sādhakaḥ  k dadāti hāraṃ sā kanyā praveśaṃ na dadāti ca hāraṃ gale dhārayettaṃ tena sārasvataṃ bhavet  k tasmāddakṣiṇadigdvāre vrajedbhītikaraṃ param tatra paśyenmuktakeśaṃ jihmanetraṃ digambaram  k gadāhastaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrīkṣetrapālakam vandeta mantramuccārya stotrairvighnanivāraṇam  k hāhāhehehuṃhuṃkāraṃ phaṭ huṃ svāhāntameva ca kṣetrapālopyanenaiva mantreṇāśu prasīdati  k svāgatvaṃ vitaratyeṣa praveśaṃ na dadāti hi atha vrajet pūrvadiśo dvāraṃ tatra gaṇādhipam  k sthitaṃ prapūjayettatra praviśetsādhakottamaḥ dṛśyate divyaliṅgaṃ ca cāpastatra manoharaḥ  k oṃ huṅkāreṇa mantreṇa pūjayecca tamīśvaram upavāsena tatraiva divārātraṃ japetsudhīḥ  k pratyakṣo bhavatīśāno dadāti hi varaṃ param ityevamādayaḥ santi siddhayaḥ kadalīvane  k tatraiva sarasaḥ pūrvabhāge yojanamātrake akṣarairlikhitaṃ dvāri tatra padmāvatībilam  k vamanādyairviśuddhātmā praviśettatra sādhakaḥ tatra cāpāntaraśataṃ gacchettatra mṛdaṅgakam  k ālokya vādayettaṃ ca taddhvaniśravaṇāttadā padmāvatī svayaṃ yāti hyamṛtaṃ ca dadāti ca  k tasya pānena siddhoyamamaratvaṃ labheta ca tataḥ sainaṃ samāgamya prārthayettvaṃ mamāntikam  k samāgacchālaye divye kanyāpañcaśatākule sthitvā mama patirbhūyā brahmāyuṣyāvadhi prabho  k tadante śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ gamiṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ tasya pūrvataṭākasya cāgneyyāṃ diśi vidyate  k kadambeśvaradevopi vṛkṣaḥ kādambakogrataḥ tatra patrāṇi cādāya kaṭutailena lepayet  k tadbījasaṃbhavaistailair limped vātha pacetsudhīḥ tatkāṣṭhaistāni matsyāḥ syustāmrapātre vinikṣipet  k varjyamasthi śiraḥ pucchaṃ kṣaudrasarpiryutaṃ bhajet tatsevayā bhavetsiddho rudratulyo mahābalaḥ  k tadvṛkṣaśca nadītīre kuṇḍaleśasya sannidhau vidyate pūrvavadyuktyā siddhirbhavati nānyathā  k astyuttare puṣpagiriḥ kapoteśaśca vidyate triḥ pradakṣiṇamātanyāttasya mūrdhānamāvrajet  k khecaratvaṃ bhavettasya sādhakasya na saṃśayaḥ tasya pūrvottare bhāge chedikīdvārakaṃ sthitam  k udaṅmukhaṃ viśettatra tricāpāntaramādarāt mūṣikākārapāṣāṇaṃ takre piṣṭvā pibennaraḥ  k kṣipraṃ mūrcchā bhavettasya jīvedbrahmadinatrayam vedhayet sarvalohāni sparśamātrānna saṃśayaḥ  k upoṣya ca divā naktaṃ devāgre siddhimāpnuyāt vidyate devatāyugmaṃ kapoteśvaradakṣiṇe  k ā nābhimātraṃ nikhaneddevatādvayamadhyataḥ gorocanopamāstatra pāṣāṇāḥ santi tānharet  k piṣṭvā kṣaudraghṛtābhyāṃ ca pibedyaḥ somaro bhavet kapoteśasya vāyavye nikhaneddhastamātrakam  k tatra pārāvatākārapāṣāṇāḥ sparśasaṃjñakāḥ devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā teṣāmekaṃ samāharet  k aiśānyāṃ śrīgirīśasya hyastyeva bhṛgupātanam tatsamīpe divyakuṇḍaṃ mṛdaṃ tasmātsamāharet  k gavyapañcakayuktāṃ tāṃ dhametkhadiravahninā tasmāllohaṃ patennīlaṃ madhvājyābhyāṃ pratāpitam  k tatsecayetsaptadhaute tadgolaṃ nikṣipenmukhe viṣṇutulyo bhavetsiddhaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvagaḥ sukhī  k bhṛgupātanaśailāgrāt krośe dadhikavāṭakam acchatailagirir nāmnā tadagre vidyate sadā  k bilaṃ tatpaścime hyasti tanmadhye cāpapañcake gate paśyettatra kuṇḍaṃ tatra lākṣāsamaṃ rasam  k alābupātre gṛhṇīyāt sa sūtaḥ koṭivedhakaḥ prākāraścandraguptasya śrīgirīśasya paścime  k tanmadhye vidyate veśma caityaṃ tatpūrvataḥ sthitam caityātpūrve śilā divyā mudgābhā sparśasaṃjñakā  k tatrāste mohano dantī tamāruhya samāhitaḥ pṛṣṭhāttasya tṛṇaṃ grāhyaṃ tatsarvaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhavet  k tadgajasyottare pārśve jānudaghnāṃ khaneddharām jambūphalābhāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ sparśasaṃjñā bhavanti te  k kṣitiṃ khanedgajasyādho jānumātraṃ labhettataḥ lakṣavedhakarā siddhā trikoṇe ghuṭikā parā  k mallināthasya vāyavye natvā devahradaḥ paraḥ tīrthaṃ tatrāsti pāṣāṇā mudgābhāḥ sparśasaṃjñaḥ  k liṅgaṃ kūrmopamaṃ tatra sparśasaṃjñaṃ śubhaṃ priye pūrṇimāyāṃ kṛttikāyāṃ pūjayitvā samāharet  k tasmādgavyūtiyugalātsmṛtā nīlavanī parā tasyā liṅgaṃ ca salilaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ praśasyate  k aśvāmrakākasaṅkāśāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ sparśavedhakāḥ devālayāntarnikhanejjānumātrāntarāddharām  k mūṣikākārapāṣāṇāḥ sparśasaṃjñā bhavanti te śrīgirīśasya nairṛtyāṃ khyātā guṇḍīprabhākhyayā  k tasyāgragarte pītābhāṃ mṛttikāṃ ca puṭe dahet tasyānniḥsarati svarṇaṃ śuddhadevārhakaṃ param  k tatrāste bhṛṅgacūtopi pūrvavat siddhidāyakaḥ tathā tambīpure cāsti tīrthe ca vipule śubham  k sadāphalaṃ tu vikhyātaṃ tasyāḥ pūrvottare sudhīḥ śrīgirer nairṛte bhāge mahānandeti viśrutaḥ  k vrajed ghaṇṭāpathenaiva tasya pūrvottare sudhīḥ tatrāste kālakaṇṭheśo nāmnāgre tasya kuṇḍakam  k tatrendragopasaṅkāśaṃ siddhiḥ sūtasya vidyate bhavanti sapta lohāni svarṇaṃ taptāni sekataḥ  k aiśānye śrīgirīśasya cāsti śrīmālinīśvaraḥ tasyottaradiśi khyātas tūmāparvatasaṃjñakaḥ  k tasyāgre ca triśūlābhāḥ santi darbhāḥ śubhaṅkarāḥ tadadho nikhanennābhimātraṃ nīlāṃ mṛdaṃ haret  k akṣakāṣṭhaiḥ pacettāṃ ca devātithyagnaye kramāt ekaikabhāgaṃ kalpeta caturthāṃśaṃ svayaṃ bhajet  k jīvetkalpāyutaṃ siddho mahābalaparākramaḥ ileśvarasya nikaṭe tatra koṭīśvaraḥ sthitaḥ  k puṣpaṃ patraṃ tadagresti sparśavedhakaraṃ bhavet tatrācaleśvaro devaḥ sparśavedhakaraḥ paraḥ  k tasya yojanamātre ca dakṣiṇe cāmareśvaraḥ tataḥ svarṇaśilā cāsti tadūrdhvaṃ naramāṃsakam  k gomāṃsaṃ vā kṣipetkāṣṭhairbādarairjvālayetsudhīḥ prātaḥ kāñcanasaṅkāśā dṛśyate sā śilā tadā  k pratyagrapuṣpavatyāśca rajasā bhāvitāṃśukam loḍayettacchilāyāṃ ca kṣipedalpāmbupātrake  k tasya saṃsparśamātreṇa lehaḥ syātkāñcanaṃ param śrīgurau yatra tatrāpi piṇḍabhūmisthitopalāḥ  k karṣamātraṃ tu taccūrṇaṃ bhakṣayettriphalā samam valīpalitajinmāsājjīvedācandratārakam  k śrīgirīndrasya nairṛtyāṃ paṭāhakarṇa īśvaraḥ tasya pūrvottare bhāge pañcaviṃśaticāpake  k dvihastamātrordhvaśilā khanettatra dvihastakam śarāvasaṃpuṭākārān dṛṣadas tānsamāharet  k kurvīta tān agnivarṇān siñcyāt kūṣmāṇḍajair dravaiḥ tanmadhyānnavanītaṃ tu dadyāddevāya bhāgakam  k bhāgaikamatitherdeyaṃ bhāgamekaṃ svayaṃ lihet divā naktaṃ bhavenmūrcchā vinidro bhavati svayam  k valīpalitasaṃvarjyo jīvedvarṣāyutaṃ naraḥ sparśakāntasya sopānaṃ dvitīyaṃ bhavati priye  k taddevapārśvayoḥ sarve pāṣāṇāḥ śvetapītakāḥ sparśāḥ sarvā bhavantyete teṣu caikaṃ samāharet  k prācyāṃ hi tasya devasya samīpe kūpamasti ca maṇḍūkābhāśca pāṣāṇāḥ santi ca sparśasaṃjñakāḥ  k tasyeśvarasya codīcyāṃ liṅgādrir vidyate mahān taduttarasyāṃ diśyasti taṭinī pūrvavāhinī  k taṭinyāḥ paścimāśāyāṃ piṅgābhaṃ liṅgamasti hi pūrṇaśailodakaṃ kuṇḍaṃ tatra syātkṣaṇavedhakam  k dviyojane maheśasya dakṣiṇe caṇḍikā sthitā piṇḍikākhyā suvikhyātā tasyā vāyavyakoṇataḥ  k andhurasti hi tanmadhye mudgavarṇāstathopalāḥ kecitpathyānibhāḥ santi te sarve sparśasaṃjñakāḥ  k atratyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sparśānāṃ vidhirucyate yadi sthūlaṃ peṣayettaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ mūṣāntareṇa hi  k kuryātsarvāṇi lohāni tasyāmāvartayet priye tatsarvaṃ jāyate svarṇaṃ kuryādevaṃ yatheṣṭakam  k sūkṣmaścetsarvalohānāṃ drutānāmantare kṣipet tatsparśāt sarvalohāni kāñcanatvaṃ prayānti hi  k vāyavyāṃ mallināthasya tīrthe sarveśvarākhyakam tasya dakṣiṇadigbhāge rājamārge dviyojane  k gate ḍoṃgalikā tatra dṛśyate tasya mūrdhani kṛṣṇadhātrīphalānyeva santi tāni ca bhakṣayet  k saptavāsaraparyantam ā samam cūrṇitaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ karṣaṃ prātarlihecchuciḥ  k saṃvatsaraprayogeṇa triśatāyurbhavennaraḥ  jyotiṣmatīkalpaḥatha jyotiṣmatīkalpaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu pārvati  k divyā jyotiṣmatī vallī taptakāñcanasannibhā bahupratānā svarṇābhā phalabījā śubhapradā  k āṣāḍhe śuklapakṣe ca śubharkṣe śubhavāsare kuṅkumāktena sūtreṇa tāṃ vallīṃ pariveṣṭayet  k raktagandhākṣataiḥ puṣpairarcayitvā praṇamya ca raktamālyāmbaradharaḥ kuṅkumāgarucarcitaḥ  k tāṃbūlacarvaṇaṃ kurvanhṛṣṭo niyatamānasaḥ abhīṣṭadevatāmantraistārāmantreṇa vārcayet  k abhīṣṭadevatāṃ dhyātvā tataścodaṅmukhaḥ priye pakvabījāni gṛhṇīyādātape śoṣayettataḥ  k tvagvarjyāni nidhāyādau cūrṇitāni viśeṣataḥ tebhyastailaṃ samāhṛtya tattailasadṛśaṃ payaḥ  k pādāṃśaṃ madhu saṃyojya tailaśeṣaṃ pacecchanaiḥ tasminkarpūratakkolatvagjātīphalameva ca  k etāni samabhāgāni cūrṇayitvā ca kovidaḥ tattailaṃ ṣoḍaśapalaṃ taccūrṇaṃ palamātrakam  k ekīkṛtyāvaloḍyātha snehabhāṇḍe vinikṣipet triḥ saptavāsaraṃ dhānyarāśau bhāṇḍe vinikṣipet  k daśāhamathavā triṃśatṣaṣṭirvā navatistathā adhikaṃ vā yathāyogaṃ paścāttailaṃ samāharet  k śuddhakoṣṭhaḥ śubhadine kṛtadevadvijārcanaḥ sūryodaye pibeddhīro binduvṛddhyā kramātpriye  k palāntaṃ sādhakastena niḥsaṃjñatvam avāpyate mandaṃ mandaṃ labdhasaṃjño muhuḥ krandati nandati  k rodityeva muhuḥ kṛcchrāllabdhasaṃjño bhavennaraḥ gokṣīraṃ pāyayetpaścātsakṣaudraṃ śrāntacetase  k kramādevaṃ bhavetsvasthaḥ sādhakosau na saṃśayaḥ ṣaṣṭikānnaṃ sagokṣīraṃ taile jīrṇe ca bhojanam  k evaṃ kuryātpratidinaṃ māsamekaṃ nirantaram māsātsūryasamaḥ sākṣāttejasā mantraśāstravit  k sāṅgopāṅgaśrutiṃ vetti tvanadhītopi mānavaḥ madhyāhne bhāskaraṃ paśyetpūrṇacandramivāparam  k vainateyasamā dṛṣṭirdivā paśyati tārakāḥ annavajjīryate kṣvelaṃ suptopyākarṇayeddhvanim  k aṣṭādaśavidhaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ sarvarogānvināśayet phalaṃ dvitīyamāsasya śṛṇu vakṣyāmi bhairavi  k gandharvoragarakṣobhiḥ sevyate tailasevakaḥ mahāpātakakartāro devatāpitṛnindakāḥ  k samayācārarahitās ta ete muktakilbiṣāḥ amuṣya sevayā muktāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim  k phalaṃ tṛtīyamāsasya śṛṇu pārvati vakṣyate devāśca divyā ṛṣayo vasavoṣṭau mahoragāḥ  k amuṣya sevāṃ kurvanti priyaṃ nityahitaṃ tathā tasya mūtraṃ tāmraghaṭe pūrayitvā khanedbhuvam  k tadgarte vihitaṃ kṛtvā ṣaṇmāsātkanakaṃ bhavet caturthamāsasya phalaṃ śarvāṇi śṛṇu sāṃpratam  k adṛśyosau bhavenmartyaḥ sarvaiśvaryayuto balī daśabrahmadinaṃ jīvetsarvalokagatau paṭuḥ  k tanmūtramalagharmāmbūdvartanais tāmralepanam kuryādvahnau pratapanaṃ tacchulbaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhavet  k atha pañcamamāse tu sadehaḥ khecaro bhavet sākṣādbrahmā bhaved devi śṛṇu ṣāṇmāsikaṃ phalam  k mahāsiddhaiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvalokān yadṛcchayā vicarecchivatulyaḥ syānmahātejā mahāyaśāḥ  k atha saptamamāsasya phalaṃ kalyāṇi vakṣyate jitāriṣaḍvargamanāḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  k viṣṇvāyuṣyamavāpnoti puṇyāpuṇyavivarjitaḥ vicarecca mahāvīryaḥ śrīmān viṣṇurivāparaḥ  k aṣṭamāsaphalaṃ vacmi śṛṇu tvaṃ sarvamaṅgale matpriyo divyakarmā ca sarvajño muktimāpnuyāt  k phalaṃ navamamāsasya śṛṇu kātyāyani priye dvitīyacintāmaṇivad vīrosau kāmarūpavān  k brahmaviṣṇvindracandrāṇāṃ rūpaṃ sṛjati sādhakaḥ manasā cintitaṃ yadyattattatkartuṃ svayaṃ prabhuḥ  k etadrasāyanaṃ divyaṃ sukaraṃ mokṣasādhanam puṇyaṃ paramaguhyaṃ ca gopanīyaṃ tvayā priye  k etasya sadṛśaṃ nāsti devānāmapi durlabham bahunātra kimuktena tvatpriyārthaṃ mayoditam  k rasāyanam idaṃ divyaṃ na kurvanti ca mānavāḥ ajñānopahatāḥ kecit kecin nāstīti śaṅkayā  k antarāyeṇa kecic ca tadalābhena kecana tatkalpājñānataḥ kecitkecid guruvivarjitāḥ  k kecid rogākulā devi tvitthaṃ tairapi vighnitāḥ yatra jyotiṣmatī vallī sā bhūmiḥ puṇyabhūmikā  k tatraiva sarvatīrthāni siddhayo vividhā api jyotiṣmatīphalabhavaṃ sevyaṃ divyarasāyanam  k  guggulukalpaḥatha guggulukalpaṃ ca śṛṇu tvaṃ caṇḍikedhunā caturvidho gugguluḥ syātkumudaḥ padmakastathā  k mahiṣākṣaṃ ca hemākhyas tattadvarṇasamujjvalaḥ hemākhyaṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ rasāyanam udāhṛtam  k kaṇaśo gugguluṃ kṛtvā goghṛtena śanaiḥ pacet ḍolāyantre yuktiparo ghṛtabharjitamāṃsavat  k pathyāvibhītakau dhātrī gandhakaśca pṛthakpṛthak samāṃśaṃ tānvicūrṇyaiva etatsarvasamaṃ puram  k śuddhakoṣṭho lihetprātastailaṃ hyeraṇḍasaṃbhavam lolayitvā niṣkamātraṃ vṛddhiḥ karṣāvadhirbhavet  k evaṃ varṣaprayogeṇa śītavātavraṇāstathā piḍakāgaṇḍamālādyā vinaśyanti mahārujaḥ  k dvādaśābdaprayogeṇa vajrakāyo bhavennaraḥ yadyaddravyaṃ ca sātmyaṃ syāt tattaddravyeṇa vā bhajet  k yasya yasya ca rogasya yadyadbheṣajamīritam taistaiḥ sahaiva seveta tattadrogaharaṃ bhavet  k  vijayākalpaḥvijayotpattiḥśrībhairavī devadeva jagannātha surāsuranamaskṛta pañcakṛtyapradhāneśa namastubhyaṃ parātpara  k sarvepyauṣadhakalpāśca matprītyā kathitāstvayā āścaryaṃ bhūtadeveśa sadyaḥ siddhipradāyakam  k sukhasevyaṃ sukhakaraṃ jñānadaṃ bhuktidaṃ śucim asmatsāyujyadaṃ brūhi prītyā mama rasāyanam  k tataḥ smitamukho bhūtvā śaṅkaro lokaśaṃkaraḥ śrībhairavaḥ devi vakṣyāmyahaṃ kalpaṃ spṛhaṇīyaṃ surāsuraiḥ  k siddhaiśca munibhiḥ strībhiḥ sarvavarṇaiśca yogibhiḥ bālairvṛddhaiśca rugṇaiśca ṣaṇḍhaiśca bahuyoṣitaiḥ  k śṛṇu tvamamṛtodbhūtaṃ sāvadhānena cetasā āgneyo māmako ṃśaḥ syātsaumyāṃśastāvakaḥ priye  k agnīṣomātmakaṃ sarvamauṣadhaṃ jaladhau surāḥ asurāḥ prākṣipaṃścakrurmathanaṃ mandarādriṇā  k atīva mathanāttatra devyāgneyo mamāṃśakaḥ jvalanmahāviṣaṃ ghoraṃ jātaṃ hālāhalākhyakam  k tena vyākulitā mlānā gatavegāḥ surāsurāḥ kṛpayā tanmayā sarvaṃ viṣaṃ ca kabalīkṛtam  k tato devā ditisutā mamanthurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ tato lakṣmīprabhṛtayaḥ prādurāsaṃstatomṛtam  k tad udbhūtaṃ paraṃ divyaṃ jarāmaraṇakṛntanam tadā tadā mahāviṣṇurmama hastāmbujerpayat  k trivāraṃ bindavo dattāḥ parasmai paramātmane parāśaktiyuje paścāttubhyaṃ datte mayā priye  k pītaṃ tvayā ca me dattaṃ madhusūktamudīrya ca svīkṛtaṃ ca mayā kānte cidānandātmakāmṛtam  k sāndrānandena ca mayā sphūtkṛtir lajjayā kṛtā patitā bindavaḥ sūkṣmāstebhyo jātā mahauṣadhiḥ  k tāmālokya śubhāṃ divyāṃ muditāḥ paryapālayan matkarāṃbujanītena pīyūṣeṇa vivardhitam  k tasmāttriśūlasadṛśaparṇaṃ ca paṭalaṃ bahu tasmānmahauṣadhirjātā madādiṣṭairguṇairvṛtā  k kadācidbhairavo dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭastāṃ prārthayanmayā dattā tasmai bhairavopi yoginībhyaḥ samarpipat  k tāśca prītāḥ svabhaktebhyo bhaktebhyaḥ pradaduśca te ninyuśca bhūtalaṃ divyāmauṣadhiṃ sarvasiddhidām  k vijayābhedāḥśrībhairavī kiṃnāmnī sā kathaṃvīryā sevanīyā kathaṃ prabho kīdṛgvarṇā kiyadbhedā kīdṛgrūpaguṇā ca sā  k kathaṃ vā siddhidā sā syātkramānme brūhi vallabha śrībhairavaḥ atha tasyāścaturvarṇā yugadharmāśritāḥ priye  k śuklavarṇā kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ śoṇitaprabhā dvāpare pītavarṇā ca nīlavarṇā kalau yuge  k ekaparṇā triparṇā ca pañcaparṇā municchadā daśaparṇā rudraparṇā trayodaśadalānvitā  k navaparṇeti vijñeyā bhedā hyete sureśvari vijayālakṣaṇamstrīrūpā saphalā vallī puṃrūpā ca drumākṛtiḥ  k saphalā tu madaṃ mūrchāṃ sukhaṃ satvaṃ karoti ca yogavāhā tiktarasā sā kaṭuś cūgragandhinī  k śivamūlī ca vijayā bhaṅgī gañjā vimardinī divyā siddhā siddhidā ca siddhamūlī manonmanī  k madhudravā cidāhlādā paśupāśavināśinī kālaghnī sarvarogaghnī nāmānyetāni pārvati  k śivo mūlaṃ bhavedyasyāḥ śivamūlīti kathyate trilokān ariṣaḍvargān vijayākhyā jayediti  k tāpatrayādiduḥkhānāṃ bhañjanād bhaṅginī smṛtā gañjeti mādayatyeṣā madirāsthānakāriṇī  k sadṛśaṃ marśanaṃ yasyāḥ saiva proktā vimarśinī krīḍāmodadyutimadakāntidatvācca divyakā  k svataḥsiddheti siddhākhyā diṣṭasiddhipradāyikā siddhideti mahāsiddhaiḥ sā nītā siddhamūlikā  k manaścintitakāryāṇāṃ sādhanācca manonmanā saṃvidānandadatvācca cidāhlādeti kīrtitā  k brahmarandhrasthitasudhādrāvaṇācca madhudravā kṛṣṇā pāṃsulā ca mṛdulā sakarīṣakā  k bhujaṅgamāṃsasahitā tatra bījāni vāpayet ahivaktreṣu satvañci snigdhāni ca gurūṇi ca  k puṣyārke siddhayoge vā śravaṇe śuklapakṣake snāto liptatanurgandhaiḥ kṛtanyāsajapārcanaḥ  k udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā dhyātvā ca gurupādukām sakṣīrāṅkolatailena jalena pariṣecayet  k aṅkure ca samutpanne siñcetsaghṛtavāriṇā parṇe kīṭe samutpanne sāmudraṃ vāri secayet  k kṛṣṇapakṣasya caturdaśyāṃ ca sādhakaḥ snātaḥ śuddhāmbaro gandhapuṣpabhūṣaṇasaṃyutaḥ  k arcayedbhairavaṃ tatra nandīśaṃ ca krameṇa ca madyamāṃsopahāreṇa raktapītasitāsitaiḥ  k tantubhirveṣṭayeddevi saptadinaṃ kāryaṃ pañcamyām amṛteśvarīm dhyātvā kundendukarpūrasaṃkāśāṃ dhavalāṃbarām  k sitamālyānulepārdrāṃ muktābharaṇamaṇḍitām dakṣiṇekṣaguṇaṃ vāme sudhāpūrṇaghaṭaṃ tataḥ  k tadadho dakṣiṇe vāme sugandhikā kramājjñeyā caikaikapalamānataḥ  k yojanīyāścūrṇitāśca tatsarvasadṛśā jayāḥ sitā sarvasamā yojyā tatsamaṃ gopayaḥ kṣipet  k kṣīramadhye sitāṃ kṣiptvā tantupākaṃ bhavedbhiṣak māseṣu dvādaśeṣu ca mantratrayaṃ ca prajapetpratimāseṣu sādhakaḥ  k sādhakonena yogena jarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ bhavatyeva na sandehaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane  k rasatrigandhakṛṣṇābhrarudrākṣasvarṇabhasma ca asamyagbahu vā bhuktaṃ pacecchīghraṃ tu pittajān rogānkuryāttu mandāgniḥ samāne kaphapīḍite  k samyagbhuktaṃ mitaṃ vāpi hitaṃ cānnaṃ cirātpacet vaktraśoṣādhmānatāśca gauravaṃ cāntrakūjanam  k durbhuktam acirād vātajān gadān kuryāttasmādapramattaḥ samāgniṃ rakṣayetpriye  k yāmadvaye pacettīkṣṇaḥ ṣaḍyāmānmandapāvakaḥ kṛcchrādannaṃ samāgnistu caturyāmātpacetsukham  k asamāgniḥ kadācit tu rasāyanaṃ ca sakalamākhyātuṃ ca savistaram ājñāpayāhaṃ yadi te hṛdyā prāṇapriyā vibho  k jīvanmuktiḥ kathaṃ nātha yogarūpaṃ ca kīdṛśam anugṛhṇīṣva deveśa sukhopāyaṃ bhavāpaham  k śrutvā stutiṃ smitamukho bhairavaḥ parayā mudā uvāca devīṃ kalyāṇīṃ parvatādhipanandinīm  k śrībhairavaḥ sādhu sādhu mahāmāye sarvaṃ vetsi sanātane tathāpi pṛcchasīśāni lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  k pravakṣyāmi samāsena sāvadhānaṃ śṛṇu priye tvattonyā vallabhā kā me rahasyārthavibhāṣaṇe  k jīvanmuktalakṣaṇamśṛṇu vakṣyāmi deveśi jīvanmuktasya lakṣaṇam kāmaṃ krodhaṃ bhayaṃ lobhaṃ madaṃ mohaṃ ca matsaram  k mānaṃ lajjāṃ kulaṃ śīlaṃ kutsāṃ dambhaṃ ca vañcanām avidyāṃ jaḍatāṃ garvaṃ śītamuṣṇaṃ tathātapam  k vātaṃ sukhaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ ca pāpaṃ puṇyaṃ hitāhitam tāpatrayaṃ putramitrakalatrādīni yastyajet  k na saktaḥ sarvaviṣaye tattvacintāparāyaṇaḥ padmapatram ivāmbhobhir nirliptahṛdayo bhavet  k maitrīkṛtātaṭopekṣāmadaitair maṇḍitāśayaḥ aihikāmuṣmikasukhaprāptikāryāviraktadhīḥ  k nityānityavivekajño hyantaḥkaraṇanigrahaḥ jarāmaraṇahīnaśca śivasāmarasātmavān  k jīvanmuktaḥ sa vijñeyastīrṇasaṃsārasāgaraḥ devadaityādibhirvandyaḥ sa sevyaḥ sa guruḥ śivaḥ  k yathāhaṃ sarvalokeṣu pūjanīyo maheśvari tathāsau sarvalokeṣu sarvaiḥ sampūjyate sadā  k dehānteṣu tu muktiryā prāṇināṃ sāprayojanā dehānte dehinaḥ sarve muktiṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ  k bhagasaṃdrāvaṇānmuktir bhavecced gardabhādayaḥ pakṣiṇo vṛṣabhā meṣāḥ kiṃ muktāstripurāmbike  k retoviṇmūtrasevāyāṃ yadi muktirbhavetpriye kapiśca sūkarādyāśca kathaṃ muktā bhavanti te  k na kevalāmaratvācca na śivatvādbhavettathā taddvayor melanācca syājjīvanmuktiriyaṃ smṛtā  k sarvasminsamaye śāstre muktirastyantakālajā na dṛśyate karāntasthamaṇivatsā ca śāmbhavi  k atigopyamavācyaṃ yaddevānāmapi durlabham kathayiṣyāmi deveśi dehasthairyaṃ sadātanam  k jīvanmuktisādhakaśarīrasthairyasaṃpādanopāyaḥyogasiddhiḥśivatvaṃ khecaratvaṃ ca sarvasiddhipradaṃ śubham dehaṃ vinā na kiṃcit syāddehoyaṃ sarvasādhanam  k tasmāddehaṃ prayatnena rakṣayetsarvataḥ sadā dehapāte dharmanāśo dharmanāśe kriyācyutiḥ  k kriyācyutau kuto yogo yogabhraṃśe na cidbhavet cidabhāve kuto mokṣo mokṣe bhraṣṭe na kiṃcana  k anyopāyaśatenāpi na deho dhāryate vāyoḥ saṃdhāraṇājjñānaṃ jñānānmokṣaḥ prajāyate  k sarveṣāṃ dehamūlaṃ syāttatsthairye pavanaḥ prabhuḥ parasmādakṣarāttasmādākāśaṃ samabhūttataḥ  k vāyustasmācca dahanastasmādāpastato mahī eteṣāṃ pañcabhūtānāmakṣaraṃ kāraṇaṃ param  k vyoma śabdātmakaṃ vāyuḥ śabdasparśātmako bhavet vahniḥ śabdasparśarūpamayaḥ salilamucyate  k śabdarūpasparśarasātmakaṃ bhūmirviśeṣataḥ śabdarūparasasparśagandharūpā bhavet priye  k bhūvāyvagnyanilākāśādhiṣṭhātryaścaiva devatāḥ brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca maheśvarasadāśivau  k bhūmir naṣṭāmbusaṃmagnā tāśca grastā mahāgninā sa ca caṇḍasamīreṇa śamitaḥ sopi pārvati  k vyomni līnaḥ kramāt tasmād ākāśād udbhavanti te antarbahiḥ sthitaṃ vyāptaṃ nirādhāraṃ nirāśrayam  k ākāśaṃ cetasā dhyāyan pracchindyād bhavabandhanam jagatprāṇamayaṃ vāyuṃ cidānandapradaṃ jalam  k niścalīkurute yuktyā vāyuvatsyātsa khecaraḥ anantārkāgnisaṃdīptaṃ dahantaṃ jagatāṃ trayam  k tejo dhyātvā svahṛdaye nāgninā sa tu bādhyate sudhātaraṅganikaraplāvyamānamahītalam  k aptattvaṃ bhāvayan svānte vāri taṃ na hi bādhate abhūtalacarākrāntaṃ bhūtalaṃ bhūtasaṃplavam  k hṛdaye bhāvayannityaṃ tasya no pārthivaṃ bhayam yadyadbhāvayate citte tattadrūpam avāpnuyāt  k yathāgnitvaṃ vrajet kāṣṭhaḥ kīṭo bhramaratāṃ yathā yogāṅgāniāsanaṃ prāṇaniyamaḥ pratyāhāraśca dhāraṇā  k dhyānaṃ samādhiḥ ṣoḍhā syuryogāṅgāni krameṇa ca
