k saptatidvisahasrāḥ syustāsu mukhyā daśa smṛtāḥ iḍā ca prathamā nāḍī piṅgalā ca dvitīyakā  k suṣumnā ca tṛtīyā syādgāndhārī ca caturthikā pañcamī hastijihvā syātṣaṣṭhī pūṣā tarasvinī  k saptamyalambuṣā nāḍī cāṣṭamī ca kuhūḥ smṛtā navamī śaṅkhinī caiva daśamī ca krameṇa hi  k etāstu prāṇavāhinyo vāyavastu japāḥ smṛtāḥ prāṇāpānau tathā vyānodānau caiva samānakaḥ  k nāgaḥ kūrmaśca mṛtyuthopi vivasvatām  k oḍyāṇabandhaḥoḍḍiyāṇe nābhivivaramūrdhvaṃ jaṭhare dṛḍham ākṛṣya paścimaṃ tānaṃ bandhayetpavanastadā  k viśrāntaḥ syānmahāmāye coḍyāṇo yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ mṛtyudāvānalo dīpto jarārogābdhivāḍabaḥ  k khecarīmudrāāsyāntarvivare jihvāṃ tālurandhre praveśayet viparītāṃ bhruvormadhye paśyenniścalayā dṛśā  k eṣā hi khecarī mudrā gopanīyātidurlabhā jihvā tu khagatā yasmānmanaścarati khe tataḥ  k khecarīti prasiddheyaṃ mṛtyurogajarāpahā nidrā kṣudhā tṛṣā nāsti khecaryā mudritasya ca  k mūrcchā bhavati sādhvī ca karmabandhabhayaṃ na hi ramaṇyā saṃgatasyāpi reto na svayam  k yonimudrānibaddhaḥ sansā mudrā tena durlabhā bījastu dvividhaḥ proktaḥ śukraṃ caiva mahārajaḥ  k śiraḥsthānagataṃ śukraṃ yonisthānagataṃ rajaḥ śukraṃ tu śvetavarṇaṃ syātpravālābhaṃ rajaḥ smṛtam  k śukraṃ candragataṃ nityaṃ rajaḥ sūryeṇa saṅgatam śukraṃ śivo rajaḥ śaktistayā yogaḥ sudurlabhaḥ  k marutā śakticāreṇa rajaścordhvaṃ praṇīyate aikyaṃ tadbindunā yāti tadā divyaṃ vapurbhavet  k mahāmudrāvāmāṅghrimūlabhāgena yonisthānaṃ prapīḍayet dakṣiṇāṅghriṃ ca vitataṃ hastābhyām abhidhārayet  k hanuṃ vakṣasi nikṣipya vāyunā jaṭharaṃ tataḥ āpūrya recayeddevi sthitvā baddhāsano yamī  k kuṭīsthaḥ praṇavaṃ japet trilokaśca trikālaśca tridevāstrīśvarā api  k trijyotīṃṣīndumukhyāni trivedāścāgnayastrayaḥ śaktitrayaṃ tripadavī brāhmī caindrī ca vaiṣṇavī  k varṇatrayaṃ ca bhāsante yatra tajjyotiromiti tam oṃkāraṃ ca manasā vacasā karmaṇā tu yaḥ  k dhyāyejjapedabhyasecca sa mukto bhavabandhanāt gacchaṃs tiṣṭhañjapañjāgracchucir vāpyaśucir yadi  k na karmaṇā ca liptaḥ syājjalenābjadalaṃ yathā vāyau calati sarvepi calantīndriyadhātavaḥ  k sthite vāyau sthire sarvaṃ vapuḥprabhṛti śāmbhavi tasmādvāyuṃ nibadhnīyātsthire vāte sthiraṃ manaḥ  k sthire manasi jīvaśca ṛjvaṅgaḥ sthiramānasaḥ vāmanāsāpuṭenaiva pūrayetprāṇamārutam  k yāvatṣoḍaśamātraṃ ca kumbhayed dvādaśa priye recayeddaśamātraṃ ca dakṣanāsāpuṭena ca  k punaśca sūryamārgeṇa pūrayet pūrvavatpriye kumbhayitvā recayecca vāmanāsāpuṭena ca  k prāṇāyāmavidhiḥ proktastrividho yogivandite adhamo madhyamo devi hyuttamopi yathākramam  k prokto yam adhamas tasmād dviguṇo madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ uttamastriguṇaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmoyamīśvari  k yadā tu vāmanāsāyāṃ pūrayeccandramakṣaram dhyāyedamṛtavārīśamadhyasthaṃ kṣīrasannibham  k yadā tu dakṣanāsāyāṃ pūrayet sūryamakṣaram jvalajjvalanasaṅkāśaṃ nābhisthaṃ cintayetsadā  k evaṃ bījadvayaṃ dhyātvā nāsārandhradvayena ca pūrayedyastu matimānnāḍīśuddhirato bhavet  k evaṃ māsatrayābhyāsādyatheṣṭaṃ vāyudhāraṇam pradīpto jāṭharo vahnirnādavyaktiśca jāyate  k ārogyaṃ prāpnuyāddevi nityamabhyāsayogataḥ prathameyaṃ na dharmaḥ syāddvitīye kampate vapuḥ  k uttiṣṭhati tṛtīye tu baddhapadmāsanasthiteḥ prāṇāyāmādiṣaṭkena pratyāhāro bhavecchive  k taddviṣaṭkena vidhinā dhāraṇā tu praśasyate dhāraṇādvādaśena syāddhyānaṃ taddvādaśātmakaḥ  k samādhiḥ kathyate devi tena dṛśyaṃ parātparam tasminparāpare dhāmni kṣīyate karmasaṃcayaḥ  k janmamṛtyū na bhavato jarārogaśca naśyati yuktiyuktena yogena cirāyuśca sukhī bhavet  k ayuktyābhyāsanāddhikkākarṇarogaśirovyathā śvāsakāsādayo rogā doṣāḥ syurbahavastathā  k viparītakaraṇīmudrāsaumyasthānātsamāyātā dvābhyāṃ caikā tu bhujyate tatastṛtīyo yaḥ kaścitsa syājjanmajarojjhitaḥ  k prajvalajjvalanākāro nābhimadhye sthito raviḥ tālumadhye śaśī bhāti sudhāṃ varṣatyadhomukhaḥ  k tāṃ grasatyūrdhvavadano bhāskaraḥ kiraṇatviṣā etasya viparītaṃ yatkaraṇaṃ viparītakam  k kākacañcuvadāsyaṃ ca kṛtvā vāyuṃ sasūtkṛtam ādāya nāsārandhreṇa punastaṃ śvasanaṃ tyajet  k śītalīkaraṇākhyoyaṃ yogastu jvarapittahṛt amṛtaṃ śītalaṃ tasya pibataśca jarā na hi  k jihvayā tālumūlena prāṇaṃ yaḥ pibati priye tasya ṣaṇmāsataḥ sarve rogā naśyanti yoginaḥ  k rasanāmūrdhvataḥ kṛtvā somaṃ pibati yaḥ priye siddhirmāsārdha āyāti rogāstasya na santi hi  k jihvāgreṇa ca saṃpīḍya rasanāntarbilaṃ mahat dhyātvāmṛtajharīmambām ardhābdena bhavetkaviḥ  k amṛtāplāvitatanor yogino vatsaratrayāt retaścordhvaṃ prayātyeva sidhyanti hyaṇimādayaḥ  k trividhaṃ garalaṃ tasya śarīre ca na saṃkramet jarā ca maraṇaṃ nāsti duṣṭasattvabhayaṃ tathā  k  dhāraṇamuktāsanasamārūḍhaḥ prāṇāyāmarataḥ sadā pratyāhāraprasannaḥ sannabhyaseddhāraṇaṃ tataḥ  k cetaso niścalatvaṃ yaddhāraṇā sā smṛtā śive pṛthvyādipañcabhūtānāṃ yā pṛthagdhāraṇā hṛdi  k caturaśrā suvarṇā salakārā ca hṛdi sthitā brahmaṇā sahitā bhūmirdhyātavyā pañca nāḍikāḥ  k prāṇaṃ tatraiva manasā dhārayetsaha śāṃbhavi eṣā stambhakarī vidyā pṛthvījayamavāpnuyāt  k ardhacandrapratīkāśaṃ karpūrahimanirmalam kaṇṭhasthānagataṃ nityaṃ sudhāplutavakārayuk  k jalatattvaṃ ca saṃyuktaṃ viṣṇunā tatra dhārayet prāṇaṃ cittena sahitaṃ dhyātavyaṃ pañcanāḍikāḥ  k eṣā hi vāruṇī vidyā viṣapittajvarāpahā grasane kālakūṭasya mayaiva parikalpitā  k trikoṇaṃ taptahemābhaṃ sarephaṃ rudradaivatam tālusthānagataṃ dhyāyedvahnitattvaṃ jvalatprabham  k tatraiva pañcaghaṭikāḥ prāṇaṃ ca manasā saha dhārayennihitaṃ yogī hyeṣā vaiśvānarī parā  k viṣāgnibhītisaṃhartrī vātaśleṣmādirogahṛt vartulaṃ nīlameghābhaṃ bhruvormadhye pratiṣṭhitam  k sayakāraṃ vāyutattvaṃ nityamīśvaradaivatam tatraiva nāḍikāḥ pañca prāṇaṃ ca manasā saha  k dhārayedvāyavīyaiṣā vidyā khagatidāyinī mṛgatṛṣṇāmbusaṅkāśaṃ hakāreṇa samanvitam  k sadāśivādidaivaṃ ca brahmarandhragataṃ sadā vyomatattvaṃ nirākāśaṃ śāntaṃ sarvagataṃ priye  k tatra prāṇaṃ ca saṃyamya manasā saha dhārayet yāvatsyuḥ pañca ghaṭikā nabhovidyeyamīśvari  k kathitā mokṣadā devi yogināṃ duḥkhahāriṇī stambhanī pārthivī vidyā plāvanī vāruṇī matā  k tato vaiśvānarī vidyā dāhinīti prakīrtitā vāyavī bhrāmaṇī proktā śamanī vyomarūpiṇī  k kramaśaḥ pañcavidyāśca dhāraṇīyāḥ pṛthakpṛthak svanāmakarmasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ dadati yoginām  k eṣā pañcavidhā devi dhāraṇā bhuvi durlabhā  dhyānamtattveṣu niścalā cintā yā taddhyānaṃ prakīrtyate  k dhyānaṃ dvidheti vikhyātaṃ saguṇaṃ nirguṇaṃ priye saguṇaṃ varṇasahitaṃ nirguṇaṃ varṇavarjitam  k lakṣaṃ ca vājapeyānāmaśvamedhasahasrakam sakṛddhyānasya yogasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  k pratyaṅmanā bahirdṛṣṭir ṛjuḥ padmāsanasthitaḥ dhyānayogaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sadyaḥ siddhipradaḥ śubhaḥ  k mūlādhāre suvarṇābhe cakresminprathame priye dhyātvātmānaṃ ca nāsāgre lakṣayeddhanti kilbiṣam  k svādhiṣṭhāne ca ratnābhe hyātmānaṃ paricintayet nāsāgralakṣo duḥkhebhyo mucyate yogisattamaḥ  k bālāruṇābhe cātmānaṃ cakresminmaṇipūrake smṛtvā nāsāgradṛṣṭiḥ saṃstrijagatkṣobhayedyamī  k vidyunmālānibhe cakrenāhate hṛdayasthale prāṇāyāmena bahudhā sādhite parameśvari  k ātmānaṃ cintayedyastu nāsāgragatalocanaḥ bhavedbrahmasamo yogī vaśīkṛtamanāḥ priye  k ghaṇṭikāyāṃ viśuddhākhye svarṇacampakasannibhe ghrāṇāgradṛṣṭirātmānaṃ dhyātvānandamayo bhavet  k lambikāyāṃ sudhāpūrṇe candramaṇḍalamaṇḍite nāsāgradṛṣṭirātmānaṃ dhyātvānandamayo bhavet  k bhruvormadhyeñjanākāre dhyāyedātmānamīśvari jitaprāṇo bhavedyogī yogānandamayo bhavet  k nirguṇaṃ nirapāyaṃ ca śivaṃ śāntaṃ parātparam viśvataijasam ātmānaṃ dhyāyedbhrūmadhyalocanaḥ  k brahmānandamayo yogī bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ājñācakramiti khyātaṃ pare vyomni nirāmaye  k śivam ātmānamācintya bhavejjñānamayo vaśī gaganākāramamalaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇāmbusannibham  k dhyātvātmānaṃ sarvagataṃ mokṣaṃ vrajati saṃyamī apānameḍhrau nābhiśca hṛdayaṃ ghaṇṭikā tathā  k lambikā ca bhruvormadhyaṃ nabhaśca brahmarandhrakam tava cakramiti khyātaṃ deyaṃ sthānaṃ ca yoginām  k dhāraṇā pañcaghaṭikā ṣaṇṇāḍī dhyānamucyate samādhirdvādaśāhaṃ syātprāṇasaṃyamanātpriye  k  samādhiḥjalasaindhavayoryogādekatvaṃ ca yathā bhavet cittātmanoḥ sāmarasyaṃ samādhiḥ sa tu kathyate  k manaḥ pralīyate cānte yadā prāṇakṣayo bhavet sāmarasyaṃ tadā syācca samādhiḥ sa tu kathyate  k praṇaṣṭākhilasaṅkalpo jīvātmā paramātmanā yadekatvaṃ bhajeddevi samādhiḥ sa tu kathyate  k parāpekṣojjhitaṃ cittamindriyeṣu pravartate yadā jīvo gataścaikyaṃ tadā naivendriyaṃ manaḥ  k śabdaṃ sparśaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca rasaṃ gandhaṃ paraṃ tathā ātmānaṃ ca sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ mānāmānaṃ priyāpriye  k śītāśītaṃ tathā vātamātapaṃ yo na vetti ca na bādhyate svakarmaughairna kaiścidapi bādhyate  k na śastrairbādhyate mantrairyantraistantrairna gṛhyate nāgninā na jalenāpi vāyunā na ca pīḍyate  k avadhyo dehibhiḥ sarvair mānanīyaḥ surairapi āhāre ca vihāre ca nidrāyām avabodhane  k sarvakarmasu sarvagaṃ vibhu saṃtatam etadbrahmapadaṃ tattvaṃ viddhi tvaṃ vindhyavāsini  k anāmaye nirālambe nirātaṅke mahādyutau nirābhāse pare tattve yogayuktaḥ pralīyate  k dugdhe dugdhaṃ ghṛte yogasiddhidakuṭīnirmāṇavidhiḥśrībhairavī kuṭī proktā tvayā pūrvaṃ kathaṃ kāryā ca kīdṛśī tatra kālaṃ kiyacchaṃbho vastavyaṃ brūhi me prabho  k śrībhairavaḥ vakṣyāmi tāṃ kuṭīṃ samyak śṛṇu mūrtidvayorayaṃ mantraḥ kathitaḥ suravandite  k mantrasyāsya ca yadyantraṃ tadyantraṃ tatra saṃlikhet ramāṃ ca bhuvaneśīṃ ca kāmaṃ cintāmaṇiṃ kramāt  k karṇikāyāṃ likhetpūrvaṃ vaṭukāyeti vīpsitam gaṇaśo likhet  k antyākṣare cāntyadale mātṛkāmanulomataḥ lekhe ca pratilomenāṅkuśapāśāvṛtaṃ tataḥ  k bhūmandireṇa subhagaṃ yantraṃ gaṇapateḥ śubham gajāntaṃ śrīpadaṃ divyamāyuṣyārogyavardhanam  k etāni yantrajālāni kuṭyantardevatā likhet kuṭībhittibahirbhāge bhairavaṃ varṇamālikhet  k asitāṅgaṃ ruruṃ caṇḍaṃ krodhamunmattabhairavam kapālinaṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ ca saṃhāraṃ bhairavaṃ kramāt  k dvitīyāvaraṇasyāntar bhittāvekādaśa kramāt rudrāṃstrilocanāṃścandrakalājūṭajaṭān likhet  k tadbāhye nava nāthāṃśca nava siddhāṃśca ṣoḍaśa sanatkumārasanakasanandādīn likhettataḥ  k tṛtīyāvaraṇasyāntar bhittau brāhmyādimātaraḥ catuḥṣaṣṭiśca yoginyo lekhanīyā yathāvidhi  k tadbhittibāhye devendramukhā dikpatayaḥ kramāt grahāśca candrasūryādyā aśvinyādyāśca tārakāḥ  k meṣādyā rāśayo lekhyāḥ sālaṅkārāśca sāyudhāḥ kuṭīdvāravipārśve ca gaṇeśaṃ bhairavaṃ likhet  k dvitīyāvaraṇadvārapārśve dvau śaṅkhapadmakau garutmantaṃ hanūmantaṃ tṛtīyāvaraṇasya ca  k dvārasya pārśvayordevi kṣipettattriphalāṃ tataḥ  k loḍayedamarīyuktaṃ pibetprāgānanaḥ sadā iṣṭadevāngurūnvṛddhān natvārcitagaṇeśvaraḥ  k mitāhāro yuktaceṣṭo vātātapavivarjitaḥ ekamaṇḍalamātreṇa bāhyāntaḥ śucibhāg bhavet  k maṇḍale pañcadaśake karṣāṃśau śṛṅgagandhakau  k śivatoyena sammiśraṃ prapibedekaviṃśatim maṇḍalaṃ ca tadante syātsiddhibhāgdehalohayoḥ  k dvāviṃśanmaṇḍale devi cābhrakaṃ varayā yutam evaṃ bhajedyamī nāgadūṣaṇam  k kṛṣṇadhūrtena cāñcalyaṃ triphalābhirviṣaṃ haret giridoṣaṃ trikaṭukairasahyāgnistu gokṣuraiḥ  k vaṅgādisaptadoṣāṇāṃ nāśārthaṃ saptavāsaram tattaccūrṇaiḥ kalāṃśaiśca kumāryā rasasaṃyutaiḥ  k mardayitvā rasaṃ paścātkṣālayeduṣṇakāṃjikaiḥ pāradaḥ sakalairdoṣairmucyate saptakañcukaiḥ  k vaidyakarmaṇi yojyaścedrasaḥ syātsarvarogahā dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥdevadārumalayajajayāvāyasatuṇḍikā  k kumārīmusalīvandhyākarkoṭīrasasaṃyutam sūtaṃ dinaṃ mardayecca punaḥ pātanayantrake  k pātayedyojayetsūtaṃ śuddhaṃ vaidyasya karmaṇi tṛtīyaḥ prakāraḥdagdhaṃ pāṣāṇacūrṇaṃ ca niśākanyārasai rasam  k mardayeddinamekaṃ ca pūrvayantre ca pātayet evaṃ saṃskārasaṃśuddhaṃ yojayedvaidyakarmaṇi  k caturthaḥ prakāraḥdaradaṃ yāmamātraṃ tu pāribhadradravaiḥ priye athavā jambīrarasairmardayitvā tu pācayet  k yantre pātanake devi doṣakañcukavarjitaḥ pañcamaḥ prakāraḥpunarnavārasaiḥ peṣyaṃ dhānyābhraṃ pāradaṃ samam  k taptakhalve dinaṃ kṛtvā vajramūṣāgataṃ rasam pacedbhūdharayantre ca punaḥ saṃmardayecca vinikṣipet  k varājambīrakanyāgnidravairyāmaṃ vimardayet pātayetpātanāyantre kuryādevaṃ tu saptadhā  k sagandhakaṃ mardanaṃ ca pātanaṃ bhavati priye śuddhaḥ syātpārado devi yojyaḥ pāradakarmaṇi  k saptamaḥ prakāraḥtilatailair māhiṣikair mūtrair madyāmlakena ca gomāṃsair hiṅgulaṃ pācyaṃ lohapātre kramāgninā  k saptāhaṃ lohadaṇḍena cālayettaddravaṃ muhuḥ sārdraṃ mayūrapittena bhāvayedātape dinam  k pātayetpātanāyantre daradaṃ kharavahninā śuddho bhaveccaturyāmātpārado yogavāhakaḥ  k jāraṇārho vaḍabānalaviḍaḥśṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi jāraṇārhaṃ biḍaṃ priye cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā dagdhaśaṅkhaṃ gharme rkakṣīrabhāvitam  k kuryāddinaṃ tato devi dhūmasāraṃ ca bhāvayet dinaṃ jambīrakarasairātape cātitīvrake  k caturyāmamajāmūtraiḥ ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ suvarcalam yathā sāndratvamāpnoti tāvatkvāthyaṃ varānane  k naramūtre ṣoḍaśāṃśe kaṇṭakārīṃ samūlakām yāvad ghanībhavet tāvat kvāthanīyā prayatnataḥ  k tintriṇīkṣārakāsīsasarjakṣārāḥ śilājatu jambīrasya rasaiḥ sarvaṃ caturyāmaṃ pṛthakpṛthak  k jepālaṃ tattvacāhīnaṃ mūlakakṣārasaindhavam guñjāṃ ca ṭaṅkaṇaṃ śigrudravairbhāvyaṃ pṛthakpṛthak  k jambīrāṇāṃ dravairbhāvyaṃ śaṅkhādyaṃ tattrayodaśa sarvaṃ samāṃśaṃ ca dinamekīkṛtya tu gālitam  k rakṣayetsarvadā jñeyo nāmnā ca vaḍabānalaḥ suvarṇādimalohānāṃ ratnānāṃ jāraṇe tathā  k abhrādyuparasānāṃ ca yojanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ pāradabhasmavidhiḥprathamaḥ prakāraḥśuddhasūtaṃ śuddhagandhaṃ mardayedgoghṛtaiḥ samam  k piṇḍībhūtaṃ kumāryāśca dalagarbhe niveśayet samyaksūtreṇa saṃveṣṭya tamayaskāntasaṃpuṭe  k nirudhya taṃ mṛdupuṭe tridhā pācyaṃ punaḥ priye ādāya dṛḍhamūṣāyāmandhayitvā dhametsudhīḥ  k bhasmībhavetsūtarājo yojyo yoge rasāyane dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥchāyāśuṣkāṇi kurvīta śākapakvaphalāni ca  k mardayedarkapayasā tena mūṣodaraṃ lipet agraprasūtagojātajarāyoḥ śiṣitaṃ rajaḥ  k mūṣāmadhye kṣipetpaścātsūtaṃ gandhaśca tadrajaḥ kṣiptvā nirudhya ca dhamedbhasmībhavati pāradaḥ  k tṛtīyaḥ prakāraḥvandhyā kārkoṭakī kākatuṇḍī ca kaṭutumbikā kañcukī nalikā kākamācī vai kālamañjarī  k kākajaṅghāstvimāḥ sarvāḥ piṣṭvā mūṣāntare kṣipet pūrvoktavandhyāmukhyābhir aṣṭābhir mardayed rasam  k tadrasaṃ liptamūṣāyāṃ kṣiptvā ruddhvā ca bhūdhare pacedevaṃ cāṣṭavāramevaṃ mūṣāpralepanam  k mardanaṃ dhamanaṃ kuryād bhūyo bhūyaḥ sureśvari mṛto bhavati sūtendro yogyo roge rasāyane  k caturthaḥ prakāraḥniyāmakauṣadhairmardyaṃ caturyāmaṃ rasaṃ dṛḍham dviguṇe gandhataile ca śanairmandāgninā pacet  k yāvat khoṭatvamāpnoti tāvadevaṃ pacedrasam tatkhoṭaṃ saṃpuṭe lauhe kṣiptvā rundhyāddṛḍhaṃ sudhīḥ  k pathyājalairlohakiṭṭaṃ piṣṭvā sampuṭamālikhet tasyordhvaṃ śrāvake kācaṃ kṛtvā nāgaṃ vinikṣipet  k sa nāgo dravate yāvattāvadevaṃ dhametpriye yāvanna yāti kāṭhinyaṃ tāvannaiva dhametsudhīḥ  k punaḥ kaṭhinatāṃ prāpte dhametpūrvoktavanmuhuḥ triyāmadhamanādevaṃ bhasmībhavati pāradaḥ  k bhasmīkṛte mūlikābhirjāraṇārahito rasaḥ dehe lohe na yojyaḥ syādyojyo bheṣajakarmaṇi  k pañcamaḥ prakāraḥdviguṇe gandhataile ca śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ vimardayet ekāhaṃ taṃ punarmardyaṃ sarpākṣībhṛṅgarāḍapi  k viṣṇukrāntā tryahaṃ caiṣāṃ rasaiḥ ślakṣṇaṃ vimardayet pacedyantre trisaṃghaṭṭe hyaṣṭavāramiti priye  k kuryādbhasmati sūtendro rogasaṃghātanāśanaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ prakāraḥśvetāṅkolasya mūlottharasairmardyastryahaṃ rasaḥ  k mūṣāyāṃ nikṣiped ruddhvā pacedbhūdharayantrake pārado bhasmatāṃ yāti sarvarogaharaḥ paraḥ  k saptamaḥ prakāraḥviṣṇukrāntāṃ vedikāṃ ca kāñjikena vimardayet tatkalkena raso mardyaḥ saptadhā mūrchitotthitaḥ  k taṃ rasaṃ śrāvake kṣiptvā siñcayettadrasairmuhuḥ dīpāgninā dinaṃ pacyādbhasma syāllavaṇākṛtiḥ  k aṣṭamaḥ prakāraḥkākoduṃbarikākṣīrair bhāvayet somarāmaṭham punaḥ punaḥ saptadhaivaṃ śoṣayenmardayet sudhīḥ  k kākodumbarapañcāṅgaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśe jale kṣipet yathaikāṃśovaśiṣṭaḥ syāttena taddhiṅgu mardayet  k tadgolake rasaṃ kṣiptvā mūṣāyāṃ taṃ ca rodhayet bhūdhare ca puṭedevamaṣṭavāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ  k puṭe puṭe ca taddhiṅgu dadyātsūto mṛto bhavet navamaḥ prakāraḥurubūkasya bījāni tathāpāmārgajāni ca  k pūrṇayet tacca mūṣāyāṃ kṣiptvā sūtaṃ tataḥ kṣipet tadūrdhvaṃ pūrvacūrṇaṃ ca samyaṅmūṣāṃ nirodhayet  k pacellaghupuṭairevaṃ caturbhirbhasmatāṃ vrajet daśamaḥ prakāraḥkuḍuhuñcyāḥ kandamadhye kāntāstanyapariplute  k rasaṃ kṣiptvā mukhaṃ ruddhvā tanmajjakalkataḥ sudhīḥ taṃ gomayaiḥ samālipya svedayedgomayāgninā  k evaṃ kṛte saptavāraṃ raso bhasmatvam āpnuyāt ekādaśaḥ prakāraḥaṅkolasya śiphānīraiḥ sūtaṃ gandhaṃ samaṃ samam  k dinamekaṃ mardayecca mūṣāgarbhaṃ nirodhayet puṭedbhūdharayantre ca dinānte bhasma jāyate  k dvādaśaḥ prakāraḥsūtaṃ dhānyābhrakaṃ tulyaṃ mārakauṣadhijai rasaiḥ mardayed dinamekaṃ tu tatkalkairvastralepanam  k tadvastraṃ vartikāṃ kṛtvā dhṛtvā daṃśena dīpayet taddrutiṃ patitāṃ kāṃsye kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ ca tadbhavet  k tatpunarmārakairmardyaṃ pātanāyantrake pacet mṛto bhaveddinaikena tadbhasmākhilarogahṛt  k trayodaśaḥ prakāraḥkāladhuttūratailena mardanīyaśca pāradaḥ tato niyāmakairmardyāddinaikaṃ kūrmayantrake  k pācayedbhasmatāṃ yāti śubhraḥ syātsarvarogahā caturdaśaḥ prakāraḥśuddhasūtād ardhabhāgaṃ śuddhaṃ gandhaṃ vimardayet  k mārakauṣadhajair drāvair dinaṃ mūṣāgataṃ pacet yantre bhūdharasaṃjñe ca dinenaikena bhasmati  k pañcadaśaḥ prakāraḥsūtamabhraṃ vaṭakṣīraistriyāmaṃ mardayetpriye divyauṣadhidravairmardyaṃ dinaṃ mūṣādhṛtaṃ rasam  k divānaktaṃ karīṣāgnau pacedvā tuṣavahninā svedayettaṃ samuddhṛtya bhūyo divyauṣadhodbhavaiḥ  k bījaiḥ samāṃśaiḥ saṃmardyaṃ caturyāmaṃ sureśvari vajramūṣāgataṃ dhāmyaṃ bhasmībhavati pāradaḥ  k tadbhasma divyaṃ yuñjīta sadā roge rasāyane saptadaśaḥ prakāraḥsvajīrṇe pārade svarṇaṃ samamamlena mardayet  k piṣṭībhūtaṃ kāñjikena prakṣālyādāya tāṃ punaḥ piṣṭyardhaṃ śuddhagandhaṃ ca tadardhaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kṣipet  k sarvatulyāṃ niśāṃ nārīpuṣparaktadravairdinam mardayettāṃ dinānte ca kuryāttadgolakaṃ tataḥ  k paced gaḍḍukayantre ca dinaṃ mandāgninā sudhīḥ samādāya vicūrṇyaiva dattvā tatsamagandhakam  k garbhayantre tryahaṃ pācyaṃ laghunā tattuṣāgninā raso bhasma bhaveddevi nirutthaḥ syādrasāyanam  k aṣṭādaśaḥ prakāraḥkarṣatrayaṃ śuddhasūtaṃ karṣaṃ tāmrarajaḥ priye amlaiḥ saṃmardayedgāḍhaṃ dinaṃ khalve tato bhavet  k piṣṭistāṃ kṣālayettoyaistata ādāya nirmalam mākṣīkasatvaṃ tatsarvaṃ cakramardacchadadravaiḥ  k tridinaṃ mardayedgāḍhaṃ tāṃ piṣṭiṃ garbhayantrake tuṣāgninā paceddevi tridinaṃ vā divāniśam  k karīṣāgnau bhavetsūtabhasma rogajarāpaham ekonaviṃśaḥ prakāraḥsūtaṃ svarṇaṃ vyomasatvaṃ samaṃ svarṇasamaṃ biḍam  k rambhādaṇḍadravaiḥ sarvaṃ tat khalve mardayeddinam tato divyauṣadhodbhūtairbījaistulyaṃ dinadvayam  k saha saṃmardayed rambhātoyais tad garbhayantrake pūrvakrameṇa vipacedrasabhasma bhavecchubham  k jarāmaraṇarogaghnaṃ śoṣayedvālukāyantre dinaṃ mandāgninā pacet rasabhasma bhaveddivyaṃ rugjarāmaraṇāpaham  k ekaviṃśaḥ prakāraḥkarṣadvayaṃ rasendraṃ ca tadardhaṃ śuddhagandhakam mākṣīkasatvaṃ gandhāṃśaṃ tatsarvaṃ mardayeddinam  k nirguṇḍīpatrasāraiśca taṃ golaṃ nikṣipetpriye mūṣāmadhye tato mūṣāvaktraṃ ruddhvā vinikṣipet  k tāṃ mūṣāṃ gaḍḍukāyantre pacenmandāgninā dinam rasabhasma bhaveddivyaṃ sindūrāruṇasannibham  k jarāmaraṇarogaghnaṃ sarvasiddhipradaṃ śubham dvāviṃśaḥ prakāraḥpakvamūṣodare tulyagandhakāntaritaṃ rasam  k tayoścaturguṇaṃ dattvā kākamācīrasaṃ punaḥ ācchādya gaḍḍukāyantre tāṃ nidhāya pacetkramāt  k mṛdumadhyamacaṇḍākhyavahnau yāmacatuṣṭayam tataśca sarvarogaghnaṃ rasabhasma bhavecchubham  k trayoviṃśaḥ prakāraḥsnuhīkṣīrairdinaṃ sūtaṃ mardayet tadabhāvataḥ amlavallyā rasair eva taṃ rasaṃ gandhakaiḥ samam  k garbhayantre vinikṣipya pūrvavad vipacedbudhaḥ mṛto bhavedrasaḥ soyaṃ sarvarogaharo bhavet  k caturviṃśaḥ prakāraḥguñjāphalaṃ rasasamaṃ madhuṭaṅkaṇayāvakaiḥ bhṛṅgapatrarasairyuktaṃ dinam ekaṃ vimardayet  k chāditaṃ vajramūṣāyāṃ dhamayenmṛduvahninā ayaṃ rasāyano vṛṣyo rasaḥ syācchaśisannibhaḥ  k pañcaviṃśaḥ prakāraḥsamaṃ gandharasaṃ śuddhaṃ kīṭamāriṇikādravaiḥ ajamāryahimāryorvā śvetāṅkolarasena vā  k mardayettridinaṃ kṣiptvā mṛṇmaye saṃpuṭe tataḥ dinamekaṃ karīṣāgnau tuṣāgnau vā dinatrayam  k pacettataḥ sūtabhasma jāyate rugjarāpaham śubhaḥ saptaviṃśaḥ prakāraḥvāsitaṃ pāradaṃ karṣamaṣṭaguñjaṃ suvarṇakam  k mṛtavajraṃ caturguñjaṃ mardyaṃ haṃsapadīrasaiḥ taptakhalve vajramūṣāgataṃ kṛtvā nirodhayet  k paced bhūdharayantre ca punarādāya taṃ rasam haṃsapādīdravairmardyaṃ taptakhalve dinatrayam  k pūrvavad bhūdhare yantre pacettaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ evaṃ śatapuṭaṃ kṛtvā bhasma syādraktavarṇakam  k jarāmaraṇadāridryanāśanaṃ bhavanāśanam aṣṭāviṃśaḥ prakāraḥyugāṃśaḥ śuddhasūtaḥ syādekāṃśaṃ tāmracūrṇakam  k amle dinaṃ mardayettaṃ prakṣālyādāya piṣṭikām tāpyasatvaṃ piṣṭisamaṃ cakramardadaladravaiḥ  k mardayet tridinaṃ sarvaṃ golakaṃ garbhayantrake nikṣipya tridinaṃ pācyaṃ tuṣāgnau vā sureśvari  k divārātraṃ karīṣāgnau pacedbhasma bhavedrasaḥ ekonatriṃśaḥ prakāraḥmukhīkṛtarasaṃ cābhrasatvaṃ svarṇaṃ trayaṃ samam  k raṃbhādraveṇa saṃmardyaṃ dinaṃ sarvasamaṃ biḍam tato divyauṣadhīnāṃ ca bījairmardyaṃ dinatrayam  k garbhayantre pacetpaścātkarīṣāgnau mṛto bhavet triṃśaḥ prakāraḥkhajīrṇasūtaṃ vimalāṃ samaṃ nirguṇḍikārasaiḥ  k mardayitvā tryahaṃ kācakūpikāyāṃ vinikṣipet sikatāyantrake pacyāccaturyāmena bhasmitaḥ  k ekatriṃśaḥ prakāraḥtāpyasatvaṃ samaṃ gandhaṃ dvābhyāṃ tulyaṃ ca jāritam sūtaṃ nirguṇḍikāṃ mardya dinaṃ tadgolakaṃ punaḥ  k vajramūṣāndhitaṃ kṛtvā dhamedvā gaḍḍuyantrake pacettadraktavarṇaṃ syātsa rasaḥ sarvarogahā  k rasabhasmalakṣaṇamakṣayitvaṃ nirutthatvaṃ nirlepatvaṃ subhasmatā mārakatvaṃ ca lohānāṃ lakṣayed rasabhasmataḥ  k  gandhapiṣṭīprathamaḥ prakāraḥsaṃcūrṇya śodhitaṃ gandhaṃ pūrvapatrarasena ca saptadhā bhāvayed gharme strīṇāṃ ca rajasā tathā  k tathā mānavapittena lolayedgandhakaṃ punaḥ palamekaṃ śuddharasaṃ karpare cātape nyaset  k tadūrdhvaṃ lolitaṃ gandhaṃ vinyasyāṅguṣṭhamarditam kuryātsūto bhavetpiṣṭiḥ sarvakarmasu siddhidaḥ  k dvitīyaḥ prakārasvarṇagandhapiṣṭīgandhakaṃ śodhitaṃ devi tilaparṇīrasena ca saptadhā mardayecchoṣyaṃ chāyāyāṃ bhāvayet kramāt  k mūṣāyāṃ pāradaṃ śuddhaṃ palamātraṃ vinikṣipet suvarṇaniṣkagulikāṃ mūṣāyāṃ nikṣipettataḥ  k tatra nārīrajomūtramalamātraṃ vinikṣipet vālukāyantramadhye ca tāṃ mūṣāṃ sthāpayecchive  k alpamalpaṃ pūrvagandhaṃ vāraṃ vāraṃ vinikṣipet mṛdvagninā pacedyāvatkarṣagandhaṃ ca jīryate  k avatārya svāṅgaśītamāharetsvarṇagolakam svarṇapiṣṭirbhaveddivyā sarvavāñchitadāyinī  k tṛtīyaḥ prakāraḥbhāvayenmarkaṭītoyaiḥ śatadhā śuddhagandhakam chāyāyāṃ śuddhasūtaṃ ca gharme mṛtkarpare kṣipet  k kiṃcit kiṃcit pūrvagandhaṃ nikṣipenmarkaṭīrasam jīrṇe gandhe dravaṃ deyaṃ muhur gandhaṃ muhurdravam  k yāvatpādāṃśakaṃ jīrṇaṃ gandhaṃ ca piṣṭikā bhavet divyā sā sarvakarmārhā devānāmapi durlabhā  k caturthaḥ prakāraḥśuddhagandhaṃ cūrṇayitvā trivāraṃ kāñjikena ca jambīrāmlaistrivāraṃ ca haṃsapādīrasena ca  k saptadhā kṣālayedevaṃ karpūraṃ bhāvayetpṛthak śvetādrikarṇikātoyair ātape ca trivārakam  k dviguñjamātraṃ karpūraṃ yantrāntaḥ parilepayet tatra gandhaṃ sārdhaniṣkaṃ bhāvitaṃ cūrṇitaṃ kṣipet  k tadūrdhvaṃ ca palaṃ sūtaṃ nikṣipettasya pṛṣṭhataḥ pūrvamātraṃ ca karpūraṃ tadūrdhvaṃ sārdhaniṣkakam  k gandhakaṃ ca punaḥ kṣiptvā tato gomūtrakena ca śvetādrikarṇikāmūlaṃ piṣṭvā tatkalkakena ca  k ācchādya taccharāveṇa rodhayetpācayetkramāt jālikāyantramadhye ca divyaṃ paścāttamuddharet  k evaṃ kuryāttrivāraṃ ca gandhapiṣṭir bhaved dhruvam pañcamaḥ prakāraḥsnehalipte khalvamadhye śuddhasūtaṃ palaṃ nyaset  k karṣaṃ ca śodhitaṃ gandhaṃ devadālīdravaṃ kṣipet karāṅgulyā khare gharme mardayet piṣṭikā bhavet  k ṣaṣṭhaḥ prakāraḥtāmrakhalve palaṃ sūtaṃ karṣārdhaṃ gandhakaṃ kṣipet mṛdvagninā pacedyāmaṃ karāṅguṣṭhena cālayet  k gandhapiṣṭirbhaveddivyā sarvakarmakarī śubhā piṣṭīstambhanam piṣṭīnāṃ stambhanaṃ vakṣye tiktakośātakībhavam  k bījaṃ caṇḍālinīkandaṃ tulyaṃ kāntāstanodbhavaiḥ kṣīraiḥ piṣṭvā ca tāṃ piṣṭīṃ lepayedaṅgulaṃ dṛḍham  k vandhyākandethavā kṣīrakande vā sūraṇodbhave kande vā vajrakande vā kande vā kuḍuhuñcije  k tāṃ piṣṭiṃ nikṣipettattanmajjayā rodhayenmukham tatkandaṃ ca mṛdā liptvā puṭedbhūdharayantrake  k divānaktaṃ karīṣāgnāvūrdhvādhaḥ parivartanam yathā kandaṃ tu na dahettathā pākakramaḥ smṛtaḥ  k atha piṣṭiṃ samānīyād bhavetsā stambhitā priye piṣṭījāraṇam piṣṭīnāṃ stambhitānāṃ ca jāraṇā vakṣyate śive  k stanayantre lohakṛte gandhakaṃ piṣṭitulyakam kṣipedūrdhvaṃ ca deveśi stambhitāṃ gandhapiṣṭikām  k tadūrdhvaṃ piṣṭitulyaṃ ca gandhakaṃ cūrṇitaṃ kṣipet nirudhya bhūdhare yantre pācayejjārayetkramāt  k gandhaṃ punaḥpunardeyamevaṃ śataguṇaṃ priye jīrṇe śataguṇe gandhe yantrātpiṣṭiṃ samāharet  k sarvāsāṃ gandhapiṣṭīnāṃ jāraṇaṃ syācca rañjanam piṣṭīmāraṇam jāritānāṃ ca piṣṭīnāṃ pravakṣye māraṇakramam  k taptakhalve vinikṣipya jāritāṃ gandhapiṣṭikām divyauṣadhirasaiḥ piṣṭvā dinaṃ kuryācca golakam  k divyauṣadhīnāṃ bījāni piṣṭvā divyauṣadhodbhavaiḥ svarasair vajramūṣāntar lepayetpūrvagolakam  k kṣiptvā nirudhya mūṣāsyaṃ pacedbhūdharayantrake pravartayaṃścordhvamadho dinamekaṃ punaḥ priye  k samāhṛtya yathāpūrvaṃ pūrvatoyaiśca mardayet puṭayetpūrvavaddevi daśavāramiti kramāt  k asaṃśayaṃ gandhapiṣṭirmriyate sarvakāryakṛt gandhapiṣṭikramāj jātarasabhasmāni bhairavi  k sarvakarmasu mukhyāni viśeṣādvādakarmaṇi rasabandhāḥprathamaḥ prakāraḥvaikrāntabandhaḥvakṣyāmi rasabandhāni śṛṇu bhairavi samprati  k śodhitaṃ pāradaṃ khalve daśaniṣkaṃ vinikṣipet niṣkaikaṃ śuddhagandhaṃ ca svalpaṃ svalpaṃ vinikṣipet  k kuṭṭayenmardayed grāvṇā piṣṭiḥ syādyāmamātrake kṣīrakandethavā vandhyākande vā kuḍuhuñcije  k kande vā nikṣipetpakve śubhe gandhakapiṣṭikām niṣkārdhaṃ bhasma vaikrāntamūrdhvādho nikṣipetsudhīḥ  k tatkandamajjayā vaktraṃ nirudhya ca mṛdā bahiḥ limpedaṅgulimātreṇa śoṣayitvātha sarvataḥ  k aṣṭavāraṃ pacedyantre bhūdhare kaukkuṭe puṭe karīṣāgnau punaḥ kuryādūrdhvabhāgamadhaḥ priye  k adhobhāgaṃ tathordhvaṃ ca bhūyo bhūyaḥ pravartanam evamekadinaṃ paścātpacedyugakarīṣakaiḥ  k pakvadāḍimabījābho baddho bhavati pāradaḥ vaikrāntabaddhanāmā syāccūrṇito yogavāhakaḥ  k dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥgandhakabandhaḥpūrvoktāṃ gandhapiṣṭīṃ tāṃ vastre baddhvātha saṃpuṭe lohaje poṭṭalīṃ sthāpyacordhvādhaḥ samagandhakam  k nirudhya saṃpuṭaṃ samyak pacet bhūdharayantrake yathā jīrṇo bhavedgandho bhūyo bhūyastathāpi ca  k eva ṣaḍguṇagandhastu jāraṇīyo maheśvari evaṃ gandhakabaddhoyaṃ rasaḥ sarvāmayāpahaḥ  k tṛtīyaḥ prakāraḥgandhakabandhaḥṣoḍaśāṅguladīrghā ca jambīraphalavistṛtā pakvamūṣā dṛḍhatarā vālukāyantramadhyataḥ  k tribhāgamagnāṃ kurvīta bahiḥ pādāṃśasaṃsthitām tasyāṃ kṣipedgandhasūtaṃ palamekaṃ sureśvari  k sūtād athordhvabhāge tu dvipalaṃ śuddhagandhakam nikṣipettanmukhaṃ samyagrodhayenmandavahninā  k pacennirdhūmatā yāvattāvaddhūme gate punaḥ kākamācīdravaiḥ pūryā taddrave jīrṇatāṃ gate  k rasena nāgavallyāśca pūraṇīyā punaḥ priye unmattakarasaiḥ pūryā śanairmandāgninā pacet  k gandhakaṃ jīryate yāvatkākamācyādikadravaiḥ dhattūrāntaiḥ pacedevaṃ baddho bhavati pāradaḥ  k nāmnā gandhakabaddhoyaṃ sarvayogeṣu yojayet caturthaḥ prakāraḥ gandhakasvarṇabandhaḥpūrvavadgandhapiṣṭiṃ ca vidhāyādau vicakṣaṇaḥ  k saptārdhaniṣkasūtaḥ syādadhyardhaṃ śuddhahāṭakam yāmamamlena saṃmardyaṃ khyātoyaṃ hemapiṣṭikā  k gandhapiṣṭiṃ hemapiṣṭyā samayāveṣṭya bāhyataḥ stanākāre lohamaye saṃpuṭe vastrabandhitām  k kṛtvā tāṃ piṣṭikāṃ kṣiptvā piṣṭyūrdhvādhaśca gandhakam sarvatulyaṃ kṣipet sandhiṃ ruddhvāmlalavaṇaiḥ sudhīḥ  k pacedbhūdharayantre ca jīrṇe jīrṇe punaḥ punaḥ ṣaḍguṇaṃ gandhakaṃ dadyāttato vastraṃ śanairharet  k samāṃśaṃ gandhakaṃ bhūyo bhūyo jāryaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ niḥśeṣaṃ gandhakaṃ naiva kuryāccetpāradacyutiḥ  k evaṃ śataguṇe jīrṇe gandhapiṣṭiṃ samāharet tatsamāṃśasuvarṇasya saṃpuṭe piṣṭikāṃ kṣipet  k kācaṃ kanyādravaiḥ piṣṭvā lepayedbāhyatoṅgulam tataṣṭaṅkaṇakairliptvā paścānmṛllavaṇaiḥ kramāt  k ekaikaṃ lepanaṃ kāryaṃ veṣṭyamaṅgulamānakam pratilepaṃ śoṣayecca koṣṭhīyantragataṃ dhamet  k vaṅkanālena tīvreṇa vahninā praharaṃ bhavet udayādityasaṅkāśaṃ khoṭaṃ divyarasāyanam  k gandhahāṭakabandhoyaṃ jarāvyādhidaridrahā pañcamaḥ prakāraḥ gandhakabandhaḥathavā gandhapiṣṭiṃ tāṃ vastre baddhvātha gandhakam  k tulyaṃ dattvā nirudhyātha saṃpuṭe lohaje dṛḍham puṭettadbhūdhare tāvadyāvajjīryati gandhakam  k evaṃ punaḥ punardeyaṃ yāvadgandhaṃ tu ṣaḍguṇam ityevaṃ gandhake baddhaḥ sūtaḥ syātsarvarogajit  k ṣaṣṭhaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥkārkoṭīmūlajairdrāvaiḥ pāradaṃ mardayeddinam markaṭīmūlaje piṇḍe kṣipettaṃ marditaṃ rasam  k taṃ piṇḍaṃ vajramūṣāyāṃ ruddhvā tīvrāgninā pacet jāyate khoṭabaddhoyaṃ sarvakāryakaraḥ śubhaḥ  k saptamaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥarkamūlaṃ ravikṣīraiḥ piṣṭvā mūṣāṃ pralepayet tanmadhye rañjitaṃ sūtaṃ kṣiptvā baddhvātha rodhayet  k mṛṇmaye saṃpuṭe taṃ ca nirundhyāllohasaṃpuṭe pacedgajapuṭe paścātpārado bandhamāpnuyāt  k aṣṭamaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥjalakumbhīrasaiḥ sūtaṃ mardayeddivasatrayam jalakumbhīdalairmūṣāṃ kṛtvā tatra kṣipedrasam  k ruddhvā tāṃ vajramūṣāyāṃ chāyāśuṣkaṃ puṭellaghu chagaṇairekavṛddhyā tu triṃśadvāraṃ puṭaiḥ pacet  k tato gajapuṭe deyaṃ samyagbaddho bhavedrasaḥ navamaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥekavīrādravairmardyaṃ dinaṃ śuddhaṃ tu sūtakam  k ekavīrākandakalkairvajramūṣāṃ pralepayet tasyāṃ pūrvarasaṃ kṣiptvā dhmāte baddho bhavedrasaḥ  k daśamaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥāraktakṣīrakandotthadravaiḥ strīstanyasaṃyutaiḥ tridinaṃ pāradaṃ mardyaṃ vajrakandadravaistryaham  k kṣīrakandasya kalkena vajramūṣāṃ pralepayet tatra pūrvarasaṃ baddhvā dhmāte baddho bhavedrasaḥ  k ekādaśaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥarkamūlaphalaṃ piṣṭvā mūṣāṃ tena pralepayet tanmadhye nikṣipenmūṣāṃ puṅkhāmūlavinirmitām  k tanmadhye sūtakaṃ kṣiptvā puṅkhāmūlasamudbhavaiḥ pūrayitvā rasairmūṣāṃ nirundhyāt tanmukhaṃ dṛḍham  k evamandhīkṛtāṃ mūṣāṃ kṣipetsampuṭamadhyataḥ tatastaṃ lepayedyatnāllavaṇena mṛdā tathā  k tatosau puṭayogena sūto bandhamavāpnuyāt rājikādvayamātreṇa citrakadravasaindhavaiḥ  k cūrṇito bhakṣitaḥ prātaḥ sarvarogavināśakaḥ dvādaśaḥ prakāraḥ mūlikābandhaḥkapitthasya śiphānīrairyāmaṃ sūtaṃ vimardayet  k anyasyām andhamūṣāyāṃ sūtamūṣāṃ nirodhayet tathā dhamettato mūṣāṃ yathā sindūravad bhavet  k evaṃ kṛte rasendrosau badhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ mūlikābandhanaṃ hyetadrasendrasya prakīrtitam  k ityete māritāḥ sūtā mūrchitā bandhamāgatāḥ pratyekaṃ yojitāstatra prayogairyogavāhinaḥ  k rasamūrcchanāvidhiḥprathamaḥ prakāraḥatha śuddhasya sūtasya mūrcchanāvidhirucyate meghanādavacāhiṅgulaśunair mardayedrasam  k dinaṃ piṣṭaṃ tu tadgolaṃ hiṅgunā veṣṭayedbahiḥ pacellavaṇayantrasthaṃ dinaikaṃ caṇḍavahninā  k ūrdhvalagnaṃ samādāya dṛḍhaṃ vastreṇa bandhayet ūrdhvādho gandhakaṃ tulyaṃ dattvā somānale pacet  k jīrṇe gandhaṃ punardeyaṃ ṣaḍbhirvāraiḥ samaṃ samam ṣaḍguṇe gandhake jīrṇe mūrchito rogahā bhavet  k dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥgandhakaṃ dhūmasāraṃ ca śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ samaṃ samam yāmaikaṃ cūrṇayetkhalve kācakupyāṃ niveśayet  k ruddhvā dvādaśayāmāntaṃ vālukāyantrake pacet sphoṭayet svāṃgaśītaṃ tamūrdhvasthaṃ gandhakaṃ tyajet  k adhaḥsthaṃ rasam ādāya sarvayogeṣu yojayet tṛtīyaḥ prakāraḥśuddhasūtaṃ tathā gandhaṃ sūtārdhaṃ saindhave kṣipet  k dravaiḥ sitajayantyāśca mardayeddivasatrayam kṛtvā golaṃ tu saṃśoṣya mūṣāyāṃ taṃ nirodhayet  k śoṣayitvā dhamet kiṃcit sutaptetha jale kṣipet tasmādrasaṃ samuddhṛtya trikandarasabhāvitam  k yojayet sarvarogeṣu dhamedvā bhūdhare pacet caturthaḥ prakāraḥrasārdhaṃ gandhakaṃ mardyaṃ ghṛtairyuktaṃ tu golakam  k kṛtvā tadbandhayedvastre ḍolāyantragataṃ pacet gomūtre tadgataṃ yāmaṃ naramūtrairdinatrayam  k śoṣayettatpunarvastrairbaddhvā veṣṭyaṃ mṛdā dṛḍham śuṣkaṃ nirudhya mūṣāyāṃ pacedatha tuṣāgninā  k ūrdhvabhāgamadhaḥ kṛtvā tvadhobhāgamathordhvagam ityādiparivartena svedayeddivasatrayam  k paścāduddhṛtya taṃ sūtaṃ yogavāhaṃ rujāpaham sadyojātasya bālasya viṣṭhāṃ pālāśabījakam  k caṇḍālīrudhiraṃ sūtaṃ sūtapādaṃ ca ṭaṅkaṇam jayantyā mardayed drāvairdinamekaṃ tu golakam  k piṣṭayā sahadevyātha lepayettāmrasampuṭam tanmadhye golakaṃ kṣiptvā dviyāmaṃ svedayellaghu  k vālukāyantramadhye tu samuddhṛtya tataḥ punaḥ citrakaiḥ sahadevyā ca gandhakaṃ lepayedbahiḥ  k sampuṭaṃ bandhayedvastre mṛdā lepyaṃ ca śoṣayet taṃ ruddhvā cānyamūṣāyāṃ dhmāte sampuṭamāharet  k sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ haredrogānyogavāho mahārasaḥ sampuṭaṃ sūtatulyaṃ syācchāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā  k pañcamaḥ prakāraḥdhuttūrakadravairmardyaṃ dinaṃ gandhāṃśasūtakam andhamūṣāgataṃ svedyaṃ bhūdhare mūrchito dināt  k ṣaṣṭhaḥ prakāraḥkṛtvā ṣaḍaṅgulāṃ mūṣāṃ supakvāṃ mṛṇmayīṃ dṛḍhām mūṣāgarbhe vilipyātha mūlair vartulapattrajaiḥ  k tanmadhye sūtakaṃ kṣiptvā mūṣāṃ pūryāttu taddravaiḥ ruddhvā tāṃ vālukāyantre cullyāṃ dīpāgninā pacet  k saptāhānte samuddhṛtya yojayettaṃ jarāpaham saptamaḥ prakāraḥkuraṇḍakarasaiḥ sāndramātape mardayedrasam  k latākarañjapatrotthaiḥ pādāṃguṣṭhena mardayet dinaikaṃ mūrchitaṃ samyak sarvayogeṣu yojayet  k aṣṭamaḥ prakāraḥkāsīsaṃ saindhavaṃ sūtaṃ tulyaṃ tulyaṃ vimardayet kāsīsasyāpyabhāve tu dātavyā phullatūrikā  k stokaṃ stokaṃ kṣipetkhalve trayamekatra mūrchayet pratyekaṃ śataniṣkaṃ syādūnaṃ naivādhikaṃ kvacit  k sthālīsampuṭayantreṇa dinaṃ caṇḍāgninā pacet ūrdhvalagnaṃ tataḥ śubhraṃ mūrchitaṃ cāharecchubham  k navamaḥ prakāraḥatha śuddhasya sūtasya mūrchitasyāparo vidhiḥ sūtatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ svarṇaṃ dvābhyāṃ tulyaṃ ca gandhakam  k ravikṣīrairdinaṃ mardyamandhayedbhūdhare puṭe dinaikena bhavetsiddho raso hairaṇyagarbhakaḥ  k śubhraḥ śoṇothavā kṛṣṇavarṇo gurutaro rasaḥ punarutthānavānyastu mūrchitaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ  k mūlikābandhāḥśrībhairavī kīdṛśī oṣadhī nātha rasamūrcchākarī śubhā kena vā bhasma sūtaśca kena vā khoṭabandhanam  k śrībhairavaḥ śṛṇu bhairavi tattvena rahasyaṃ rasabandhanam brahmaviṣṇusurendrādyairna jñātaṃ suravandite  k niśācaramūlikākalpaḥgaṅgāyamunayormadhye prayāgo nāma rākṣasaḥ tasyāsane varārohe kṣaṇādbadhyeta sūtakaḥ  k niśācarasya patrāṇi gṛhṇīyātsādhakottamaḥ tato nipīḍyate devi raso bhavati cottamaḥ  k rasaṃ saṃmardya tenaiva dināni trīṇi vārtikaḥ āroṭaṃ bandhayetkṣipraṃ gaganaṃ tatra jārayet  k tena patrarasenaiva sādhayedgandhakaṃ punaḥ saptadhā bhāvitaṃ tena tryūṣaṇena sahaikataḥ  k yantre vidyādhare devi gaganaṃ tatra jārayet māsamātreṇa deveśi jīryate tu samaṃ samam  k samajīrṇe tu gagane śatavedhī bhavedrasaḥ niśācararase devi gandhakaṃ bhāvayettataḥ  k bhāvayetsaptavāraṃ tu dvipadyāśca rasena tu tārasya patralepena ardhārdhe kāñcanottamam  k gandhake samajīrṇe smin śatavedhī bhavedrasaḥ niśācararasairbhāvyaṃ saptavāraṃ tu tālakam  k tenaiva ghātayedvaṅgaṃ nāgaṃ tāre tu nirvahet tattāraṃ jārayetsūte tatsūtaṃ bandhitaṃ bhavet  k catuḥ ṣaṣṭitame bhāge śulbavedhaṃ tu dāpayet tadaṃśaṃ jāyate śreṣṭhaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam  k niśācarasya puṣpāṇi sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet palāni daśacūrṇasya rasairdhātryāstu bhāvayet  k ghṛtena madhunāloḍyaṃ navabhāṇḍe vinikṣipet dhānyarāśau nidhātavyaṃ triḥ saptāhaṃ sureśvari  k tena bhakṣitamātreṇa valīpalitavarjitaḥ valkalaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu madhunā sahitaṃ lihet  k ardhamāsaprayogeṇa pratyayogaṃ bhavetpriye tasya mūtrapurīṣeṇa śulbaṃ bhavati kāñcanam  k māsamātraprayogeṇa pannagaḥ kāñcanaṃ bhavet mercury paṭṭabandhagrāhyaṃ tatphalatailaṃ tu yantre pātālasaṃjñake  k tena tailena deveśi rasaṃ saṃkocayed budhaḥ tatkṣaṇājjāyate devi pāṭabandho mahārasaḥ  k kaṭakaṃ kaṅkaṇaṃ kāryaṃ rasaliṅgaṃ varānane saṃkocamaraṇaṃ tena kartavyaṃ paramādbhutam  k aṅganāyikākalpaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham trailokyajananī yā sā oṣadhī aṅganāyikā  k tayā saṃparkamātreṇa baddhastiṣṭhati pāradaḥ saptāhaṃ marditasyāsya mahauṣadhyā rasai rasaḥ  k śatāṃśenaiva vedhena kurute divyakāñcanam triḥ saptāhaṃ rase tasyā mardanādvaravarṇini  k lakṣavedhī rasaḥ sākṣādaṣṭau lohāni vidhyati trisaptāhena deveśi daśalakṣāṇi vidhyati  k caturthe caiva saptāhe koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ svedatāpanigharṣeṇa mahauṣadhyā rasena tu  k dadāti khecarīṃ siddhimanivāritagocaraḥ kāmayetkāminīnāṃ tu sahasraṃ divasāntare  k naṣṭacchāyo hyadṛśyaśca trailokyaṃ ca bhramedasau mahauṣadhyā rasenaiva mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ bhavet  k anena ghātayetsūtaṃ pañcāvasthaṃ kuru priye mṛtasya dāpayennasyaṃ hastau pādau tu mardayet  k tasya tu praviśejjīvo mṛtasyāpi varānane narasārakalpaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham  k narasārasparśanena kṣaṇādbadhyeta sūtakaḥ narasārarasaṃ dattvā dvipadīrajasā rase  k dinānte bandhamāyāti sarvalohāni rañjati narasārarasenaiva bhāvayettu manaḥśilām  k nirgandhā jāyate sā tu ghātayettena pannagam dvipadīrajasā sārdhaṃ niruddhaḥ pannago bhavet  k narasārarasenaiva jīrṇe ṣaḍguṇapannage tāre tāmrepi vā devi koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ  k narasārarase stanye bhāvitaṃ saptadhā pṛthak rasasya dāpayedgrāsaṃ yantre vidyādharāhvaye  k jīryate gaganaṃ devi nirmukhe ca varānane narasāraraseneśi kīṭanārīrasena ca  k drāvayedgaganaṃ devi tīkṣṇalohaṃ ca pannagam narasāraraseneśi hanumatyā rasena ca  k jāyate kāñcanaṃ divyaṃ niṣekādbhāskaraḥ priye narasārarase dattvā mañjiṣṭhāṃ raktacandanam  k svarasairmadayantyāśca pannagaṃ devi secayet tatkṣaṇātkāñcanaṃ divyaṃ saptavārā niṣecitam  k aṣṭamāṃśayutaṃ hema hemakarmaṇi cauṣadham narasārarase bhāvyaṃ saptavāraṃ tu hiṅgulam  k tenaiva ghātayettīkṣṇaṃ bhasmībhūtatvamāpnuyāt tadbhasma tāmrapiṣṭe tu triguṇaṃ tena nirvahet  k tacchulbaṃ hemasaṅkāśaṃ tāre vāṣṭāṃśayojitam tāraṃ hemasamāṃśaṃ tu dvivarṇaṃ patitaṃ bhavet  k narasārarase bhāvyaṃ rasakaṃ saptavārataḥ narasārarasenaiva rasendraṃ saptavārataḥ  k taṃ rasaṃ rasakaṃ caiva tīkṣṇalohaṃ ca pannagam narasārarasenaiva tenaikatra vimardayet  k tatkṣaṇājjāyate baddho rasasya rasakasya ca tīkṣṇanāgaṃ tathā śulbaṃ rasakena tu rañjayet  k haṭhāttajjāyate hema kūṣmāṇḍakusumaprabham kaṅkālakhecarīkalpaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham  k kaṅkālakhecarī nāmnā oṣadhī parameśvari tasya tailaṃ tu saṃgrāhyam ādyakhecarisaṃyutam  k sthāpayeddinamekaṃ tu pātre bhāskaranirmite dvitīye vāsare prāpte vajraratnaṃ tu ghātayet  k anale dhāmayettaṃ tu sutaptaṃ prajvalatprabham mantrasihmāsanīkalpaḥsabījā cauṣadhī grāhyā kācidgulmalatā priye  k mantrasiṃhāsanī nāma tṛtīyā devi khecarī pātālayantre tattailaṃ gṛhṇīyāttāmrabhājane  k tasya tailasya madhye tu prakṣipetkhecarīrasam medinīyantramadhye tu sthāpayecca varānane  k pūrvauṣadhyāṃ tu taddevi gaganaṃ medinījale rase māsaṃ tato dattvā mardanād golakaṃ kuru  k baddhvā poṭṭalikāṃ tena gaganaṃ jārayetpriye same tu gagane jīrṇe baddhastiṣṭhati pāradaḥ  k bhastrāphūtkārayuktena dhāmyamāno na naśyati kākaviṣṭhāsamaṃ rūpaṃ samajīrṇasya jāyate  k dviguṇe gagane jīrṇe hyaṣṭalohāni saṃharet irindirīkalpaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham  k śivadehātsamutpannā oṣadhī tu irindirī jārayedgandhakaṃ sā tu jārayetsāpi tālakam  k kāñcanaṃ jārayetsā tu rasendraṃ sā ca bandhayet pravālaṃ drāvayetsā tu drāvayedgaganaṃ tathā  k vajraṃ ca ghātayetsā tu sarvasatvaṃ ca ghātayet jārayetsarvalohāni satvānyapi ca jārayet  k irindirīrase nyasya gośṛṅge tu varānane dhānyarāśau nidhātavyaṃ drutastiṣṭhati pāradaḥ  k divyauṣadhyā rasenaiva rasendraḥ suravandite same tu kanake jīrṇe daśakoṭiṃ tu vedhayet  k pañcame lakṣakoṭiṃ tu ṣaḍguṇe sparśavedhakaḥ saptame dhūpavedhī syādaṣṭame tvavalokataḥ  k navame śabdavedhī syādata ūrdhvaṃ na vidyate bhramanti paśavo mūḍhāḥ kulauṣadhivivarjitāḥ  k tṛṇauṣadhirasānāṃ ca naiva siddhiḥ prajāyate tasmātsarvaprayatnena jñātavyā tu kulauṣadhiḥ  k divyauṣadhyaścatuḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ kulamadhye vyavasthitāḥ naiva jānāti mūḍhāstāḥ śivamohena mohitāḥ  k adivyāstu tṛṇauṣadhyo jāyante girigahvare tṛṇauṣadhyā rase sūto naiva baddhaḥ kadācana  k akṣayo naiva tiṣṭheta kulauṣadhivivarjitaḥ kulauṣadhyā vihīnāstu gaganaṃ cārayanti ye  k sa rasastu varārohe vahnimadhye na tiṣṭhati na khoṭaṃ na ca vā bhasma naiva dravyaṃ karoti saḥ  k kiṃciddravyaṃ prakurvanti dhāmyamānaṃ na tiṣṭhati patre pāke kaṣe chede naiva tiṣṭhati kāñcanam  k na vedhaṃ ca śatādūrdhvaṃ karoti sa rasaḥ priye yāvanna cābdam ekaṃ tu vikrāntaṃ trapu tattu kāñcanam  k dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu naiva dadyāttataḥ priye śrībhairavī nirjīvatvaṃ gataḥ sūtaḥ kathaṃ jīvaṃ dadāti saḥ  k nirjīvena tu nirjīvaṃ kathaṃ jīvati śaṃkaraḥ śrībhairavaḥ divyauṣadhyā yadā devi rasendro mardito bhavet  k kālikārahitaḥ sūtastadā bhavati pārvati parasya harate kālaṃ kālikārahito rasaḥ  k aṣṭānāṃ caiva lohānāṃ malaṃ śamayati kṣaṇāt mahāmūrcchāgataṃ sūtaṃ ko vā vikathayenmṛtam  k divyauṣadhyā rasenaiva jāyate naṣṭacetanaḥ pañcabhūtātmakaḥ sūtastiṣṭhatyeva sadāśivaḥ  k kṣmāpālakalpaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhanamīśvari kṣmāpālena haredvajram anenaiva tu kāñcanam  k vajrabhasma hemabhasma tadvā ekatra bandhayet anye kulamūlikākalpāḥniśācararase jāryaṃ narajīvena jārayet  k taṃ sūtaṃ mārayedbhadre jāgarir divya oṣadhiḥ bhakṣitaḥ sa raso yena sopi sākṣātsadāśivaḥ  k bhakṣite tolakaikena sparśavedhī bhavennaraḥ prasvedāttasya gātrasya aṣṭau lohāni kāñcanam  k lakṣavarṣasahasrāṇi sa jīvetsādhakottamaḥ prasvedāttasya gātrasya rasarājaśca badhyate  k ajāpatiḥ kṛṣṇatejāḥ kṣaṇādbadhnāti sūtakam jāgarīsparśanāddevi kṣmāpālena ca badhyate  k turuvallyā rasenaiva bhāvitaṃ gaganaṃ priye jārayedvālukāyantre khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k drutagolakamāṣaikaṃ māṣaikaṃ hemagolakam ekīkṛtya tu saṃmardya luṅgāmlena dinatrayam  k karṣaikaṃ nāgapatrāṇi rasakalkena lepayet veṣṭayedvṛścikālīṃ ca tatpiṇḍaṃ lepayettataḥ  k mārayetpannagaṃ devi śakragopanibhaṃ bhavet karṣaikaṃ tāraparṇāni mṛtanāgena lepayet  k lepayed vṛścikālīṃ ca tatpatraṃ lepayettataḥ tattāraṃ mriyate devi sindūrāruṇasannibham  k sahasrāṃśena tenaiva śulbavedhaṃ pradāpayet jāyate kanakaṃ divyaṃ devābharabhūṣaṇam  k kṣīrayuktā bahuphalā granthiyuktā ca pārvati nāmnā vartulapattrāṇi śasyate rasabandhane  k ekavāraṃ kandakalke mūkamūṣāgataṃ rasam dhamenmukhānilairbaddho bhakṣaṇāya praśasyate  k raktakañcukikandaṃ tu strīstanyena tu peṣitam mūṣāyāṃ pūrvayogena kurute sūtabandhanam  k vṛścikāpattrikābījaṃ nārīkṣīrasamanvitam dhamayet pūrvavatsūtaṃ bhakṣaṇārthāya vārtikaḥ  k vajrakandaṃ samādāya rasaṃ madhye vinikṣipet gajendrākhyaṃ puṭaṃ dadyātsaptadhā bandhatāṃ nayet  k bhakṣayettaṃ rasaṃ prājñaḥ ṣaṇmāsādamaro bhavet lāṅgalīkandamādāya karkoṭīkandam eva ca  k rasaṃ tanmadhyagaṃ kṛtvā svedayenmardayetpunaḥ mriyate nātra sandeho dhmātastīvrānalena tu  k śukacañcugataṃ sūtaṃ puṭayeddhāmayettataḥ śatāṃśavedhakartāyaṃ dehasiddhikaro bhavet  k haṃsapādīrasaṃ sūtaṃ śuṣkakandodare kṣipet gajendrapuṭanaṃ dadyānmriyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  k sahasravedhakartā ca jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ haṃsāṅghriṃ śukacañcuṃ ca gṛhītvā mardayedrasam  k krauñcapādodare kṣiptvā tato dadyātpuṭatrayam mriyate nātra sandeho lakṣavedhī mahārasaḥ  k tṛṇajyotiḥkalpaḥtṛṇajyotiriti khyātāṃ śṛṇu divyauṣadhiṃ priye niśā tu prajvalennityaṃ nāhnā jvalati pārvati  k tasya mūle tu saṃkṣipte kṣīraṃ raktaṃ bhavetkṣaṇāt tanmūlarasagandhābhrair mātuluṅgāmlapeṣitaiḥ  k śulbapatraṃ viliptaṃ tu bhaveddhema puṭatrayāt tanmūlacūrṇasaṃyukto rasarājaḥ sureśvari  k mātuluṅgarase ghṛṣṭamabhrakaṃ carati kṣaṇāt uccāṭākalpaḥathoccāṭāṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhakarīṃ priye  k ekameva bhavennālaṃ tasyā romapraveṣṭanam tasyāgre ca bhavetpuṣpaṃ śukatuṇḍasya sannibham  k tatpatrāṇi ca deveśi śukapiñchanibhāni ca tatkandaṃ kūrmasaṃsthānaṃ kṣīraṃ sindūrasannibham  k jalaṃ sravenmadhūcchiṣṭe tatsamādāya pārvati vedhayetsarvalohāni kāñcanāni bhavanti ca  k rasatālakatutthāni mardayeduccaṭārasaiḥ ātape mriyate tapto raso divyauṣadhībalāt  k vedhayetsarvalohāni lakṣāṃśena varānane āvartitaṃ bhavedyāvajjāyaterkasamaprabham  k raktasnuhīkalpaḥrasaṃ raktasnuhīkṣīraṃ kunaṭīṃ gandhakābhrakam daradaṃ caiva lohāni sahasrāṃśena vedhayet  k snuhīkṣīraṃ samādāya niśācūrṇena veṣṭayet guṭikīkṛtya tenaiva nāgaṃ vidhyati tatkṣaṇāt  k sthalapadminīkalpaḥathātaḥ sthalapadminyā divyauṣadhyā vidhiṃ śṛṇu padminīsadṛśā patraiḥ puṣpairapi ca tādṛśī  k bhaṅge caiva sravetkṣīraṃ raktavarṇā suśobhanā ākramya vāmapādena paśyedgaganamaṇḍalam  k paśyecca tārakāyuktaṃ grahanakṣatramaṇḍalam lakṣayojanato devi sā jñeyā sthalapadminī  k tasyāḥ pañcāṅgamādāya haragaurīsamanvitam manaḥśilātālayuktaṃ mākṣikeṇa samanvitam  k mardayetsaptarātraṃ tu tena śulbaṃ ca vedhayet sahasrāṃśena deveśi viddhaṃ bhavati kāñcanam  k tasyāḥ pañcāṅgamādāya pūrvoktavidhinā priye cārayetsūtarājaṃ tu mūkamūṣāgataṃ dhamet  k mriyate mūṣikāmadhye saṃkocena na saṃśayaḥ tenaiva sarvalohāni sahasrāṃśena vedhayet  k citrakakalpaḥcitrakasya yathā guhyaṃ kathayāmi samāsataḥ trividhaścitrako jñeyaḥ kṛṣṇo rakto rasāyanam  k śuklo vyādhipraśamanaḥ śreṣṭhamadhyakanīyasāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ raktaṃ sitaṃ vāpi hemante noddhared budhaḥ  k kṛṣṇacitrakamutpāṭya gobhirnāghrātamīśvari kṣīramadhye kṣipetkṣīraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ bhavet kṣaṇāt  k tasya pañcāṅgacūrṇena pāradaṃ saha mardayet dhamecca mūkamūṣāyāṃ khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k raktāṃbaradharo bhūtvā raktamālyānulepanaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe tu pañcamyāṃ raktamālyaudanena tu  k baliṃ dattvā mahādevi raktacitrakamuddharet raktacitrakacūrṇena vaṅgaṃ pāyaistribhistribhiḥ  k sarvadoṣavinirmuktaḥ stambhamāyāti tatkṣaṇāt tanmūlaṃ sūtakaṃ tāmraṃ kuṅkuṇītailasecanāt  k ekaviṃśativāreṇa śuddhaṃ jyotiṣmatītailakalpaḥjyotiṣmatītailavidhiṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu pārvati  k jyotiṣmatī nāma latā yā ca kāñcanasannibhā vallīvitānabahulā hemavarṇaphalā śubhā  k āṣāḍhapūrvapakṣesyā gṛhītvā bījamuttamam tilavatkvāthayitvā vā hastapādairathāpi vā  k tasyāstailaṃ samādāya kumbhe tāmramaye kṣipet sthāpayedbhūgataṃ kumbhaṃ kramādūrdhvatuṣāgninā  k ṣaṇmāse tu vyatikrānte sa ghaṭaḥ kāñcanaṃ bhavet tāmraṃ hemasamaṃ kṛtvā tailamākṣīkamiśritam  k prativāpena siñcet taddhema tāmrasamaṃ bhavet tathā ca śatavedhī syādvidyāratnam anuttamam  k dagdharuhākalpaḥdagdharuhāṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabandhakarīṃ priye sparśauṣadhīti sā jñeyā sarvakāmārthasādhanī  k śaśvacchinnā mahādevi dagdhā sā pāvakena tu prarohati kṣaṇāddivyā dagdhā sā tu mahauṣadhī  k raktaṃ pītaṃ sitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tasyāḥ puṣpaṃ prajāyate caṇakasyeva patrāṇi suprasūtāni lakṣayet  k sā sthitā gomatītīre gaṅgāyāmarbude girau ujjayinyā dakṣiṇato vanānteṣu ca dṛśyate  k tasyāḥ kandarasaṃ divye kṛṣṇarājīsamanvitam tāmbūlena samaṃ kṛtvā ghuṭikāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ  k sarveṣāmeva lohānāṃ drutānāṃ vahnimadhyataḥ sahasraṃ vedhayitvā tu kāñcanaṃ kurute kṣaṇāt  k tathaiva mriyate sūtaḥ kāntahemābhrasaṃyutaḥ kaṭutumbīkalpaḥkaṭutuṃbī tu vikhyātā devi divyauṣadhiṃ śṛṇu  k tasyā bījāni saṃgṛhya sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu kārayet ekaviṃśativārāṇi bhāvyaṃ dhātrīrasena ca  k payasā saha tenaiva viśvabheṣajasaṃyutam bījaṃ yantre vinikṣipya tailaṃ saṃgṛhya piṇḍitaḥ  k rasaṃ mūrchāpayettena cakramardena mardayet lohadaṇḍakalpaḥgopittaṃ śikhipittaṃ ca kāṃkṣīkāsīsasaṃyutam  k tāratulyāni caitāni sarveṣāṃ sūtakaṃ samam meṣaśṛṅge nidhātavyaṃ māsamekaṃ nirantaram  k lohadaṇḍena saṃsiktaṃ sarvalohāni vedhayet gandhakaṃ lohadaṇḍena ekaviṃśatibhāvitam  k yuktaṃ lohakulenaiva jambīrarasasaṃyutam sabījaṃ sūtakopetamandhamūṣāniveśitam  k bhūgataṃ tu sudaṇḍena tu kārayet pañcaviṃśaddinānte tu jāyate kanakottamam  k kṣīrakandakalpaḥkṣīrakandavidhiṃ vakṣye sarvasiddhikaraṃ tathā caturvarṇaṃ viṣaṃ tatra raktakandaṃ praśasyate  k bhagnametatsravetkṣīraṃ raktavarṇaṃ suśobhanam meghānāṃ tu ninādena saṃjātair upaśobhitam  k patraiḥ snuhīsamaiḥ snigdhaiḥ samabhir hemasatprabhaiḥ bandhanaṃ rasarājasya sarvasatvavaśaṃkaram  k tasya kṣīraṃ tu saṃgṛhya tāraṃ nirvāhayedbudhaḥ dhameddhaṭhāgninā caiva jāyate hema śobhanam  k tintriṇīpatraniryāsamīṣattāmrarajoyutam mardayetpāradaṃ prājño rasabandho bhaviṣyati  k toyamadhye vinikṣipya gulikā vajravadbhavet śākavṛkṣakalpaḥśākavṛkṣasya deveśi niṣpīḍya rasamuttamam  k raktacandanasaṃyuktaṃ sarvalohāni jārayet milanti sarvalohāni dravanti salilaṃ yathā  k gandhakaṃ rasakaṃ tāpyaṃ pāradaṃ raktacandanam rudantyā rasasaṃyuktaṃ tāramāyāti kāñcanam  k śākavṛkṣasya niryāsaṃ yatnataḥ parigālayet śigrumūlasya cūrṇaṃ tu tadrasena tu mardayet  k praliptaśulbapatrāṇi puṭetkṣiptvā vipācayet taddrutaṃ kāñcanaṃ divyaṃ bhavellakṣaṇasaṃyutam  k phalāni śākavṛkṣasya paripakvāni saṃgṛhet tadrasena tu samprājñaḥ saptarātraṃ tu bhāvayet  k tadrasena samāyuktaṃ mañjiṣṭhāmiśritaṃ tathā lepayettārapatrāṇi dhmātaṃ bhavati kāñcanam  k devadālīkalpaḥdevadālyā mahauṣadhyā vidhiṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param sā śvetā vyādhiśamane kṛṣṇā pītā rasāyane  k paurṇamāsyāṃ trayodaśyāṃ rāhugraste divākare athavā kṛṣṇapañcamyāmimāṃ vidhivaduddharet  k devadālīphalaṃ devi viṣṇukrāntāṃ ca sūtakam mūrchayed bandhayetkṣipraṃ śulbaṃ hema karoti ca  k devadālīphalaṃ mūlamīśvarīrasameva ca toyena marditaṃ kṛtvā vaṅgaṃ stambhayati kṣaṇāt  k śvetaguñjākalpaḥathātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi śvetaguñjāvidhiṃ priye kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāmaṣṭamyāṃ ca surārcite  k kapāle mṛttikāṃ nyasya secayetsalilena tu bījāni sitaguñjāyāḥ puṣyayoge tu vāpayet  k vakṣyamāṇena yogena kuryāt saṃgrahaṇaṃ tathā oṃ namo bhagavati śvetavalli śvetaparvatavāsini  k sarvakāryāṇi kuru kuru apratihataṃ namo namaḥ svāhā śuddhaśulbaṃ tu saṃgṛhya mūṣāmadhye tu saṃsthitam  k tripañcapalasaṃkhyā tu karṣārdhasitaguñjayā sahaikatra bhavaṃ tāraṃ tasya gandhavivarjitam  k brahmarītisamāyuktaṃ guñjācūrṇaṃ sahaikataḥ devīnāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ devi jāyate hema śobhanam  k kartarīrasabandhaḥathātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi kartarīrasabandhanam asurāṇāṃ samāyoge krodhāviṣṭena cetasā  k sudarśanaṃ mahācakraṃ preṣitaṃ muravairiṇā bhālapaṭṭāttatastasya nipetuḥ svedabindavaḥ  k te bhūmau patitā divyāḥ saṃjātāḥ kartarīrasaḥ rakṣārthaṃ sthāpitaṃ tatra viṣṇunā ca sudarśanam  k cakratulyaṃ bhramatyetadāyudhāni nikṛntati kurute garjanaṃ nādaṃ dhūmajvālāṃ vimuñcati  k kartarīdṛṣṭimātreṇa tathānyā śabdakartarī lokānāṃ tu hitārthāya ghoraśaktirvyavasthitā  k rasarūpā mahāghorā sā siddhānāṃ tu vedinī tasya kṣetraṃ yadā gacchedaghorāstraṃ japettadā  k punarghoraṃ nyasettatra athānyaṃ vinyasedbudhaḥ anulomavilomena dehedhiṣṭhāpya kartarīm  k mudrayā mudrayettāṃ tu aghorāstreṇa yojitām dīptena rodhayettāṃ tu stambhayed dīpanena tu  k niṣṭhayā mudrayā tāṃ tu sthānayogena yojayet udakabandhāḥcandrodakabandhaḥatha candrodakeneśi vakṣyāmi rasabandhanam  k dṛṣṭvā candrodakaṃ mantrī paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣataḥ grahaṇaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ prayatnataḥ  k nirgacchati mahīṃ bhittvā candravṛddhyā tu vardhate kṣetrabandhaṃ purā kṛtvā devamabhyarcya śaṅkaram  k caturdaśyāṃ tu tatkṣetraṃ pūjayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ahorātroṣito bhūtvā baliṃ tatra nivedayet  k paurṇamāsyāṃ ca rātrau ca gatvā tasya samīpataḥ candrodakaṃ tu saṃgṛhya mantrayuktaḥ sumantritam  k āloḍya madhusarpirbhyāṃ pibettattu samāhitaḥ pītamātreṇa tenaiva mūrchito bhavati kṣaṇāt  k candrodaye tathottiṣṭhetkṣāraṃ tasya tu dāpayet saptarātraprayogeṇa candravannirmalo bhavet  k ekaviṃśatirātreṇa jīved brahmadinatrayam ekamāsaprayogeṇa brahmāyuḥ sa bhavennaraḥ  k candrodakena gaganaṃ rasaṃ hema ca mardayet mūṣāmadhyagataṃ dhmātaṃ tatkṣaṇādghuṭikā bhavet  k ayaṃ tu sparśamātreṇa lohānyaṣṭau ca vedhayet tadrasaṃ tu rasaṃ cānyaṃ vajreṇa samajāritam  k catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśato vidhyeddviguṇena sahasrakam daśasaṅkalikābaddhaṃ guñjāmātraṃ rasaṃ tataḥ  k trilohaveṣṭitaṃ vaktre dhṛtvā cādṛśyatāṃ vrajet oṃ namo rudrāya daṃṣṭrotkaṭāya vighnaṃ nāśaya nāśaya diśo rakṣa rakṣa rudro jñāpayati huṃ phaṭ svāhā iti digbandhamantraḥ oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya triśūlahastāya amṛtodbhava rakṣa rakṣa huṃ phaṭ svāhā iti pānamantraḥ viṣodakabandhaḥathātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi viṣodarasabandhanam  k sitapītādivarṇāḍhyaṃ tatra devi rasottamam tatra gatvācaloddeśe smaredghoraṃ sahasrakam  k keśāḥ kṣiptāḥ sphuṭantyasminnātmacchāyāṃ na dṛśyate tailaṃ ca golakākāraṃ ghṛtaṃ tena visarpati  k gandhakasya haredgandhaṃ palalaṃ lavaṇāyate jñātvā palāśapatreṇa kaṭukālābuke kṣipet  k viṣodakaṃ gandhakaṃ ca harabījaṃ ca tatsamam ajākṣīreṇa piṣṭvā tu śulbapātre tu lepayet  k tatpuṭena bhaveddevi sindūrāruṇasannibham śatāṃśenaiva taddevi sarvalohāni vedhayet  k anena vidhinā devi nāgaḥ sindūratāṃ vrajet sahasrāṃśena tasyaiva tāraṃ bhavati kāñcanam  k raktaṃ pītaṃ tathā kṛṣṇamuttarottarakāryakṛt triphalākāntapātre vā pātrelābumayepi vā  k gṛhītvā pūrvavatpatraiḥ pālāśairveṣṭayedbahiḥ sthāpayeddhānyamadhye tu divasānekaviṃśatim  k mahiṣīkṣīramadhye tu bindumekaṃ tu sādhayet pāyasaṃ bhakṣayedyastu payomadhvājyasaṃyutam  k yāvatpūrṇaṃ balaṃ devi jīvettadbindusaṃkhyayā lāṅgalī gṛhadhūmaśca sindūraṃ rajanīdvayam  k meṣasya śṛṅgaṃ śṛṅgīṃ ca kṛṣṇonmattāśvamārakam sabījasūtakaṃ caiva viṣatoyena mardayet  k viṣatoyena medhāvī saptavārāṇi bhāvayet athavā bhāvayettaṃ tu yāvaccūrṇaṃ tu mardayet tadbhavet  k tena nāgaṃ pratīvāpya ṣoḍaśāṃśena khaṃ bhavet mūṣāsthaṃ veṇuyantre ca trīṇi vārāṇi bhāvayet  k dhūmaṃ pariharettasya aṅgavyādhikaraṃ param sthāpayennāgasindūraṃ pātrelābumaye ca tat  k taccūrṇaṃ tu śatāṃśena tāratāmrādi vedhayet viṣapānīyamādāya vaṅgamāvartitaṃ śubham  k niṣiktaṃ caiva tattoyaistāraṃ bhavati kāñcanam viṣapānīyamādāya prakṣipecca rasottame  k kunaṭīgandhapāṣāṇaviṣaṭaṅkaṇalāṅgalīḥ naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ khalve tārapatrāṇi lepayet  k andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ nirbījaṃ kanakaṃ bhavet oṃ hrīṃ nīlakaṇṭhāya ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ asya ayutaṃ japet iti viṣodakagrahaṇapānamantraḥ sañjīvanījalakalpaḥsaṃjīvanījalasyātha vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi pārvati  k śukreṇārādhito devi prāgahaṃ suravandite dānavānāṃ hitārthāya mṛtānāṃ devasaṅgare  k mayā saṃjīvanī vidyā dattā codakarūpiṇī tayā saṃjīvitā daityā ye mṛtā devasaṅgare  k nikṣiptā martyaloke sā samyak te kathayāmyaham asti martyā mahāpuṇyā pavitrā dakṣiṇāpathe  k dakṣiṇe tu taṭe tasyā utpalīnagaraṃ param tasya dakṣiṇataḥ śailaḥ sarvalokeṣu viśrutaḥ  k nāmnā kṛṣṇagiriḥ ceti dṛśyate sarvamaṅgale suprasiddhāmbikā nāma grāmastasyāsti sannidhau  k tatrāpyudakamālokya parīkṣeta surārcite gṛhītvā śuṣkavaṃśaṃ tu kṣipettoyasya madhyataḥ  k jāyate haritaṃ snigdhamahorātreṇa niścitam muñcatyaṅkurapatrāni dṛśyatetimanoharam  k balipuṣpopahāreṇa tato devi samarcayet kṣetrādhipaṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca candraṃ yogigaṇaṃ tathā  k oṃ candrāya pinākine śūlapāṇaye oṃ diśo bandha bandhaya diśo bandha bandhaya ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ tilāṃśca sarṣapāṃścaiva mantreṇānena sarṣapān saptābhimantritānkṛtvā sādhako dikṣu nikṣipet  k kaṭukālābuke toyaṃ kṛtarakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ gṛhītvā tatprayatnena nijaṃ sthānaṃ samāśrayet  k oṃ namo mṛte amṛtarūpiṇi amṛtaṃ kuru kuru evaṃ rudra ājñāpayati svāhā saptābhimantritaṃ kṛtvā mantreṇānena tajjalam dinamekaṃ tathā sūtaṃ svarṇamāṣadvayānvitam  k mardayettena toyena pibettattu vicakṣaṇaḥ ekaviṃśatirātraṃ tu kṣīrāhārotha yatnataḥ  k jīvetkalpāyutaṃ sāgraṃ kāmarūpo mahābalaḥ yojanānāṃ śataṃ gatvā punareva nivartate  k avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ svecchāhāraḥ sa khecaraḥ kanakaṃ pāradaṃ vyoma samam ekatra yojayet  k mardayettena toyena saptāhaṃ svedayettataḥ sa rasaḥ sarvalohāni ṣaṣṭyaṃśena tu vedhayet  k athavā taṃ rasaṃ divyaṃ madhunā saha bhakṣayet māsamātraprayogena jīved brahmadināyutam  k tasya mūtramalasvedaiḥ śulbaṃ bhavati kāñcanam nirvāte toyamādāya pāradaṃ ca manaḥśilām  k mardayet khalvapāṣāṇe naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ bhavettataḥ svedayetsaptarātraṃ tu trilohena ca veṣṭayet  k antardhānaṃ kṣaṇādgacchedvidyādharapatir bhavet siddhakanyāśatavṛto yāvatkalpāṃścaturdaśa  k dineṣu teṣu sarveṣu dadyācchālyodanaṃ ghṛtam payasā ca samāyuktaṃ nityamevaṃ ca kārayet  k uṣṇodakakalpaḥuṣṇodakavidhiṃ vakṣye samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu paśyatyuṣṇodakaṃ yatra vāsaṃ tatraiva kārayet  k śarvarīmuṣitāṃ tatra caṇakāstu dine dine bhakṣayenmāsamātraṃ tu jīvedvarṣaśatāṣṭakam  k tasya mūtrapurīṣeṇa śulbaṃ bhavati kāñcanam uṣṇodakaṃ ca kāsīsaṃ gandhapāṣāṇasaṃyutam  k caturthāṃśena rasakaṃ daśabhāgaṃ vinikṣipet śulbaṃ ca mardayetsarvaṃ naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ kṣaṇena tu  k tena lepitamātreṇa śulvaṃ bhavati kāñcanam niṣiktaṃ tena toyena prativāpaṃ dadedbudhaḥ  k śulbaṃ ca jāyate hema taruṇādityavarcasam tāraṃ ca tena mārgeṇa niṣiktaṃ hematāṃ vrajet  k uṣṇodakena bhallātaṃ tilamuṣṭiṃ ca bhakṣayet māsadvayaprayogeṇa jīvedvarṣaśatatrayam  k rasagandhāśmarasakatutthaṃ daradamākṣikam yāmamuṣṇāmbunā ghṛṣṭvā tārapatrāṇi lepayet  k vibhrāmya tu dhameddevi syāccaturdaśavarṇakam krameṇānena deveśi śulbaṃ ṣoḍaśavarṇakam  k ekaikaṃ hematārāṃśaṃ dvayaṃ kāṃtābhrayoḥ pṛthak uṣṇodakena saṃmardya dhamanātkhoṭatāṃ nayet  k taṃ mukhe dhārayenmāsaṃ vajrakāyo bhavettataḥ taccūrṇaṃ yavamātraṃ tu bhakṣayenmadhusarpiṣā  k yāvatpalaṃ tasya malaiḥ śulbaṃ bhavati kāñcanam uṣṇodapācitān khādet kulutthānkṣīrapo bhavet  k snānam uṣṇāṃbhasā kuryād varṣādvarṣācchatāyuṣaḥ kṣīramuṣṇodakaṃ kvāthaṃ triphalāyāśca pācayet  k pācayetpāyasaṃ kāntapātre bhuktvā mahāyuṣaḥ śailodakakalpaḥataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śailodakavidhiṃ priye  k kardamāpo mahīśailaśilā ceti caturvidham kānicit kṣaṇavedhīni dinavedhīni kāni ca  k pakṣamāsādiṣaṇmāsavedhanāni mahītale kṣiptaṃ jale yadā kāṣṭhaṃ śailībhūtaṃ ca dṛśyate  k bahirantaśca deveśi vedhakaṃ tatprakīrtitam hiṅgulaṃ haritālaṃ ca gandhakaṃ ca manaḥśilām  k eṣāṃ gandhāpahāraṃ tu kurute tacca vedhakam anyathā ceṣṭakaṃ devi tadagrāhyaṃ nirarthakam  k śrīśaile śrīvanaprānte paryaṅkākhye śilātale tatrasthaṃ kṣaṇavedhi syānnadyāṃ bhagavatītaṭe  k ekāhe vedhakaṃ tatra gokarṇe tu dinatrayam bhadrāṅge dinavedhi syāttristhalānte trivatsaram  k dhāreśvare pākṣikaṃ syāt karṣāpuryāṃ dinaikataḥ brahmeśvare māsikaṃ syādvyāghrapuryāṃ tu vāsaram  k aghoreśe māsikaṃ syātsiṃhadvīpe tathā punaḥ dinamekaṃ brahmagirau vindhye tu kṣaṇavedhakam  k vāsaraṃ mālyavante tu kṣaṇavedhī tu tatra ca kiṣkindhe parvate ramye pampātīre kṣaṇodakam  k tasya paścimato devi yojanadvitaye punaḥ bhūśailamasti tatraiva tridinaṃ vedaparvate  k anyatra yatra yatrāpi brahmaviṣṇuśivodbhavam amṛtaṃ tatra tatrāpi vajrīkaraṇam uttamam  k tasyotpattiṃ pravakṣyāmi yathā jānāti sādhakaḥ mahīṃ samuddhṛtavato varāhasya kalevarāt  k yaḥ svedaḥ patitastasmājjātaṃ śailodakaṃ param taṃ mukhe kṣaṇikaṃ jātaṃ karṇadeśe tu vāsaram  k bāhubhyāṃ tryahavedhī syānmāsavedhī tu pārśvayoḥ ṣaṇmāsamaparāṅge ca sarvaṃ samaphalaṃ ca tat  k aghorāstreṇa tatkṣetre rakṣāṃ kṛtvā diśāṃ balim dattvā lakṣaṃ japitvā tu gṛhṇīyādamṛtaṃ param  k śaradgrīṣmavasanteṣu hemante vā surārcite āyase tāmrapātre vā kāntalohamayethavā  k śilāmbupalamaṣṭau tu palaṃ kṣīrasya nikṣipet kṣīrāvaśeṣaṃ saṃkvāthyaṃ trisaptāhaṃ pibennaraḥ  k jīvedvarṣasahasraṃ tu valīpalitavarjitaḥ athavāṣṭapalaṃ kṣīraṃ palaikenāmbumiśritam  k kṣīrāvaśeṣaṃ seveta pūrvoktaṃ labhate phalam kulutthāṣṭaguṇaṃ vāri pacedaṣṭāvaśeṣitam  k caturguṇena tenājyaṃ pācayed ghṛtaśeṣitam lihyānmadhusitopetaṃ trisaptāhādbṛhaspatiḥ  k dviraṣṭavārṣikākāraḥ sahasrāyur na saṃśayaḥ avaśiṣṭakulutthaṃ tu pādāṃśamadhusarpiṣā  k bhakṣayetkarṣamekaṃ tu māsenāyutajīvitaḥ tatsiddhatailenābhyaṅgaṃ mrakṣaṇaṃ caiva kārayet  k pāmāvicarcikādadrukuṣṭhāni sahasā jayet valīpalitanirmuktaḥ sahasrāyuśca jāyate  k yaḥ pibetprātarutthāya śailāmbu culukaṃ payaḥ ṣaṇmāsāt syāt sahasrāyur nirvalīpalitaśca saḥ  k athavā sūtakaṃ devi vāriṇā saha mardayet māsenaikena deveśi naṣṭapiṣṭirbhaviṣyati  k māsamātraṃ samaśnīyātsa bhavedajarāmaraḥ athavā taṃ rasaṃ hemnā dhāmayetkhadirāgninā  k gulikā sundarī nāma sarvāyudhanivāriṇī kartā hartā svayaṃ siddho jīveccandrārkatārakam  k atha tenodakenaiva kṣīrārdhaṃ pāyasaṃ pacet māsamātraprayogeṇa valīpalitavarjitaḥ  k paktvā tenāmbhasā pathyāḥ ṣaṣṭistrīṇi śatāni ca madhu saṃyojya bhāṇḍasthaṃ bhūmau sarvaṃ nidhāpayet  k dine dine tadekaikaṃ bhakṣayetprātar utthitaḥ valīpalitanirmukto jīvedvarṣasahasrakam  k śailībhūtaṃ kulutthaṃ vā bhakṣayenmadhusarpiṣā ṣaṇmāsāttu prayogeṇa jīvedvarṣasahasrakam  k kūṣmāṇḍamāditaḥ kṛtvā yāni kāni phalāni ca jale kṣiptāni lohāni śailabhūtāni bhakṣayet  k kṣīrāhāraśca jīrṇānte vajrakāyo bhavennaraḥ tenodakena saṃmardyam abhrakaṃ kvāthayetpriye  k kaṭutrayayutaṃ khādejjīvedvarṣasahasrakam athavā rasakarṣaikaṃ tajjalena tu marditam  k iṅgudīphalamadhyasthaṃ tacchailodakamadhyagaḥ kālena triguṇenaiva kāṭhinyaṃ tasya jāyate  k ṣaṇmāsaṃ tanmukhe dhāryaṃ vajrakāyaṃ karoti tat daśanāgasamaprāṇo devaiḥ saha sa modate  k gṛhītvā triphalāṃ tatra śailavāriṇi nikṣipet yadā bhavati tacchailaṃ gṛhītvā cūrṇayettataḥ  k kāntajīrṇarasaṃ tena sārdhaṃ ghṛtamadhuplutam bhakṣayedvarṣamekaṃ tu tataḥ kṣīrāśano bhavet  k udayādityasaṅkāśo medhāvī priyadarśanaḥ nīlakuñcitakeśaśca jīveccandrārkatārakam  k pāradaṃ haritālaṃ ca śilāṃ mākṣikameva ca daradaṃ ca viṣaṃ caiva sarvamekatra kārayet  k mardayet khalvapāṣāṇe mātuluṅgarasena tu golakaṃ kārayitvā tu vārimadhye vinikṣipet  k tena tāraṃ ca śulbaṃ ca kāṃcanaṃ bhavati dhruvam upayuñjīta māsaikaṃ valīpalitavarjitaḥ  k sahasraṃ jīvitaṃ tasya mahābalaparākramaḥ śailībhūtaharidrāṃ tu taccūrṇāvāpamātrataḥ  k hematvaṃ labhate nāgo bālārkasadṛśaprabhaḥ śailodake vinikṣipya bhūśaile kardamepi vā  k jñātvā kālapramāṇena bandhayetpāradaṃ tataḥ raktakṣārayutaṃ dhmātaṃ suvarṇasamasāritam  k śatāṃśena tu lohānāṃ sarveṣāṃ hemakārakam dvitīyasāraṇāṃ prāpya sahasrāṃśena vidhyati  k taṃ khoṭaṃ dhārayedvaktre divyatvaṃ labhate dhruvam kecana ghuṭikāyogāḥnicule kakubhe caiva kiṃśuke madhukepi vā  k iṅgudīphalamadhye vā rajanīdvayamārdrake amṛte kandake vātha uktakandauṣadhīṣu ca  k vidhāya koṭaraṃ tatra kṣiptvā tenaiva ḍolayet triphalāvyoṣakalkena veṣṭayitvā prayatnataḥ  k pādena kanakaṃ dattvā pāradaṃ tatra yojayet śailodake kṣipettatra gulikā vajravadbhavet  k pūrvavatsāraṇā kāryā pūrvavatsiddhidā bhavet dhāryamāṇā mukhe sā tu sahasrāyuṣkarī bhavet  k dvitīyasāraṇāyogādayutaṃ vedhayettu sā dhāryamāṇā mukhe saivamayutāyuṣyadā bhavet  k tṛtīyasāraṇāyogājjāyate lakṣavedhinī taṃ khoṭaṃ dhārayedvaktre lakṣāyurjāyate naraḥ  k caturthī sāraṇā devi koṭivedhī na saṃśayaḥ koṭyāyurjīvitaṃ tasya khecaratvaṃ ca labhyate  k pañcabhirdaśakoṭiḥ syātṣaḍbhiḥ koṭiśataṃ bhavet yāvaccandrārkajīvitvam anantabalavīryavān  k dadāti saptamī cāpi sāraṇā gulikā parā khecarī nāma vikhyātā bhairaveṇa pracoditā  k yastu tadrājikāmātraṃ māsamekaṃ tu bhakṣayet vajradehaḥ sa siddhaḥ syād divyastrījanavallabhaḥ  k krīḍate khecarair bhogaiḥ svecchayā śivatāṃ vrajet nānāvidhaphalāścāsyā ghuṭikāṃ śṛṇu sundari  k śuddhabaddhaṃ rasendraṃ tu gandhakaṃ tatra jārayet triguṇe gandhake jīrṇe tena hema tu kārayet  k kārayedbhasma sūtaṃ tu kāñcanaṃ tena sūtakam tadbhasma sūtake jāryaṃ rasendrasya same samam  k tena sūtakajīrṇena vajraratnaṃ tu ghātayet tadvajraṃ jāyate bhasma sindūrāruṇasannibham  k tadbhasma jārayetsūte triguṇe tu surārcite hāṭakaṃ sārayettaṃ tu ghuṭikāṃ tena kārayet  k trilohāveṣṭitaṃ taṃ tu mukhe prakṣipya sādhakaḥ naṣṭacchāyo bhavetsoyamadṛśyo devadānavaiḥ  k lakṣavarṣasahasrāṇi nirvalīpalito bhavet śūlinaṃ śaktisaṃyuktaṃ ratnādiguṇabhūṣitam  k vaktre kare ca bibhṛyātsarvāyudhanivāraṇam vyoma mākṣikasatvaṃ ca tāraṃ tāmraṃ surāyudham  k sāralohaṃ sūtakaṃ ca ratnādiguṇabhūṣitam ghuṭikā sā varārohe madhuratrayasaṃyutā  k vaktrasthā nāśayetsākṣātpalitaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ śivaḥ śaktiśca deveśi ratnāni sitagonasā  k hema tāraṃ tathā bhānuḥ samabhāgāni kārayet strīrajo vyāghramadhyasthaṃ padmasūtreṇa veṣṭayet  k sitayena tathā veṣṭyaṃ guhyasthāne niveśayet raṇe rājakule dyūte divye kāme jayo bhavet  k vaikrāntābhrakakāntaṃ tu sasyakaṃ tu surāyudham vibhītakādisambhūtakāṃjikasya samaṃ bhavet  k samāvartya tataḥ sūte yojayetpādayogataḥ kumārīrasasaṃghṛṣṭā kṛtaiṣā ghuṭikā śubhā  k rogamṛtyujarā hanti vaktrasthā nātra saṃśayaḥ pañca tāraṃ varārohe sūtakadvayameva ca  k trayo gaganabhāgāḥ syurekaikaṃ hemakāntayoḥ ardhaṃ śulbaṃ vibhāgena gulikāmarasundarī  k akṣayo hyajaraścaiva bhavettena mahābalaḥ bhasma sūtapalaikaṃ ca mṛtakāntapalaṃ tathā  k mākṣikasya palaṃ caiva śilājatu palaṃ tathā palamekaṃ viḍaṅgasya pathyācūrṇapalaṃ tathā  k ekīkṛtya tu tatsarvaṃ madhvājyena tu peṣayet gulikāḥ kārayettena ṣaṣṭyādhikaśatatrayam  k ekaikāṃ bhakṣayennityaṃ varṣamekaṃ nirantaram jīvedvarṣaśatāyuḥ sa yathā rudro mahābalaḥ  k kecana rasāyanakalpāḥataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rasabhasmarasāyanam vijñeyaṃ niṣparihāraṃ sākṣāddivyauṣadhaṃ param  k āmalakyādi kāntaṃ ca pāradaṃ ca manaḥśilām vākucīsamabhāgāni kṣīriṇīrasapeṣitam  k meghanādarasopetaṃ mūkamūṣāgataṃ pacet māṣaṃ dvimāṣaṃ triguṇaṃ bhakṣayettatkrameṇa tu  k varṣatrayaṃ paraṃ devi pādaniṣkārdhakaṃ kramāt ṣaṭ saptāṣṭau ca varṣāṇi kramānniṣkapramāṇataḥ  k bhuñjīta sa ca divyānnaṃ jarāvairūpyavarjitaḥ kiṃcit kāñcanasaṃyuktaṃ niṣkaṃ niṣkārdhameva vā  k yo bhakṣayet tribhir varṣaiḥ sarvavyādhīñjayatyayam aṣṭavarṣasahasrāyurdvādaśe lakṣavedhakaḥ  k ṣoḍaśe vatsare devi divyarūpaḥ sa jāyate uttamo mūlabandhastu madhyamaṃ sārabandhanam  k adhamaḥ pākabandhastu evaṃ trividhabandhanam śatapalamabhayānām akṣadhātryostathaiva kvathitajalasamāṣṭau bhāgamaṣṭāvaśiṣṭam ghṛtamadhusitayāḍhyaṃ vyoṣacitraṃ daśaiva rasapaladaśasiddhaṃ lohajīrṇaṃ mṛtaṃ ca  k giriyutasamam abhraṃ kāntabhṛṅgaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ rasasahitavibhāvyaṃ taṇḍulair bilvamajjaiḥ himakarakṛtakalkaṃ lohapātrasthamāsaṃ tridinatanuviśuddhaṃ kalkamenaṃ variṣṭham  k lihati śayanakāle vāmanetrārdhasevī ghananibiḍasamādhir mattamātaṅgadarpaḥ vigatasakaladoṣaḥ sarvadṛk divyacakṣuḥ madana iva sukāntiḥ kāminīnāṃ pravīraḥ  k jalada iva vapuṣmānkuñcitāgrāgrakeśaḥ turaga iva viśuddhaḥ satkaviścitrakārī vṛṣabhagativiceṣṭo mandagambhīraghoṣaḥ suragaja iva loke candratārārkajīvī  k kāntahemaravicandram abhrakair golakaṃ nihitamiṅgudīphale śailavārivarisiddhagolakaṃ sundarī hyamarasaṃjñikā śubhā  k kāntahemaravicandram abhrakaṃ vajraratnarasamahirājagolakam kṣiptam āmalakakāṣṭhakodare bhūmiśailanihitaṃ samuddhṛtam  k śailatāṃ gatamathāhitaṃ mukhe vajrakāyakarakalpavāsaraiḥ tārahemavaraśulbasūtakairgolakaṃ varaṇakāṣṭhayantritam  k śailavārikṛtasundarīrasaiḥ khecarīti gulikā nigadyate  k śailāmbunikṣiptapalāśabījaṃ śailīkṛtaṃ kṣaudraghṛtena khādet trisaptarātraṃ dinamekamekaṃ sahasrajīvī vidito naraḥ syāt  k sūtakaṃ cābhrakaṃ caiva vajratīkṣṇasamanvitam hāṭakena samāyuktaṃ gulikā khecarī bhavet  k karañjaphalamadhyasthaṃ sūtaṃ tatraiva nikṣipet dhṛtaḥ śailāmbumadhyasthaḥ sahasrāyuḥ prayacchati  k tinduke dvisahasrāyur jambīre trisahasrakam mātuluṃge ca nāraṅge catuḥpañcasahasrakam  k rambhāphale ṣaṭsahasraṃ panase saptasaṃkhyakam vibhītakaphale caiva daśasāhasrasaṃkhyakam  k nālikere mahābhāge sahasrāṇi caturdaśa triṃśatsahasraṃ pathyāyāṃ lakṣamāmalake punaḥ  k abhrapatrabhavāt kvāthād ahorātraṃ śilodake badhnāti coddhṛtaṃ sūtaṃ mṛtyudāridryanāśanam  k sāraṇākramayogena vajravajjāyate vapuḥ rase rasāyane caiva lakṣavedhī na saṃśayaḥ  k kardamaṃ tu kumāryāśca rasena kṛtapiṇḍikam dhamanātpatate sattvaṃ mukhasthaṃ dhārayennaraḥ  k ṣaṇmāsopaprayogeṇa hyajarāmaratāṃ vrajet srotoñjanayutaṃ dhmātaṃ sattvaṃ pāradamiśritam  k tatkhoṭaṃ dhārayedvaktre hyadṛśyo bhavati dhruvam yasya yo vidhirāmnāta udakasya śivāgame  k śatena bata kālena kuryāddehe rasāyanam baddhajāraṇavidhiḥyā pūrvā nirmitā seyamadhamā bālajāraṇā  k uttamā durlabhā caiva śrūyatāṃ baddhajāraṇā abaddhaṃ jārayedyastu kṣīyamāṇaḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet  k baddhasya jīryate grāso jīrṇasya ca mukhaṃ bhavet samukho durmukhaṃ datte sāmānyottamalakṣaṇam  k bandhaprakārāḥsāmānyo gnisahatvena mahāratnādijārakaḥ sāmānyaḥ prathamaḥ kāryaḥ sagrāsastu samantataḥ  k vasudehakaro devi sāmānyo hi bhavedayam grāsahīnastu yo baddho divyasiddhikaro bhavet  k uttamo mūlabandhastu madhyamaṃ sārabandhanam adhamaḥ pākabandhastu evaṃ trividhabandhanam  k mūlabandhastu yo bandho mūlasaṃkucitaṃ mahat sārabandhastu yo bandho vāsanābandha ucyate  k syāccatuḥ ṣaṣṭimūlebhyaḥ kiṃcinmūlena bandhanam prāṇyaṅgaṃ daityādīnāṃ mūlāṅgaṃ devatāmayam  k pāṣāṇaṃ caiva siddhānāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca pūjitam pīṭhikādrutisaṃkocais trividhaṃ bandhanaṃ bhavet  k divyābhirauṣadhībhiḥ prāguktaṃ saṃkocabandhanam drutibhirbadhyate sūtaḥ kṣaṇabandha udāhṛtaḥ  k abhrakaṃ harabījaṃ ca ṣoḍaśāṃśena kāñcanam dhmātaṃ prakāśamūṣāyāṃ śodhayetkācaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ  k dakṣiṇāvartitaṃ dhmātaṃ harabījena melakam mūṣāṃ tyaktvā varārohe tiṣṭhate khagabaddhavadrasaḥ  k raktikārdhārdhamātreṇa parvatānapi vedhayet bhakṣaṇāttasya deveśi rudratulyo bhavennaraḥ  k krīḍate saptalokeṣu śivatulyaparākramaḥ drutimelanavidhiḥvajrakandaṃ guḍūcī ca uccaṭādisamanvitam  k abhrakaṃ kramate śīghramanyathā nāsti saṅgamaḥ kṛṣṇāgarunābhisitaiḥ rasonapitarāmaṭhaiḥ  k nārīkusumapālāśabījatailasamanvitaiḥ soṣṇairmilanti mṛditā drutayaḥ sakalā rase  k vajrabandhaḥdaśasaṅkalikāvidhisiddhaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vajrabandhaṃ surārcite gandhakaṃ bhakṣayennārī dinānāmekaviṃśatim  k tadrajo rasarājasya bandhane jāraṇe hitam vajrabhasma tu bhāgaikaṃ bhāgāḥ śuddharasāttrayaḥ  k dvipadīrajasā mardyaṃ yāvattatkalkatāṃ gatam pādāṃśena suvarṇena pattralepaṃ tu kārayet  k somavallīrasaṃ kāntaṃ ṭaṅkaṇālaṃ sucūrṇitam dadyāttamaṣṭamāṃśena mardayecca prayatnataḥ  k naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ ca śuṣkaṃ tadandhayitvā puṭe tataḥ andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ krāmaṇena samanvitam  k khoṭastu jāyate devi śatavedhī mahārasaḥ sauvīraṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kācaṃ dattvā dattvā viśodhayet  k akṣīṇo milate hemnā samāvartaśca jāyate ekottarakrame vṛddhyā saṃkalaiḥ krāmayettataḥ  k ekaguṇena sūtena ekā saṅkalikocyate triguṇena tu sūtena dvitīyā saṃkalocyate  k ṣaḍguṇena tu sūtena tṛtīyā saṅkalī bhavet daśaguṇena sūtena caturthī saṅkalī bhavet  k pañcādaśaguṇeneśi pañcamī saṅkalī bhavet ekaviṃśadguṇeneśi ṣaṣṭhī saṅkalikā bhavet  k aṣṭāviṃśadguṇeneśi saptamī saṅkalī smṛtā ṣaṭtriṃśadguṇite baddhā bhavetsaṅkalikāṣṭamī  k pañcacatvāriṃśaguṇe saṅkalī navamī matā pañcādhyadhikapañcāśad daśasaṅkalikā smṛtā  k evaṃ ca kramavṛddhyā tu saṃkalī daśabandhitā prathame daśavedhī ca śatavedhī dvitīyake  k tṛtīye sahasravedhī syāccaturtheyutavedhikaḥ pañcame lakṣavedhī syād daśalakṣaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhake  k saptame koṭivedhī syāddaśakoṭiṃ tathāṣṭame dhūmavedhī tu navame daśame śabdavedhakaḥ  k saṃkalaiḥ sakalairbaddhe vedho daśaguṇo bhavet daśasaṃkalikābaddhaḥ śabdavedhī mahārasaḥ  k yathā lohe tathā dehe krāmate nātra saṃśayaḥ vedhayettatpramāṇena dhātūṃścaiva śarīrakam  k kārayedghuṭikāṃ divyāṃ badarāsthipramāṇataḥ mahākālīṃ pūjayitvā dhārayetsatataṃ budhaḥ  k oṃ aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ kāli kāli mahākāli māṃsaśoṇitabhojani hrāṃ hrīṃ hraṃ rakṣa kṛṣṇamukhi devi rasasiddhiṃ dadasva me śrīṃ hrīṃ aiṃ  k pūjayitvā tato devīṃ siddhacakraṃ viśeṣataḥ tāṃ kṣipeccakramadhye tu ghuṭikāṃ divyarūpiṇīm  k śatavedhena yā baddhā rasena ghuṭikā priye māsamekaṃ tu vaktrasthā jīveccaiva yathā vidhiḥ  k tathā sahasravedhena baddhā yā ghuṭikā śubhā māsadvayaṃ tu vaktrasthā jīveccandrārkatārakam  k daśasahasravedhena baddhā yā ghuṭikā yadi śakratulyaṃ tadāyuṣyaṃ tribhirmāsaistu jāyate  k lakṣavedhena yā baddhā ghuṭikā divyarūpiṇī caturmāsaṃ tu vaktrasthā brahmāyuṣyaṃ prayacchati  k daśalakṣeṇa yā baddhā ghuṭikā divyarūpiṇī saptamāsaṃ tu vaktrasthā vaiṣṇavaṃ labhate phalam  k koṭivedhena yā baddhā ghuṭikā divyarūpiṇī ṣaṇmāsasaṃsthitā vaktre sākṣādvai rudratāṃ nayet  k daśakoṭiprabhedena ghuṭikā divyarūpiṇī saptamāsaṃ tu vaktrasthā sa bhavedvyāpako naraḥ  k kartā hartā svayaṃ bhoktā śāpānugrahakārakaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvakartā ca sūkṣmarūpo nirañjanaḥ  k icchayā kurute sṛṣṭimicchayā saṃharejjagat svacchandagamano bhūtvā śivarūpo bhavennaraḥ  k pūjyate sarvadevaiśca brahmaviṣṇumaheśvaraiḥ anyo vajrabandhaḥpunaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vajrabandhaṃ sudurlabham  k samāṃśabhakṣaṇaṃ hema śuddhasūtena kārayet mṛtavajraṃ kalāṃśena mardayed dvipadīrasaiḥ  k prāgvaccheṣaṃ kriyājātaṃ pūrvavacca phalaṃ bhavet vajrabandho bhavetsiddho devadānavadurjayaḥ  k caturviṃśatisiddhānāṃ nāyakaḥ sarvasiddhimān anyo vajrabandhaḥvajracūrṇasamaṃ sūtaṃ haṃsapādyā vimarditam  k puṭitvā mārayettatra punastulyaṃ rasaṃ kṣipet dhmātaḥ khoṭo bhavatyāśu śodhitaḥ kācaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ  k yāvacchukrodayaprakhyo jāyate ca rasaḥ priye anyo vajrabandhaḥvajrasattvaṃ ca gaganaṃ rasaṃ hema ca melayet  k amaratvamavāpnoti vaktrasthena surādhipe jārayitvā rasaṃ taddhi punastenaiva jārayet  k koṭivedhī na sandeho vaktrasthaṃ khecaraṃ param vedhayettatpramāṇena dhātūṃścaiva śarīrakam  k kārayedghuṭikāṃ divyāṃ vajrasiddhena kāñcane anena kramayogena yāvacchakyaṃ tu mārayet  k tadbhasma sūtakaṃ devi sarvaroganibarhaṇam hemnā ca sārayitvā tu candrārkaṃ lepayettataḥ  k dvātriṃśāṃśena hemārdhaṃ mātṛkāryadhikaṃ bhavet badarāsthipramāṇena kārayedgulikāṃ budhaḥ  k yathā lohe tathā dehe kramate nānyathā kvacit anyo vajrabandhaḥvajreṇa dvaṃdvitaṃ hema kāntaśulbakapālinā  k rañjayetsaptavārāṇi taṃ khoṭaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇitam bhāvitaṃ strīrajenaiva bhūrjapatre niveśitam  k drutasūtena saṃyuktaṃ baddhvā vastreṇa poṭṭalīm svedayeddevadeveśi yāvadbhavati golakaḥ  k lāṅgalī jīvanī caiva gandhāryuttaravāruṇī eteṣāṃ nikṣipetpiṇḍe vajragolaṃ tu veṣṭayet  k mūṣāmadhye vinikṣipya saṃdhayitvā prayatnataḥ bhūmau mūṣāṃ vinikṣipya puṭaṃ mūrdhni pradāpayet  k anenaiva pratāpena bandhameti mahārasaḥ golakaṃ dhārayedvaktre varṣamekaṃ yadā priye  k jīvetkalpasahasrāṇi yathā nāgo mahābalaḥ varṣairdvādaśabhiḥ sākṣājjāyate rasapūruṣaḥ  k gātrasya tasya prasvedādaṣṭau lohāstu kāñcanam vajrabhasma tathā sūtaṃ kāñcanena samanvitam  k vaktrasthaṃ kurute yastu abdātpalitavarjitaḥ anye vedhopayogino bandhāḥkṛṣṇābhrakasya satvaṃ ca tāraṃ tāmraṃ ca hāṭakam  k mākṣikaṃ kāntatīkṣṇaṃ ca samabhāgāni kārayet andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k taṃ khoṭaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu drutasūtena golayet mṛtasattvasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgāścatvāri golakam  k mardayettaptakhalvena bhasmībhavati sūtakaḥ mārayedbhūdhare yantre saptasaṅkalikākramāt  k guñjāmātraṃ tu tadbhasma madhvājyena tu lehayet saṃvatsaraprayogeṇa hyayutāyurbhavennaraḥ  k valīpalitanirmukto mahābalaparākramaḥ tadbhasma palamekaṃ tu palaikaṃ gandhakasya ca  k andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ bhavati tatkṣaṇāt jīvetkalpasahasrāṇi yathā nāgo mahābalaḥ  k tasya mūtrapurīṣeṇa lohānyaṣṭau ca kāñcanam tatkhoṭaṃ rañjayet paścād vaṅgābhrakakapālinā  k rañjayetsaptavārāṇi bhavetkuṅkumasannibhaḥ hemnā saha samāvartya sāraṇātrayasāritam  k śatāṃśena tu tenaiva śulbamadhye pradāpayet jāyate kanakaṃ divyaṃ devābharaṇabhūṣaṇam  k baddhasūtasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgaikaṃ kuṭilasya ca andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ yāvadvaṅgāvaśeṣitam  k anena kramayogena vaṅgaṃ nirvāhya ṣaḍguṇam anena kramayogena vahannāgaṃ ca ṣaḍguṇam  k tatastaṃ rañjayetpaścāttīkṣṇaśulbakapālinā pakvasūtasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgaikaṃ drutasūtakam  k mardayenmadhyamāmlena golakaṃ bhavati kṣaṇāt mṛtavajrasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgāścatvāri golakam  k mardayet taptakhalvena bhasmībhavati sūtakaḥ mārayedbhūdhare yantre saptasaṃkalikākramāt  k tadbhasma tu punaḥ paścānmadhyamāmlena mardayet puṭaṃ dadyātprayatnena ṣaṣṭyādhikaśatatrayam  k tadbhasma jāyate divyaṃ sindūrāruṇasannibham tenaiva vedhayettāraṃ sahasrāṃśena kāñcanam  k mṛtavajrasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgāḥ ṣoḍaśa sūtakam devadālīśaṅkhapuṣpīrasena mṛditaṃ kramāt  k mārayedbhūdhare yantre bhasmībhavati tatkṣaṇāt pūtkārāṇāṃ sahasreṇa dhāmyamānaṃ na gacchati  k īdṛśaṃ bhasma sūtaṃ ca dehe lohe ca yojayet tadbhasma palamekaṃ tu palamekaṃ ca gandhakam  k andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ bhavati tatkṣaṇāt taṃ khoṭaṃ rañjayet paścāt kapālikramayogataḥ  k sāraṇātrayayogena śulbavedhaṃ pradāpayet bhasmasūtapalaikaṃ ca palaikaṃ pannagasya ca  k kāntapātreṇa taṃ kṛtvā mardayellohamuṣṭinā mṛdvagninā tataḥ pācyaṃ yāvannāgena melakam  k puṭena jāyate bhasma sindūrāruṇasaprabham tadbhasma tu punaḥ paścādgopittena tu mardayet  k taccaturdaśavārāṃstu puṭayedbhasmayettataḥ tadbhasma bhāgamekaṃ tu bhāgaikaṃ hemagolakam  k ekīkṛtyātha saṃmardya krāmaṇena sahaikataḥ tārapiṣṭaṃ tu tenaiva sahasrāṃśena kāñcanam  k anena kramayogena vaṅgabhasma prajāyate sahasrāṃśena tenaiva śulbavedhaṃ pradāpayet  k tacchulbaṃ jāyate tāraṃ śaṅkhakundendusannibham śvetābhrakaṃ ca sattvaṃ ca kāṅkṣī kāntaṃ tathāyasam  k vaṅgaṃ kāntaṃ tāraṃ tathā śvetaṃ vaikrāntaṃ ca kadambakam andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ kundendusannibham  k taṃ khoṭaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu drutasūtena golakam mṛtavajrasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgāścatvāri golakaḥ  k mardayettaptakhalvena bhasmībhavati sūtakaḥ mārayedbhūdhare yantre saptasaṅkalikākramāt  k tataśca jāyate bhasma śaṅkhakundendusannibham tadbhasma palamekaṃ tu palamekaṃ tu gandhakam  k andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ bhavati tadrasaḥ tāreṇa ca samāvartya sāraṇātrayasāritam  k sahasrāṃśena tenaiva śulbavedhaṃ pradāpayet tīkṣṇacūrṇapalānyaṣṭau palāṣṭau drutasūtakam  k mardayettaptakhalvena ṭeṭañcilvīrasena ca tatkṣaṇājjāyate piṇḍaṃ tīkṣṇena saha golakam  k mṛtavajrasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgāścatvāri golakam mardayettaptakhalvena bhasmībhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k mārayedbhūdhare yantre saptasaṅkalikākramāt ṣoḍaśāṃśena tenaiva vaṅgavedhaṃ pradāpayet  k tadbhasma palamekaṃ tu palaikaṃ gandhakasya ca andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k tasya khoṭasya bhāgaṃ ca tīkṣṇacūrṇaṃ ca tatsamam dvau bhāgau drutasūtasya sarvamekatra mardayet  k bhasma vajrasyaiva prabhāvataḥ  k sāmudraṃ tripalaṃ devi bhasmamadhye pradāpayet ekīkṛtyātha saṃmardya vajrīkṣīre dinatrayam  k viśvāmitrakapālasthaṃ puṭaṃ dadyāttu bhūdhare tatsarvaṃ jāyate bhasma śaṅkhakundendusannibham  k tenaiva yavamātreṇa vaṅgaṃ stambhayati kṣaṇāt vaṅgaṃ tāraṃ tathā sattvaṃ samasūtena golakam  k anena kramayogena mārayecca pṛthak pṛthak tatsarvaṃ jāyate bhasma vajrasyaiva k vajrīkṣīreṇa saṃveṣṭya puṭaṃ dadyāccaturdaśa eṣa siddharasaḥ sākṣāddurlabhastridaśairapi  k vaṅgaṃ tu dāpayet paścādbhāṇḍe caiva tu mṛṇmaye siddhaṃ bhasma bhavellohaśalākena ca cālayet  k vāpayecca madhu guñjāṭaṅkaṇakācaṃ ca karkaṭāsthi snuhīpayaḥ  k tatsarvaṃ tu samaṃ yojyaṃ strīstanyena tu mardayet mūṣālepaḥ kṛtaḥ prājño vajramelāpakaḥ sukham  k haṭhāgnau vajramūṣābhirdṛḍhaṃ vajrā milanti ca śvetavaikrāntasiddhaḥśvetavaikrāntacūrṇaṃ tu hayamūtreṇa mardayet  k ādau susvinnamādāya pale palaśataṃ kṣipet tārasya jāyate bhasma viśuddhasphaṭikākṛti  k tadbhasma melayetsūte samabhāgaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ cārayedrajataṃ sūte hayamūtreṇa mardayet  k puṭayedandhamūṣāyāṃ krameṇa mṛduvahninā ahorātraṃ trirātraṃ vā bhavedagnisaho rasaḥ  k sparśanātsarvalohāni rajataṃ ca kariṣyati pañcamaḥ prakāraḥ raktavaikrāntasiddhaḥraktasya vakṣyate karma jarādāridryanāśanam  k saptadhā bhāvayettasya vyāghrīkandāṃbhasā rajaḥ palaṃ tasya palaṃ hemnaḥ palaṃ śuddharasasya ca  k śuddhabhasma bhavetsarvaṃ
