gandhakabandhaḥprathamaḥ prakāraḥśuddhasūtapalaikaṃ ca palaikaṃ gandhakasya ca  k ekīkṛtyātha saṃmardya dhuttūrakarasena ca mārayeccakrayogena bhasmībhavati sūtakaḥ  k andhamūṣāgato dhmātaḥ khoṭo bhavati śobhanaḥ sitaṃ hema ca nāgaṃ ca candrārkaṃ cāpi vedhayet  k dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥpalaikaṃ śuddhasūtasya karṣaikaṃ gandhakasya ca mardayetsnigdhakhalvena devadālīrasaplutam  k mardayettu karāṅgulyā gandhapiṣṭistu jāyate jambīrasya rasenaiva dinamekaṃ tu mardayet  k pañcadrāvakasaṃyuktāṃ vaṭikāṃ kārayecchubhām palāśamūlakalkena vaṭikāṃ tāṃ pralepayet  k dhamet khoṭo bhavecchvetakācaṭaṅkaṇayogataḥ śodhayettaṃ prayatnena yāvannirmalatāṃ vrajet  k sa khoṭo jāyate devi triguṇaṃ pannagaṃ tataḥ śataśo rañjayetpaścācchulbābhrakakapālinā  k śulbe tāre ca khoṭoyaṃ sahasrāṃśena vedhakaḥ tṛtīyaḥ prakāraḥgandhakena hate sūte mṛtalohāni vāhayet  k punarhema samāvartya samāṃśaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ kuru sāritaḥ śulbatārair ghoṣaṃ vidhyati sūtakaḥ  k caturthaḥ prakāraḥrasaṃ hemasamaṃ kṛtvā piṣṭikārdhena gandhakam dvipadīrajasā yuktaṃ mardayeṭṭaṅkaṇānvitam  k naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ ca śuṣkaṃ ca dhmātaḥ khoṭo bhavettataḥ candrārkaṣoḍaśāṃśena viddhaṃ bhavati kāñcanam  k hemārdhamilitaṃ taṃ tu mātṛkāsamatāṃ vrajet kuryātsaṅkalikāyogādvedho daśaguṇottaraḥ  k yathā hemni tathā tāre vyāṭibījena yojitam tṛtīyasaṅkalābaddhaṃ ṣaṭśate nāgavedhakam  k caturguṇena tenaiva sahasrāṃśena kāñcanam anena kramayogena sapta saṅkalikā yadi  k kurute kāñcanaṃ divyamaṣṭalohāni pārvati taṃ punaścūrṇayitvā tu puṭayedbhasma jāyate  k sarvavyādhijayo devi palaikena subhakṣite dvipale brāhmamāyuṣyaṃ tripale vaiṣṇavaṃ bhavet  k catuṣpale ca pañcatvamīśaḥ pañcapale bhavet ṣaṭpale bhakṣite devi sadāśivatanurbhavet  k pañcamaḥ prakāraḥsūtakaṃ gandhakaṃ tāraṃ meṣavallīvasā samā tridinaṃ mardayellakṣaṃ vaṅgaṃ pādena lepayet  k andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ vaṅgaṃ stambhayati kṣaṇāt ṣaṣṭhaḥ prakāraḥgandhapiṣṭividhiḥcūrṇitaṃ gandhakaṃ devi markaṭīrasabhāvitam  k bhāvayecchatavārāṇi jīvabhasma tu gacchati dāpayenmṛṇmaye pātre rasena saha saṃyutam  k tāpayedravitāpena markaṭīrasasaṃyutam gandhakaṃ grasate sūtaḥ piṣṭikā bhavati kṣaṇāt  k tilaparṇīrasenaiva gandhakaṃ bhāvayettataḥ saptavārāṃstu deveśi chāyāśuṣkaṃ punaḥpunaḥ  k śodhitaṃ pātitaṃ sūtaṃ palaikapramitaṃ priye mūṣāmadhye vinikṣipya narendrīrasasaṃyutam  k jārayedvālukāyantre bhāvitaṃ gandhakaṃ punaḥ truṭi truṭi pradātavyaṃ gandhakaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ  k anena kramayogena jāyate gandhapiṣṭikā gandhapāṣāṇacūrṇaṃ tu kanakasya rasena tu  k bhāvayetsaptavārāṃstu strīrajena tu saptadhā śuddhasūtapalaikaṃ ca kharpare dāpayettataḥ  k bhāvitaṃ gandhakaṃ dadyānnarapittena saṃyutam dolayed ravitāpena piṣṭikā bhavati kṣaṇāt  k gandhakaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu caṇakāmlena pārvati bhāvayetsaptavārāṇi strīpuṣpeṇa ca saptadhā  k drutasūtakamadhye tu karpūraṃ gandhakaṃ rasam dāpayennikṣiped goṣṭhe saptāhād gandhapiṣṭikā  k gandhakapiṣṭīstaṃbhanaṃ vedhaścakaṭukośātakībījaṃ cāṇḍālīkandameva ca stanyakṣīreṇa saṃpeṣya piṣṭikāṃ tena lepayet  k puṭayedbhūdhare yantre stambhate nātra saṃśayaḥ hemasampuṭamadhye tu samāvartaṃ tu kārayet  k aṣṭamāṃśena tenaiva nāgavedhaṃ pradāpayet ṣoḍaśāṃśena tenaiva tāravedhaṃ pradāpayet  k saptamaḥ prakāraḥgandhapiṣṭipalaikaṃ tu nāgapiṣṭipalāṣṭakam lepayennāgapatrāṇi chāyāyāṃ śoṣayettataḥ  k āṭarūṣakapiṇḍena nāgapatrāṇi lepayet āraṇyotpalakairdevi dāpayecca puṭatrayam  k tannāgaṃ mriyate divyaṃ sindūrāruṇasaprabham tannāgaṃ palamekaṃ tu śulbacūrṇapalāṣṭakam  k vāsakasya rasenaiva praharaikaṃ tu mardayet mārayetpātanāyantre śulbaṃ tanmriyate kṣaṇāt  k ṣoḍaśāṃśena tenaiva tāravedhaṃ pradāpayet jāyate kanakaṃ divyaṃ devābharaṇabhūṣaṇam  k yā kācidgandhapiṣṭī tu ādau nāgaṃ tu mārayet nāgena vedhayecchulbaṃ śulbe tāraṃ tu vedhayet  k kanakaṃ jāyate divyaṃ siddhayoga udāhṛtaḥ aṣṭamaḥ prakāraḥgandhakaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ harabījena marditam  k bhūmisthaṃ māsamekaṃ tu tāramāyāti kāñcanam udvartanena tenaiva sarvakuṣṭhavināśanam  k ghanena saha saṃyuktaṃ vraṇarogavināśanam saṃvatsaraprayogeṇa sahasrāyurbhavennaraḥ  k tālakabandhaḥśuddhasūtapalaikaṃ tu palaikaṃ tālakasya ca ekīkṛtyātha saṃmardya unmattakarasena ca  k mārayeccakrayantreṇa bhasmībhavati sūtakaḥ andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭo bhavati śobhanaḥ  k vaṅgaṃ tāraṃ ca śulbaṃ ca kramaśo vedhayedrasaḥ śuddhavaṅgapalaikaṃ ca palaikaṃ sūtakasya ca  k dve pale tālakaṃ caitad unmattarasamarditam mārayetpātanāyantre dhamanātkhoṭatāṃ nayet  k śvetābhrakasya sattvaṃ ca tāraṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca mākṣikam andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k tatkhoṭapalamekaṃ ca palaikaṃ sūtakasya ca tālakasya palaṃ sarvamekīkṛtyātha mardayet  k mārayetpātanāyantre dhamanāt khoṭatāṃ nayet anye laghubandhāḥśuddhasūtapalaikaṃ ca palaikaṃ pannagasya ca  k paladvayaṃ kunaṭyāśca sarvamekatra mardayet mārayetpātanāyantre dhamanāt khoṭatāṃ nayet  k hemapiṣṭipalaikaṃ ca palaikaṃ gandhakasya tu ekīkṛtyātha saṃmardya dhuttūrakarasena ca  k mārayetpātanāyantre dhamanāt khoṭatāṃ nayet kṛṣṇābhrakasya satvaṃ ca kāntaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca hāṭakam  k śuddhaṃ tāraṃ ca mākṣīkaṃ samabhāgāni kārayet andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k tatkhoṭapalamekaṃ tu palaikaṃ sūtakasya ca paladvayaṃ kunaṭyāśca sarvamekatra mardayet  k mārayetpātanāyantre dhamanāt khoṭatāṃ nayet kṛṣṇābhrakapalaikaṃ tu rasakasya palaṃ tathā  k sūtakasya palaikaṃ tu sarvamekīkṛtaṃ priye unmattakarasenaiva mardayetpraharadvayam  k mardayeddinamekaṃ vā ṭaṅkaṇena samanvitam ghuṭikāṃ kārayetpaścācchāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet  k mahāvartigataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭaṃ bhavati sūtakaḥ taṃ khoṭaṃ śodhayetkācaṭaṅkaṇadravayogataḥ  k hemnā saha samāvartya sāraṇātrayasāritam sahasrāṃśena tenaiva śulbavedhaṃ pradāpayet  k anena kramayogena koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ bījadvayaṃ palāśasya palamekaṃ tu sūtakam  k jambīrāmlena saṃmardya chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet tumbīkā meghanādī ca kākajaṅghā ca bhūlikā  k stanyaṃ ca taiḥ praliptāyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ caiva nikṣipet dhamayetkhadirāṅgāraiḥ khoṭo bhavati cākṣayaḥ  k palāśataile saṃmardyaṃ yāvat syād dravapiṣṭikā andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt  k pūrvaśuddhena sūtena samahemnā ca pārvati golakaṃ kārayettena mardayitvā dṛḍhaṃ kṛtam  k brahmavṛkṣasya bījāni kārpāsāsthi vibhītakam yavaciñcā ca vandhyā ca rājikā ca samanvitam  k sūkṣmapiṇḍīkṛtaṃ sarvaṃ tena liptvā tu golakam puṭanaiḥ saptabhir devi piṣṭikāstambhanaṃ bhavet  k bṛhatpuṭaṃ tato dattvā mūṣāyāṃ tu dhamettataḥ samāvartya tu taṃ sūtaṃ samahemnā niyojitam  k śatāṃśena tu candrārkaṃ vedhayet suravandite punastenaiva yogena piṣṭīstaṃbhaṃ tu kārayet  k sārayitvā tato hemnā vedhaścaiva sahasrakaḥ evaṃ lakṣāṇi koṭiṃ ca vedhayetkramayogataḥ  k saptasaṃkalikādūrdhvaṃ kṛtvā vaktraṃ tu golakam varṣeṇaikena sa bhavedvalīpalitavarjitaḥ  k cāṇḍālīrākṣasīpuṣpairatha madhvājyaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ mahārasāṣṭamadhye tamabhrakaṃ vāpi yojayet  k nāgavaṅgasamaṃ sūtaṃ hematāramathāpi vā abhrakaṃ drutisattvaṃ vā mardayetpraharadvayam  k chāyāśuṣkaṃ tato golaṃ mūkamūṣāgataṃ priye dattvā laghupuṭaṃ dhmātaḥ khoṭo bhavati śobhanaḥ  k raṃbhā vīrā snuhīkṣīraṃ kañcukī yavaciñcikā dīnārī caiva gorambhā mīnākṣī kākamācikā  k ebhirmarditasūtasya punarjanma na vidyate pūrvavat kramayogena khoṭo bhavati śobhanaḥ  k viṣṇukrāntā ca vakrāṅkābalā ca tulasī tathā mahāsomāhivallī ca sūryāvartaṃ ca sundari  k ebhistu marditaḥ sūtaḥ pūrvavatkhoṭatāṃ nayet snuhīkṣīraṃ ca kāñjīraṃ bījāni kanakasya ca  k kañcukī lāṅgalī cendravāruṇī viṣamuṣṭikā pālāśamūlatoyaṃ ca mardayettena sūtakam  k samahemni samaṃ sūtaṃ piṣṭikāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ mahārasānpiṣṭikārdhaṃ mardayed oṣadhīrasaiḥ  k yāmatrayaṃ mardayitvā golakaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ piṣṭikāṃ bandhayitvā tu gandhataile vipācayet  k andhamūṣāgataṃ golaṃ chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet tato laghupuṭaṃ dattvā khadirāgnau tu dhāmayet  k khoṭavajjāyate devi saha hemnā tu dhāmayet akṣīṇo milate hemni samāvartaśca jāyate  k tatkṣaṇādeva sūtasya divyadeho bhavennaraḥ vedhayetsarvalohāni rañjitaḥ krāmito rasaḥ  k samāṃśabhakṣaṇe sūte mardayedoṣadhīrasaiḥ naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā pūrvayogena dhāmayet  k khoṭastu jāyate divyaḥ ṣoḍaśāṃśena vedhakaḥ baddhaḥ saṅkalikāyogād vidhyed daśaguṇottaram  k athavā cūrṇabaddhastu vidhyeddaśaguṇottaram mṛgadūrvā candravallī pakvabimbā tathaiva ca  k kāṅkṣīlā karavīraṃ ca bījaṃ conmattakasya ca kākāṇḍīpalasaṃyuktaṃ mardayetsurasundari  k samahemni samaṃ sūtaṃ piṣṭikāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ athavā sārayitvā tu samena samasūtakam  k mahārasapiṣṭikāṃ ca mardayedoṣadhīrasaiḥ yāmatrayaṃ mardayitvā golakaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ  k andhamūṣāgataṃ golaṃ chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet tato laghupuṭaṃ dattvā dhmātaḥ khoṭo bhavetpriye  k mṛgadūrvottamāsomārasaiḥ sūtakasāraṇam mūlaistrayāṇāṃ lāṅgalyā rāmaṭhena ca hanyate  k samena hemnā saṃyuktaṃ piṣṭikāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ athavā tārapiṣṭiṃ ca samasūtena kārayet  k pūrvavatkramayogena khoṭo bhavati śobhanaḥ andhamūṣāgataṃ bhūmau svedayetkarṣakāgninā  k ahorātraṃ trirātraṃ vā cūrṇabandhaṃ bhavettataḥ taccūrṇabandhaṃ kurute vedhaṃ daśaguṇottaram  k śūlinīrasasūtaṃ ca srotoñjanasamanvitam pūrvavatpiṣṭikāyogāt khoṭo bhavati śobhanaḥ  k srotoñjanaṃ satagaraṃ sṛṣṭitrayayutaṃ rasam bhavedvahnisahaḥ kṣipraṃ sūtakaḥ sarvakarmakṛt  k hemābhraṃ caiva tārābhraṃ śulbābhraṃ cābhratīkṣṇakam mārayetpūrvavidhinā garbhayantre tuṣāgninā  k samāṃśaṃ sūtakaṃ dattvā vāraṃ vāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ jāyate vividhaḥ khoṭaḥ kāntabaddho mahārasaḥ  k bhavetsaṅkalikāyogādvedho daśaguṇottaraḥ nigalabandhaḥkhoṭaḥ poṭastathā bhasma dhūlīkalpaśca pañcamaḥ  k ete nigalayogābhyāṃ sarvabandhaphalodayaḥ snuhyarkasaṃbhavaṃ kṣīraṃ bandhabījāni gugguluḥ  k saindhavaṃ dviguṇaṃ dattvā mardayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ piṣṭikābandhanaṃ kṛtvā kalkenānena sundari  k bilvapramāṇaṃ kṛtvā tu mūṣāmatidṛḍhāṃ śubhām ūrdhvādho lavaṇaṃ dattvā mūṣāmadhye rasaṃ kṣipet  k mūṣāmadhye pradātavyaṃ dagdhaśaṅkhādicūrṇakam mukhaṃ tasya dṛḍhaṃ baddhvā loṇamṛttikayā budhaḥ  k kārayetsandhiloṇaṃ ca chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet ukto nigalabandhoyaṃ putrasyāpi na kathyate  k tuṣakarṣāgninā bhūmau mṛdusvedaṃ tu kārayet ahorātraṃ trirātraṃ vā puṭaṃ dattvā prayatnataḥ  k sudhmātaṃ khadirāṅgārai rasendraṃ khoṭatāṃ nayet sauvīraṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kācaṃ dattvā dattvā tu śodhayet  k akṣīṇo milate hemni samāvartaśca jāyate samāṃśabhakṣaṇaṃ tattu śuddhasūtena kārayet  k dhamayet pūrvayogena rasendraṃ khoṭatāṃ nayet bhavetsaṅkalikāyogādvedho daśaguṇottaraḥ  k palāśabījaniryāsaṃ kokilonmattavāruṇī śūlinīrasasaṃyuktaṃ peṣayetsaindhavānvitam  k piṣṭikāveṣṭanaṃ kṛtvā nigalena tu bandhayet abhrakasya tu patreṇa vajrārkakṣīrasindhunā  k tāpyena lohakiṭṭena sikatāmṛṇmayena ca ebhistu nigale baddhaḥ pāradīyo mahārasaḥ  k nātikrāmati maryādā velāmiva mahodadhiḥ tailārkakṣīrakatakalāṅgalyā nigalottamaḥ  k kākaviṭ brahmabījāni lāṅgalī nigaloparaḥ vākucī brahmabījāni karkaṭāsthīni sundari  k sāmudraṃ śāmbaraṃ caiva lavaṇaṃ nigalottamaḥ snuhyarkasambhavaṃ kṣīraṃ brahmabījāni kārayet  k kanakasya ca bījāni loṇāṣṭena ca mardayet nigalonyastu gojihvāmūlāni strīrajoparaḥ  k vākucī brahmabījāni snuhyarkakṣīrasaindhavam jvālinī kākaviṣṭhā ca praśasto nigalottamaḥ  k lavaṇaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kṣāraṃ śilātālakagandhakam tathāmlavetasaṃ tāpyaṃ hiṅgulaṃ samabhāgikam  k snuhyarkapayasā yuktaṃ peṣayennigalottamam piṣṭikāṃ veṣṭayedeṣāmekena nigalena pātre sthitaṃ rasam  k cūrṇībhūtaṃ samādāya sāndradviguṇavāsasā baddhvā somānale yantre hyathordhvaṃ gandhakaṃ samam  k dattvā pacetpunargandhamevaṃ gandhaṃ tu ṣaḍguṇam jārayetsa raso devi mūrchitaḥ sarvarogahā  k dvitīyaḥ prakāraḥgandhakaṃ navasāraṃ ca śuddhasūtasamaṃ samam yāmaṃ saṃmardayecchlakṣṇaṃ kācakūpyāṃ vinikṣipet  k saptamṛtkarpaṭair liptvā kūpīṃ gharme viśoṣayet kūpikāṃ vālukāyantre baddharasalakṣaṇamakṣayaśca laghudrāvī tejasvī nirmalo guruḥ  k sphuṭanaḥ punarāvarto baddhaḥ sūtaḥ sa ucyate jalūkābandhāḥmardanajalūkārasasyāṣṭamabhāgaṃ tu svarṇaṃ vā nāgameva vā  k śleṣmātakaphalaṃ pakvaṃ kokilākṣakabījakam tilapiṇyākacūrṇaṃ ca taptakhalve vimardayet  k śālmalyāścaiva pañcāṅgaṃ rasaṃ tatra vinikṣipet jalūkā jāyate yāvattāvanmardyāttataḥ kṣipet  k karpūraṃ vākucītailaṃ saindhavaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kaṇām kapikacchukaromāṇi tatsarvaṃ peṣayejjalaiḥ  k etatpūrvajalūkāṃ trisaptāhaṃ taptakhalvake jalūkā jāyate divyā mardanākhyā surārcite  k nārīṇāmṛtukāle tu sā yojyā yonigahvare manmathajalūkārasendrasyāṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ svarṇaṃ vā nāgameva vā  k śālmalītvagghastikandanīlāmūlamunicchadam eṣāṃ dravaistaptakhalve sarvaṃ mardyamatandritaḥ  k śleṣmātakaphalaṃ pakvaṃ kokilākṣakabījakam supakvabilvamajjāṃ ca tasminkṣiptvā vimardayet  k jalūkā jāyate yāvat karpūrādyaṃ ca pūrvavat tasminkṣiptvā trisaptāhaṃ mardayettaptakhalvake  k manmathākhyā jalūkā syātpūrvavat phaladāyinī kandarpajalūkāsūtakasyāṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ hāṭakaṃ sīsameva vā  k śuṇṭhī bhṛṅgī varā kṣaudrī chāgakṣīraghṛtaṃ gavām mūtraṃ triḥ saptadivasaṃ mardayettaptakhalvake  k jalūkā jāyate yāvatkarpūrādyaṃ ca pūrvavat ekaviṃśaddinaṃ mardyaṃ jalūkā jāyate śubhā  k kandarpākhyā sureśāni pūrvavatphaladāyinī madanajalūkātridinaṃ mardayet khalve sūtaniṣkacatuṣṭayam  k tripalaṃ cāmraniryāsaṃ stokaṃ stokaṃ vinikṣipet payaścaiva mahāśamyā dātavyaṃ mardanakṣamam  k jalūkā madanākhyeyaṃ jāyate śubhadā nṛṇām rāmāṇāṃ madadarpāṇāṃ drāvikāgnighṛtau yathā  k pūrvavatkramayogena vīryastambhakaraṃ bhavet nānāvarṇaṃ tathā svacchaṃ dhṛtaṃ yonau jalūkavat  k badhyate sūtako yastu jalūkābandhalakṣaṇam  k k  paribhāṣāparibhāṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tvaṃ sāvadhānataḥ vaidyabhāgaḥardhaṃ siddharasaṃ devi triṣvekaṃ hemabhasma ca  k pādāṃśakaṃ rūpyabhasma ṣaṣṭhāṃśaṃ tāmrabhasma ca aṣṭamāṃśaṃ hi kāntābhraṃ kalāṃśaṃ navaratnakam  k raseśvaraṃ samuddiśya rasavaidyāya dhīmate rasācāryāya siddhāya dadyādiṣṭārthasiddhaye  k kajjalī paṅkarasaścadhātubhirgandhakādyaiśca nirdravairmardito rasaḥ suślakṣṇaḥ kajjalābhosau kajjalī sābhidhīyate  k sadrave marditaḥ sopi iti pākarasaḥ smṛtaḥ piṣṭīarkāṃśatulyādrasatotha gandhānniṣkārdhatulyāttruṭiśopi khalve arkātape tīvratare vimardyātpiṣṭirbhavetsā navanītarūpā  k khalve vimardya gandhena dugdhena saha pāradam  k peṣaṇātpiṣṭitāṃ yāti sā piṣṭīti matā paraiḥ pātanapiṣṭīcaturthāṃśasuvarṇena rasena kṛtapiṣṭikā  k bhavetpātanapiṣṭī sā tathā rūpyādibhiḥ kṛtā hemapiṣṭī tārapiṣṭī carūpyaṃ vā jātarūpaṃ vā rasagandhādibhirhatam  k samutthitaṃ ca bahuśaḥ sā kṛṣṭī hematārayoḥ kṛṣṭīṃ kṣiptvā suvarṇānte na varṇo hīyate tayā  k svarṇakṛṣṭyā kṛtaṃ bījaṃ rasasya parirañjanam lohakamtāmraṃ tīkṣṇasamāyuktaṃ drutaṃ nikṣipya bhūriśaḥ  k sagandhe likucadrāve nirgataṃ varalohakam hemaraktī tāraraktī catena raktīkṛtaṃ svarṇaṃ hemaraktītyudāhṛtā  k nikṣiptā sā drute svarṇe varṇotkarṣavidhāyinī tārasya rañjanī cāpi bījarāgavidhāyinī  k evameva prakartavyā tāraraktī manoharā rañjanī khalu rūpyasya bījānāmapi rañjanī  k candrānaladalammṛtena vā baddharasena vānyalohena vā sādhitamanyaloham sitaṃ hi pītatvamupāgataṃ taddalaṃ hi candrānalayoḥ prasiddham  k ābhāsamṛtabandhena rasena saha yojitam sādhitaṃ vānyalohena sitaṃ pītaṃ hi taddalam  k ayonāgamtāpyena nihataṃ kāntaṃ saptavāraṃ samutthitam taddvayaṃ dvipalaṃ vātha tāmrabhasma paladvayam  k sarvaṃ nikṣipya mūṣāyāṃ saptavāraṃ dhameddṛḍham tadayonāgamityuktaṃ sādhakaṃ dehalohayoḥ  k rasena sāraṇāyantre tadīyā gulikā kṛtā sā dhṛtā vadane hanti meharogānaśeṣataḥ  k kurute dantadārḍhyaṃ ca dṛśau gṛdhradṛśāviva tathānyān kṣetrajānrogān rogāñ jatrūrdhvasaṃbhavān  k śulvanāgammākṣikeṇa hataṃ tāmraṃ daśavāraṃ samutthitam tadvadviśuddhanāgaṃ hi dvitayaṃ taccatuṣpalam  k nīlāñjanahataṃ bhūyaḥ saptavāraṃ samutthitam iti saṃsiddhametaddhi śulbanāgaṃ prakīrtitam  k sādhitastena sūtendro vadane vidhṛto nṛṇām nihanti māsamātreṇa mehavyūhamaśeṣataḥ  k pathyāśanasya varṣeṇa palitaṃ valibhiḥ saha gṛdhradṛṣṭir lasaddṛṣṭiḥ sarvārogyasamanvitaḥ  k piñjarīlohaṃ lohāntare kṣiptaṃ dhmātaṃ nirvāpitaṃ drave pāṇḍupītaprabhaṃ jātaṃ piñjarītyabhidhīyate  k candrārkambhāgāḥ ṣoḍaśa tārasya tathā dvādaśa bhāsvataḥ ekatrāvartitāste tu candrārkamiti kathyate  k nirvāpahaṇamdhāryalohe nyalohaścetprakṣipto vaṅkanālataḥ nirvāpaṇaṃ tu tatproktaṃ vaidyairnirvāhaṇaṃ khalu  k kṣipennirvāhaṇaṃ dravye nirvāhye samabhāgikam āvāpyaṃ vāpanīyaṃ ca bhāge dṛṣṭe ca dṛṣṭavat  k vārtitara Defmṛtaṃ tarati yattoye lohaṃ vāritaraṃ hi tat rekhāpūrṇa Defaṅguṣṭhatarjanīghṛṣṭaṃ yattadrekhāntare viśet  k mṛtaṃ lohaṃ taduddiṣṭaṃ rekhāpūrṇābhidhānataḥ nirutthabhasmalakṣaṇamguḍaguñjāsukhasparśamadhvājyaiḥ saha yojitam  k na yāti prakṛtiṃ dhmānādapunarbhavamucyate nirutthalohena saha saṃyuktaṃ dhmātaṃ rūpyeṇa cel lihet  k tadā nirutthamityuktaṃ lohaṃ tadapunarbhavam evaṃ rūpyaṃ satāmraṃ ceddhmātaṃ tāmre lagenna hi  k tadā nirutthaṃ mantavyaṃ rajataṃ ca bhiṣagvaraiḥ bījamnirvāhaṇaviśeṣeṇa tadvadvarṇaṃ bhavedyadā  k mṛdulaṃ citrasaṅkāśaṃ tad bījamiti kathyate uttāraṇamidameva hi nirdiṣṭaṃ vaidyairuttāraṇaṃ khalu  k saṃsṛṣṭalohayorekalohasya parināśanam tāḍanampradhmātaṃ vaṅkanālena tattāḍanamudāhṛtam  k dhānyābhramcūrṇābhraṃ śālisaṃyuktaṃ vastrabaddhaṃ hi kāñjike niryātaṃ mardanādvastrāddhānyābhramiti kathyate  k sattvamkṣārāmladrāvakairyuktaṃ dhmātamākarakoṣṭhake yastato nirgataḥ sāraḥ sattvam ityabhidhīyate  k ekakolīsakaḥkoṣṭhikāśikharāpūrṇaiḥ kokilādhmānayogataḥ mūṣākarṇam anuprāptair ekakolīśako mataḥ  k svedanādyarhāḥ kokilāḥśikhitrāḥ pāvakocchiṣṭā mṛtāṅgārāśca kokilāḥ kṛṣṇāṅgāḥ kokilāśceti paryāyāste parasparam  k charcoal wooddrāvaṇe sattvapāte ca mādhūkāḥ khādirāḥ śubhāḥ durdrāve vaṃśajāpestu svedane bādarāḥ śubhāḥ  k hiṅgulākṛṣṭarasaḥvidyādharākhyayantrasthād ārdrakadravamarditāt samākṛṣṭo raso yosau hiṅgulākṛṣṭa ucyate  k ghoṣākṛṣṭaṃ vaṅgamsvalpatālayutaṃ kāṃsyaṃ vaṅkanālena tāḍitam muktavaṅgaṃ hi tattāmraṃ ghoṣākṛṣṭamudāhṛtam  k guhyanāgampalaviṃśati nāgasya śuddhasya kṛtacakrikam rūpikādugdhasampiṣṭaśilāyāṃ parilepitam  k śarāvasaṃpuṭe ruddhvā pacet kroḍapuṭena tām tāvadvāraṃ pacedyatnādyāvadbhasma prajāyate  k guḍagugguluguñjājyaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ parimardya tam mūṣāmadhye nirudhyātha dhmānādutthāpitaṃ punaḥ  k cakrīṃ tena punaḥ kṛtvā palapramitapāradaiḥ liptvā limpetsitārkasya payasā śilayāpi ca  k pacedgajapuṭairevaṃ vārāṇāṃ khalu viṃśatiḥ puṭe puṭe ca nāgasya kuryādutthāpanaṃ khalu  k nīlajyotirdravaiḥ samyagdaśavārāṇi ḍhālayet iti siddhaṃ hi tat sīsaṃ karṣamātrāvaśeṣitam  k guhyanāgākhyayā proktaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rasarasāyane niṣkamātraṃ tu nāgesmin lohākhye yā drute sati  k svato lakṣaguṇāṃ haimīṃ śalākāṃ grasate dhruvam lagettailaprataptaṃ tatsvarṇamudgirati dhruvam  k guhyanāgoyamuddiṣṭaḥ śaktisvacchandabhairavaḥ varanāgamtīkṣṇaṃ nīlāñjanopetaṃ dhmātaṃ hi bahuśo dṛḍham  k mṛdu kṛṣṇaṃ drutadrāvaṃ varanāgaṃ taducyate utthāpanammṛtasya punarudbhūtiḥ sā proktotthāpanākhyayā  k ḍhālanamdrutadravyasya nikṣepo drave tat ḍhālanaṃ matam capalaḥtriṃśatpalamitaṃ nāgaṃ bhānudugdhena marditam  k vimṛdya puṭayet tāvad yāvat karṣāvaśeṣakam na tatpuṭasahasreṇa kṣayamāyāti sarvadā  k capaloyaṃ samādiṣṭo vārtikairnāgasambhavaḥ itthaṃ hi capalaḥ kāryo vaṅgasyāpi na saṃśayaḥ  k tatspṛṣṭahastasaṃspṛṣṭaḥ kevalo badhyate rasaḥ sa raso dhātuvādeṣu śasyate na rasāyane  k ayaṃ hi piṣṭīṃ kṛtvā tu pūrveṇa pūrvakalkaiśca yojayet  k atha prakṣālya soṣṇena kāñjikena praśoṣayet palārdhaṃ śuddhasasyena aṣṭaguñjārasena ca  k vimardya kāñjikaiḥ kuryānmaricapramitā vaṭīḥ nirudhya vajramūṣāyāṃ sandhibandhaṃ vidhāya ca  k śikhitrair navabhiḥ samyagbhastrābhyāṃ pradhametkhalu tato mūṣāgataṃ sattvaṃ samādāya samantataḥ  k dhametprakaṭamūṣāyāṃ vaṅkanālena śodhayet daśaśāṇaṃ hi tatsatvaṃ bhasmanā lavaṇena ca  k sakāñjikena saṃpeṣya puṭayogena śodhayet triniṣkapramite tasminpūrvaproktena bhasmanā  k aśītiguṇitaṃ nāgaṃ dhmātvā nirvāhayet khalu iyatā pūrvasūtosau kṣīyate na kathaṃcana  k capaloyaṃ samuddiṣṭo lokanāthena śambhunā anenāpi rasaḥ śīghraṃ pūrvavad badhyate sukham  k kāravallījaṭācūrṇairdaśadhā puṭito hi saḥ bhavennāgavinirmukto grāsaṃ gṛhṇātyaśeṣataḥ  k sukhaṃ prakaṭamūṣāyāṃ bhavec cātiguṇottaraḥ jīrṇagrāso raso hyeṣāṃ dehalohakaro bhavet  k bhūnāgadhautambhūbhujaṅgaśakṛttoyaiḥ prakṣālyāpahṛtaṃ malam kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ hi tatproktaṃ dhautākhyaṃ rasavādibhiḥ  k dvandvānamdravyayormelanaṃ dhmānād dvaṃdvānaṃ parikīrtitam bhañjanībhāgādrūpyādhike kṣepamanuvarṇasavarṇakam  k dalairvā varṇikāgrāso bhañjanī vādinirmitā phullikāpataṅgīkalkato jātā lohe svāṅgaśītaṃ vahnibahiḥśītaṃ cavahnisthameva śītaṃ yattaduktaṃ svāṅgaśītalam  k agnerākṛṣṭaśītaṃ yadvahniśītaṃ tadīritam svedanamkṣārāmlair auṣadhairvāpi ḍolāyantre sthitasya hi  k pacanaṃ svedanākhyaṃ syānmalaśaithilyakārakam mardanamuddiṣṭairauṣadhaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarvāmlaiḥ kāñjikairapi  k peṣaṇaṃ mardanākhyaṃ syādbahirmalavināśanam mūrchanammardanādiṣṭabhaiṣajyair naṣṭapiṣṭitvakārakam  k dīpanamdhātupāṣāṇamūlādyaiḥ saṃyukto ghaṭamadhyataḥ  k grāsārthaṃ tridinaṃ svedo dīpanaṃ tanmataṃ budhaiḥ grāsamānamiyanmānasya sūtasya bhojyadravyātmikā mitiḥ  k iyatītyucyate yosau grāsamānamitīritam jāraṇāgrāsasya cāraṇaṃ garbhadrāvaṇaṃ jāraṇaṃ tathā  k iti trirūpā nirdiṣṭā jāraṇā varavārtikaiḥ grāsaḥ piṇḍaḥ parīṇāmastisraścākhyāḥ parāḥ punaḥ  k samukhā nirmukhā ceti jāraṇā dvividhā matā nirmukhā jāraṇā proktā bījādānena bhāgataḥ  k samukhajāraṇāśuddhaṃ svarṇaṃ ca rūpyaṃ ca bījamityabhidhīyate catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśato bījaprakṣepo mukhamucyate  k evaṃ kṛte raso grāsalolupo vedhādhikyakaraṃ lohe sāraṇā sā prakīrtitā vedhaḥvyavāyibheṣajopeto dravye kṣipto rasaḥ khalu  k vedha ityucyate tajjñaiḥ sa cānekavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ vedhabhedāḥlepaḥ kṣepaśca kuntaśca śabdākhyo dhūmasaṃjñakaḥ  k lepavedhaḥlepena kurute lohaṃ svarṇaṃ vā rajataṃ tathā lepavedhaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ puṭamatra ca saukaram  k kṣepavedhaḥprakṣepaṇaṃ drute lohe vedhaḥ syātkṣepasaṃjñakaḥ kuntavedhaḥsaṃdaṃśadhṛtasūtena drutadravyāhatiśca yaḥ  k suvarṇatvādikaraṇaḥ kuntavedhaḥ sa ucyate dhūpavedhaḥvahnau dhūmāyamāne ntaḥprakṣiptarasadhūmataḥ  k svarṇādyāpādanaṃ lohe dhūmavedhaḥ sa īritaḥ śabdavedhaḥmukhasthite rase nālyā lohasya dhamanātkhalu  k svarṇarūpyatvajananaṃ śabdavedhaḥ sa kīrtitaḥ utpāṭanampiṇḍadravyasya sūtena kāluṣyādinivāraṇam  k prakāśanaṃ ca varṇasya tadutpāṭanamīritam svedanamkṣārāmlairauṣadhaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhāṇḍe ruddhvātiyatnataḥ  k bhūmau nikhanyate yattatsvedanaṃ samudīritam saṃnyāsaḥrasasyauṣadhayuktasya bhāṇḍe ruddhasya yatnataḥ  k sadāgniyutacullyantaḥkṣepaḥ saṃnyāsa ucyate svedanasaṃnyāsaguṇāḥdvāvetau svedasaṃnyāsau rasarājasya niścitam  k guṇaprabhāvajananau śīghravyāptikarau tathā  k k  yantrāṇiraso niyantryate yena yantraṃ taditi kathyate  khalvayantramkhalvayantraṃ dvidhā proktaṃ mardanādikakarmaṇi  k khalvaṃ lohamayaṃ devi pāṣāṇotthamathāpi vā khalvayogyā śilā nīlā śyāmā snigdhā dṛḍhā guruḥ  k khalvayantraṃ dvidhā proktaṃ rasādimukhamardane ṣoḍaśāṅgulikotsedhā navāṅgulisuvistarā  k caturviṃśāṅgulīdīrghagharṣaṇī dvādaśāṅgulā viṃśatyaṅguladīrghā vā syādutsedhe daśāṅgulā  k khalvapramāṇaṃ tajjñeyaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ
